Файл: scripts/generate-listing.mjs
Рядків: 146
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   1 | import { readdir, readFile, writeFile, stat } from 'node:fs/promises'
   2 | import path from 'node:path'
   3 | import { fileURLToPath } from 'node:url'
   4 | 
   5 | const __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url))
   6 | const ROOT = path.resolve(__dirname, '..')
   7 | const OUT = path.join(ROOT, 'docs', 'listing-kodu.txt')
   8 | 
   9 | const SKIP_DIRS = new Set(['node_modules', 'dist', '.git', '.idea', '.vercel'])
  10 | const LISTING_EXTENSIONS = new Set(['.ts', '.tsx', '.css', '.html', '.js', '.mjs', '.json'])
  11 | const SKIP_FILES = new Set(['yarn.lock', 'package-lock.json'])
  12 | const TRUNCATE_FILES = new Map([
  13 |   ['src/data/schedule.json', 80],
  14 | ])
  15 | 
  16 | function rel(filePath) {
  17 |   return filePath.replace(`${ROOT}${path.sep}`, '').replace(/\\/g, '/')
  18 | }
  19 | 
  20 | async function walk(dir, acc = []) {
  21 |   const entries = await readdir(dir, { withFileTypes: true })
  22 |   for (const entry of entries.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name, 'uk'))) {
  23 |     const full = path.join(dir, entry.name)
  24 |     if (entry.isDirectory()) {
  25 |       if (SKIP_DIRS.has(entry.name)) continue
  26 |       await walk(full, acc)
  27 |       continue
  28 |     }
  29 |     acc.push(full)
  30 |   }
  31 |   return acc
  32 | }
  33 | 
  34 | function buildTreeLines(allFiles) {
  35 |   const tree = {}
  36 |   for (const file of allFiles) {
  37 |     const parts = rel(file).split('/')
  38 |     let node = tree
  39 |     for (let i = 0; i < parts.length; i += 1) {
  40 |       const part = parts[i]
  41 |       const isFile = i === parts.length - 1
  42 |       if (!node[part]) node[part] = isFile ? null : {}
  43 |       if (!isFile) node = node[part]
  44 |     }
  45 |   }
  46 | 
  47 |   const lines = ['schedule-3d/']
  48 |   function render(node, prefix = '') {
  49 |     const keys = Object.keys(node).sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, 'uk'))
  50 |     keys.forEach((key, index) => {
  51 |       const last = index === keys.length - 1
  52 |       const branch = last ? '└── ' : '├── '
  53 |       const childPrefix = last ? '    ' : '│   '
  54 |       if (node[key] === null) {
  55 |         lines.push(`${prefix}${branch}${key}`)
  56 |       } else {
  57 |         lines.push(`${prefix}${branch}${key}/`)
  58 |         render(node[key], prefix + childPrefix)
  59 |       }
  60 |     })
  61 |   }
  62 |   render(tree)
  63 |   return lines
  64 | }
  65 | 
  66 | function padLineNo(n) {
  67 |   return String(n).padStart(4, ' ')
  68 | }
  69 | 
  70 | async function main() {
  71 |   const allFiles = await walk(ROOT)
  72 |   const treeLines = buildTreeLines(allFiles)
  73 | 
  74 |   const listingCandidates = allFiles
  75 |     .filter((file) => {
  76 |       const name = path.basename(file)
  77 |       if (SKIP_FILES.has(name)) return false
  78 |       const ext = path.extname(file).toLowerCase()
  79 |       if (!LISTING_EXTENSIONS.has(ext)) return false
  80 |       return true
  81 |     })
  82 |     .sort((a, b) => rel(a).localeCompare(rel(b), 'uk'))
  83 | 
  84 |   const parts = [
  85 |     'ЛІСТИНГ ПРОГРАМНОГО ЗАБЕЗПЕЧЕННЯ',
  86 |     'Проєкт: schedule-3d — інтерактивний 3D-інтерфейс для навігації та планування навчального процесу',
  87 |     `Дата формування: ${new Date().toLocaleString('uk-UA')}`,
  88 |     `Репозиторій: https://github.com/OpamLNL/schedule-3d`,
  89 |     '',
  90 |     '═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════',
  91 |     'РОЗДІЛ 1. ІЄРАРХІЯ ФАЙЛІВ ПРОЄКТУ',
  92 |     '(без node_modules, dist, .git, .idea)',
  93 |     '═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════',
  94 |     '',
  95 |     ...treeLines,
  96 |     '',
  97 |     'Примітки до ієрархії:',
  98 |     '  • yarn.lock — файл залежностей (не включено до лістингу коду)',
  99 |     '  • src/assets/*, public/* — графічні ресурси (png, svg)',
 100 |     '  • docs/*.mmd, docs/*.svg — діаграми документації',
 101 |     '',
 102 |     '═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════',
 103 |     'РОЗДІЛ 2. ЛІСТИНГ ВИХІДНОГО КОДУ',
 104 |     `(файли: ${listingCandidates.map(rel).join(', ')})`,
 105 |     '═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════',
 106 |     '',
 107 |   ]
 108 | 
 109 |   for (const file of listingCandidates) {
 110 |     const relative = rel(file)
 111 |     const raw = await readFile(file, 'utf8')
 112 |     const lines = raw.replace(/\r\n/g, '\n').split('\n')
 113 |     const limit = TRUNCATE_FILES.get(relative)
 114 |     const shown = limit ? lines.slice(0, limit) : lines
 115 |     const truncated = limit && lines.length > limit
 116 | 
 117 |     parts.push('')
 118 |     parts.push('─'.repeat(78))
 119 |     parts.push(`Файл: ${relative}`)
 120 |     parts.push(`Рядків: ${lines.length}${truncated ? ` (показано перші ${limit})` : ''}`)
 121 |     parts.push('─'.repeat(78))
 122 |     shown.forEach((line, index) => {
 123 |       parts.push(`${padLineNo(index + 1)} | ${line}`)
 124 |     })
 125 |     if (truncated) {
 126 |       parts.push(`${padLineNo(limit + 1)} | ... [скорочено, решта ${lines.length - limit} рядків]`)
 127 |     }
 128 |   }
 129 | 
 130 |   parts.push('')
 131 |   parts.push('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════')
 132 |   parts.push('Кінець лістингу')
 133 |   parts.push('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════')
 134 | 
 135 |   await writeFile(OUT, parts.join('\n'), 'utf8')
 136 |   const info = await stat(OUT)
 137 |   console.log(`Записано: ${OUT}`)
 138 |   console.log(`Розмір: ${(info.size / 1024).toFixed(1)} KB`)
 139 |   console.log(`Файлів у лістингу: ${listingCandidates.length}`)
 140 | }
 141 | 
 142 | main().catch((error) => {
 143 |   console.error(error)
 144 |   process.exit(1)
 145 | })

Файл: scripts/import-xlsx.mjs
Рядків: 146
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   1 | import fs from 'node:fs'
   2 | import path from 'node:path'
   3 | import { fileURLToPath } from 'node:url'
   4 | import XLSX from 'xlsx'
   5 | 
   6 | const __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url))
   7 | const rootDir = path.resolve(__dirname, '..')
   8 | const parentDir = path.resolve(rootDir, '..')
   9 | 
  10 | function findXlsxFile() {
  11 |   for (const dir of [parentDir, rootDir]) {
  12 |     const match = fs.readdirSync(dir).find((name) => name.toLowerCase().endsWith('.xlsx'))
  13 |     if (match) return path.join(dir, match)
  14 |   }
  15 |   throw new Error('Не знайдено .xlsx файл у робочій папці')
  16 | }
  17 | 
  18 | const resolvedPath = findXlsxFile()
  19 | const workbook = XLSX.readFile(resolvedPath)
  20 | const sheetName = workbook.SheetNames.includes('2025') ? '2025' : workbook.SheetNames[0]
  21 | const rows = XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(workbook.Sheets[sheetName], { header: 1, defval: '' })
  22 | 
  23 | const DAYS = ['Пн', 'Вт', 'Ср', 'Чт', 'Пт']
  24 | const PERIODS = 8
  25 | const TOTAL_SLOTS = DAYS.length * PERIODS
  26 | const ROOMS = ['101', '102', '201', '202', '301', '302', '401', '402', '501', '502', '601', '602']
  27 | const groupPattern = /([A-ZА-ЯІЇЄҐ]{2,}\d{1,2})/g
  28 | 
  29 | function normalizeTeacher(value) {
  30 |   const teacher = String(value ?? '').trim()
  31 |   if (!teacher || teacher === 'В' || teacher.length < 3) return null
  32 |   if (teacher.toLowerCase().includes('прізвище') || teacher.toLowerCase().includes('викладач')) return null
  33 |   return teacher.replace(/\s+/g, ' ')
  34 | }
  35 | 
  36 | function normalizeSubject(value) {
  37 |   const subject = String(value ?? '').trim()
  38 |   if (!subject || subject.startsWith('РОЗПОДІЛ') || subject.length < 4) return null
  39 |   if (/^[\d\s.,]+$/.test(subject)) return null
  40 |   return subject.replace(/\*+/g, '').trim()
  41 | }
  42 | 
  43 | function hashString(input) {
  44 |   let hash = 0
  45 |   for (let i = 0; i < input.length; i += 1) {
  46 |     hash = (hash * 31 + input.charCodeAt(i)) >>> 0
  47 |   }
  48 |   return hash
  49 | }
  50 | 
  51 | function pickSlots(seed, count) {
  52 |   const slots = new Set()
  53 |   let cursor = seed
  54 |   while (slots.size < count) {
  55 |     slots.add((cursor % TOTAL_SLOTS) + 1)
  56 |     cursor = (cursor * 1103515245 + 12345) >>> 0
  57 |   }
  58 |   return [...slots]
  59 | }
  60 | 
  61 | const lessons = []
  62 | for (const row of rows) {
  63 |   const subject = normalizeSubject(row[0])
  64 |   const teacher = normalizeTeacher(row[1])
  65 |   if (!subject || !teacher) continue
  66 |   const groupMatches = [...`${row[0]} ${row[1]}`.matchAll(groupPattern)].map((m) => m[1])
  67 |   lessons.push({ subject, teacher, groupCode: groupMatches[0] ?? null })
  68 | }
  69 | 
  70 | const uniqueGroups = [...new Set(lessons.map((l) => l.groupCode).filter(Boolean))].slice(0, 12)
  71 | if (uniqueGroups.length === 0) {
  72 |   uniqueGroups.push('ГР1', 'ГР2', 'ГР3', 'ГР4', 'ГР5', 'ГР6', 'ГР7', 'ГР8')
  73 | }
  74 | 
  75 | const groupsMap = new Map()
  76 | uniqueGroups.forEach((code, index) => {
  77 |   groupsMap.set(code, {
  78 |     id: `g${index + 1}`,
  79 |     code,
  80 |     name: `Група ${code}`,
  81 |     specialty: code.slice(0, 2),
  82 |     course: Number.parseInt(code.match(/\d/)?.[0] ?? '1', 10),
  83 |     room: ROOMS[index % ROOMS.length],
  84 |   })
  85 | })
  86 | 
  87 | const groupedLessons = new Map()
  88 | for (const lesson of lessons) {
  89 |   const code = lesson.groupCode && groupsMap.has(lesson.groupCode) ? lesson.groupCode : uniqueGroups[0]
  90 |   if (!groupedLessons.has(code)) groupedLessons.set(code, [])
  91 |   groupedLessons.get(code).push(lesson)
  92 | }
  93 | 
  94 | const entries = []
  95 | let entryCounter = 0
  96 | 
  97 | for (const [groupCode, groupLessons] of groupedLessons.entries()) {
  98 |   const group = groupsMap.get(groupCode)
  99 |   groupLessons.slice(0, 18).forEach((lesson) => {
 100 |     pickSlots(hashString(`${groupCode}-${lesson.subject}-${lesson.teacher}`), 2).forEach((slotId, slotIndex) => {
 101 |       entryCounter += 1
 102 |       entries.push({
 103 |         id: `e${entryCounter}`,
 104 |         groupId: group.id,
 105 |         slotId,
 106 |         subject: lesson.subject.length > 42 ? `${lesson.subject.slice(0, 39)}...` : lesson.subject,
 107 |         teacher: lesson.teacher,
 108 |         room: slotIndex === 0 ? group.room : ROOMS[(hashString(lesson.teacher) + slotId) % ROOMS.length],
 109 |       })
 110 |     })
 111 |   })
 112 | }
 113 | 
 114 | if (entries.length > 8) {
 115 |   entries[3].slotId = entries[0].slotId
 116 |   entries[3].teacher = entries[0].teacher
 117 |   entries[7].slotId = entries[1].slotId
 118 |   entries[7].room = entries[1].room
 119 | }
 120 | 
 121 | const output = {
 122 |   meta: {
 123 |     sourceFile: path.basename(resolvedPath),
 124 |     generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
 125 |     note: 'Демо-розклад згенеровано з навчального плану. Слоти часу розподілено автоматично для перегляду 3D-моделі.',
 126 |     days: DAYS,
 127 |     periodsPerDay: PERIODS,
 128 |     totalSlots: TOTAL_SLOTS,
 129 |   },
 130 |   groups: [...groupsMap.values()],
 131 |   teachers: [...new Set(entries.map((entry) => entry.teacher))].map((name, index) => ({
 132 |     id: `t${index + 1}`,
 133 |     name,
 134 |   })),
 135 |   rooms: ROOMS.map((code, index) => ({ id: `r${index + 1}`, code })),
 136 |   entries,
 137 | }
 138 | 
 139 | const outPath = path.join(rootDir, 'src', 'data', 'schedule.json')
 140 | fs.mkdirSync(path.dirname(outPath), { recursive: true })
 141 | fs.writeFileSync(outPath, JSON.stringify(output, null, 2), 'utf8')
 142 | 
 143 | console.log(`Імпортовано з: ${resolvedPath}`)
 144 | console.log(`Груп: ${output.groups.length}, занять: ${output.entries.length}`)
 145 | console.log(`Збережено: ${outPath}`)
 146 |

   1 | import { useCallback, useEffect, useState } from 'react'
   2 | import { TopNav, type AppPage } from './components/AppLayout'
   3 | import { PlanningProvider } from './context/PlanningContext'
   4 | import { ThemeProvider } from './context/ThemeContext'
   5 | import { CylinderPage } from './pages/CylinderPage'
   6 | import { GroupsPage } from './pages/GroupsPage'
   7 | import { NavPlanPage } from './pages/NavPlanPage'
   8 | import { TeacherPrefsPage } from './pages/TeacherPrefsPage'
   9 | import { SubjectPrefsPage } from './pages/SubjectPrefsPage'
  10 | import { RoomRulesPage } from './pages/RoomRulesPage'
  11 | import { SchedulePage } from './pages/SchedulePage'
  12 | import { readAppPageFromHash, writeAppPageToHash } from './utils/appRouting'
  13 | import './App.css'
  14 | 
  15 | function AppRouter() {
  16 |   const [page, setPage] = useState<AppPage>(() => readAppPageFromHash())
  17 | 
  18 |   useEffect(() => {
  19 |     const syncFromHash = () => setPage(readAppPageFromHash())
  20 |     window.addEventListener('hashchange', syncFromHash)
  21 |     return () => window.removeEventListener('hashchange', syncFromHash)
  22 |   }, [])
  23 | 
  24 |   const onPageChange = useCallback((next: AppPage) => {
  25 |     setPage(next)
  26 |     writeAppPageToHash(next)
  27 |   }, [])
  28 | 
  29 |   if (page === 'cylinder') {
  30 |     return (
  31 |       <>
  32 |         <TopNav page={page} onPageChange={onPageChange} />
  33 |         <CylinderPage />
  34 |       </>
  35 |     )
  36 |   }
  37 | 
  38 |   const common = { page, onPageChange }
  39 | 
  40 |   if (page === 'nav') return <NavPlanPage {...common} />
  41 |   if (page === 'groups') return <GroupsPage {...common} />
  42 |   if (page === 'teacherPrefs') return <TeacherPrefsPage {...common} />
  43 |   if (page === 'subjectPrefs') return <SubjectPrefsPage {...common} />
  44 |   if (page === 'rooms') return <RoomRulesPage {...common} />
  45 |   if (page === 'schedule') return <SchedulePage {...common} />
  46 |   return <NavPlanPage {...common} />
  47 | }
  48 | 
  49 | export default function App() {
  50 |   return (
  51 |     <ThemeProvider>
  52 |       <PlanningProvider>
  53 |         <AppRouter />
  54 |       </PlanningProvider>
  55 |     </ThemeProvider>
  56 |   )
  57 | }
  58 |

Файл: src/components/BatchExportPanel.tsx
Рядків: 259

   1 | import { useMemo, useState } from 'react'
   2 | import type { ScheduleData } from '../types/schedule'
   3 | import {
   4 |   clearExportFolder,
   5 |   isFolderExportSupported,
   6 |   loadExportLocationPrefs,
   7 |   pickExportFolder,
   8 |   saveExportLocationPrefs,
   9 |   type ExportLocationPrefs,
  10 | } from '../storage/exportLocationStorage'
  11 | import {
  12 |   exportScheduleBatch,
  13 |   type BatchExportProgress,
  14 |   type BatchExportScope,
  15 | } from '../utils/batchScheduleExport'
  16 | 
  17 | type BatchExportPanelProps = {
  18 |   schedule: ScheduleData
  19 |   onStatus?: (message: string | null) => void
  20 | }
  21 | 
  22 | export function BatchExportPanel({ schedule, onStatus }: BatchExportPanelProps) {
  23 |   const groups = useMemo(
  24 |     () => [...schedule.groups].sort((a, b) => a.code.localeCompare(b.code, 'uk')),
  25 |     [schedule.groups],
  26 |   )
  27 | 
  28 |   const [locationPrefs, setLocationPrefs] = useState<ExportLocationPrefs>(() => loadExportLocationPrefs())
  29 |   const [scope, setScope] = useState<BatchExportScope>('all')
  30 |   const [selectedGroups, setSelectedGroups] = useState<Set<string>>(() => new Set(groups.map((g) => g.code)))
  31 |   const [includeFullScheduleJson, setIncludeFullScheduleJson] = useState(true)
  32 |   const [includeGroupHtml, setIncludeGroupHtml] = useState(true)
  33 |   const [includeGroupJson, setIncludeGroupJson] = useState(true)
  34 |   const [busy, setBusy] = useState(false)
  35 |   const [progress, setProgress] = useState<BatchExportProgress | null>(null)
  36 |   const [lastResult, setLastResult] = useState<string | null>(null)
  37 | 
  38 |   const folderSupported = isFolderExportSupported()
  39 |   const selectedCount = scope === 'all' ? groups.length : selectedGroups.size
  40 | 
  41 |   const toggleGroup = (code: string) => {
  42 |     setSelectedGroups((current) => {
  43 |       const next = new Set(current)
  44 |       if (next.has(code)) next.delete(code)
  45 |       else next.add(code)
  46 |       return next
  47 |     })
  48 |   }
  49 | 
  50 |   const selectAllGroups = () => setSelectedGroups(new Set(groups.map((group) => group.code)))
  51 |   const clearGroups = () => setSelectedGroups(new Set())
  52 | 
  53 |   const chooseDownloads = () => {
  54 |     const prefs: ExportLocationPrefs = { mode: 'downloads' }
  55 |     saveExportLocationPrefs(prefs)
  56 |     setLocationPrefs(prefs)
  57 |     setLastResult(null)
  58 |   }
  59 | 
  60 |   const chooseFolder = async () => {
  61 |     if (!folderSupported) return
  62 |     const picked = await pickExportFolder()
  63 |     if (!picked) return
  64 |     setLocationPrefs(picked)
  65 |     setLastResult(`Папка: ${picked.folderLabel ?? 'обрано'}`)
  66 |   }
  67 | 
  68 |   const resetFolder = async () => {
  69 |     await clearExportFolder()
  70 |     chooseDownloads()
  71 |   }
  72 | 
  73 |   const runExport = async () => {
  74 |     if (!includeGroupHtml && !includeGroupJson && !includeFullScheduleJson) {
  75 |       onStatus?.('Оберіть хоча б один тип файлу для експорту')
  76 |       return
  77 |     }
  78 | 
  79 |     setBusy(true)
  80 |     setProgress(null)
  81 |     setLastResult(null)
  82 |     onStatus?.('Експорт розкладу…')
  83 | 
  84 |     try {
  85 |       const result = await exportScheduleBatch(
  86 |         schedule,
  87 |         {
  88 |           scope,
  89 |           groupCodes: [...selectedGroups],
  90 |           includeFullScheduleJson,
  91 |           includeGroupHtml,
  92 |           includeGroupJson,
  93 |         },
  94 |         setProgress,
  95 |       )
  96 | 
  97 |       const message =
  98 |         result.method === 'folder'
  99 |           ? `Збережено ${result.files} файлів у папку ${result.sessionFolder}`
 100 |           : `Завантажено ${result.files} файлів (${result.groups} груп)`
 101 |       setLastResult(message)
 102 |       onStatus?.(message)
 103 |     } catch (error) {
 104 |       const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Помилка експорту'
 105 |       setLastResult(message)
 106 |       onStatus?.(message)
 107 |     } finally {
 108 |       setBusy(false)
 109 |       setProgress(null)
 110 |     }
 111 |   }
 112 | 
 113 |   return (
 114 |     <section className="panel section-block batch-export-panel">
 115 |       <div className="section-head">
 116 |         <h2>Пакетний експорт для друку</h2>
 117 |       </div>
 118 | 
 119 |       <div className="batch-export-grid">
 120 |         <div className="batch-export-block">
 121 |           <h3>Куди зберігати</h3>
 122 |           <div className="batch-export-location">
 123 |             <label className="radio-row">
 124 |               <input
 125 |                 type="radio"
 126 |                 name="export-location"
 127 |                 checked={locationPrefs.mode === 'downloads'}
 128 |                 onChange={chooseDownloads}
 129 |               />
 130 |               <span>Завантаження браузера</span>
 131 |             </label>
 132 |             <label className={`radio-row${folderSupported ? '' : ' disabled'}`}>
 133 |               <input
 134 |                 type="radio"
 135 |                 name="export-location"
 136 |                 checked={locationPrefs.mode === 'folder'}
 137 |                 disabled={!folderSupported}
 138 |                 onChange={() => void chooseFolder()}
 139 |               />
 140 |               <span>
 141 |                 Обрана папка
 142 |                 {locationPrefs.mode === 'folder' && locationPrefs.folderLabel
 143 |                   ? `: ${locationPrefs.folderLabel}`
 144 |                   : ''}
 145 |               </span>
 146 |             </label>
 147 |           </div>
 148 |           <div className="batch-export-location-actions">
 149 |             {folderSupported ? (
 150 |               <button type="button" className="btn" disabled={busy} onClick={() => void chooseFolder()}>
 151 |                 Обрати папку…
 152 |               </button>
 153 |             ) : (
 154 |               <p className="muted">Обрання папки недоступне в цьому браузері — файли підуть у «Завантаження».</p>
 155 |             )}
 156 |             {locationPrefs.mode === 'folder' ? (
 157 |               <button type="button" className="btn" disabled={busy} onClick={() => void resetFolder()}>
 158 |                 Скинути папку
 159 |               </button>
 160 |             ) : null}
 161 |           </div>
 162 |           <p className="muted batch-export-hint">
 163 |             У режимі папки створюється підпапка <code>schedule-export_дата_час</code> з HTML для друку, JSON і
 164 |             manifest.
 165 |           </p>
 166 |         </div>
 167 | 
 168 |         <div className="batch-export-block">
 169 |           <h3>Що експортувати</h3>
 170 |           <div className="batch-export-scope">
 171 |             <label className="radio-row">
 172 |               <input
 173 |                 type="radio"
 174 |                 name="export-scope"
 175 |                 checked={scope === 'all'}
 176 |                 onChange={() => setScope('all')}
 177 |               />
 178 |               <span>Усі групи ({groups.length})</span>
 179 |             </label>
 180 |             <label className="radio-row">
 181 |               <input
 182 |                 type="radio"
 183 |                 name="export-scope"
 184 |                 checked={scope === 'selected'}
 185 |                 onChange={() => setScope('selected')}
 186 |               />
 187 |               <span>Обрані групи ({selectedCount})</span>
 188 |             </label>
 189 |           </div>
 190 | 
 191 |           {scope === 'selected' ? (
 192 |             <div className="batch-export-groups">
 193 |               <div className="batch-export-groups-actions">
 194 |                 <button type="button" className="btn" onClick={selectAllGroups}>
 195 |                   Усі
 196 |                 </button>
 197 |                 <button type="button" className="btn" onClick={clearGroups}>
 198 |                   Жодної
 199 |                 </button>
 200 |               </div>
 201 |               <div className="batch-export-group-list">
 202 |                 {groups.map((group) => (
 203 |                   <label key={group.id} className="checkbox-row batch-export-group-item">
 204 |                     <input
 205 |                       type="checkbox"
 206 |                       checked={selectedGroups.has(group.code)}
 207 |                       onChange={() => toggleGroup(group.code)}
 208 |                     />
 209 |                     <span>{group.code}</span>
 210 |                   </label>
 211 |                 ))}
 212 |               </div>
 213 |             </div>
 214 |           ) : null}
 215 | 
 216 |           <div className="batch-export-formats">
 217 |             <label className="checkbox-row">
 218 |               <input
 219 |                 type="checkbox"
 220 |                 checked={includeFullScheduleJson}
 221 |                 onChange={(e) => setIncludeFullScheduleJson(e.target.checked)}
 222 |               />
 223 |               <span>JSON усього розкладу</span>
 224 |             </label>
 225 |             <label className="checkbox-row">
 226 |               <input
 227 |                 type="checkbox"
 228 |                 checked={includeGroupHtml}
 229 |                 onChange={(e) => setIncludeGroupHtml(e.target.checked)}
 230 |               />
 231 |               <span>HTML для друку по групах</span>
 232 |             </label>
 233 |             <label className="checkbox-row">
 234 |               <input
 235 |                 type="checkbox"
 236 |                 checked={includeGroupJson}
 237 |                 onChange={(e) => setIncludeGroupJson(e.target.checked)}
 238 |               />
 239 |               <span>JSON по групах</span>
 240 |             </label>
 241 |           </div>
 242 |         </div>
 243 |       </div>
 244 | 
 245 |       <div className="batch-export-footer">
 246 |         <button type="button" className="btn primary" disabled={busy || selectedCount === 0} onClick={() => void runExport()}>
 247 |           {busy ? 'Зберігаємо…' : `Зберегти пакет (${selectedCount} груп)`}
 248 |         </button>
 249 |         {progress ? (
 250 |           <span className="muted">
 251 |             {progress.done}/{progress.total} · {progress.label}
 252 |           </span>
 253 |         ) : null}
 254 |         {lastResult ? <span className="batch-export-result">{lastResult}</span> : null}
 255 |       </div>
 256 |     </section>
 257 |   )
 258 | }

   1 | import { useMemo } from 'react'
   2 | import { BufferGeometry, Float32BufferAttribute } from 'three'
   3 | import type { ScheduleMeta } from '../types/schedule'
   4 | import { LAYER_GAP, LAYER_HEIGHT } from '../utils/scheduleCylinderLayout'
   5 | import { slotAngle } from '../utils/slots'
   6 | 
   7 | type CylinderSurfaceGridProps = {
   8 |   meta: ScheduleMeta
   9 |   groupCount: number
  10 |   baseY: number
  11 |   totalHeight: number
  12 |   radius: number
  13 | }
  14 | 
  15 | function pushCircle(points: number[], y: number, radius: number, segments = 72) {
  16 |   for (let index = 0; index < segments; index += 1) {
  17 |     const angle0 = (index / segments) * Math.PI * 2 - Math.PI / 2
  18 |     const angle1 = ((index + 1) / segments) * Math.PI * 2 - Math.PI / 2
  19 |     points.push(
  20 |       Math.cos(angle0) * radius,
  21 |       y,
  22 |       Math.sin(angle0) * radius,
  23 |       Math.cos(angle1) * radius,
  24 |       y,
  25 |       Math.sin(angle1) * radius,
  26 |     )
  27 |   }
  28 | }
  29 | 
  30 | function pushMeridian(points: number[], angle: number, yBottom: number, yTop: number, radius: number) {
  31 |   points.push(
  32 |     Math.cos(angle) * radius,
  33 |     yBottom,
  34 |     Math.sin(angle) * radius,
  35 |     Math.cos(angle) * radius,
  36 |     yTop,
  37 |     Math.sin(angle) * radius,
  38 |   )
  39 | }
  40 | 
  41 | export function CylinderSurfaceGrid({
  42 |   meta,
  43 |   groupCount,
  44 |   baseY,
  45 |   totalHeight,
  46 |   radius,
  47 | }: CylinderSurfaceGridProps) {
  48 |   const { lineGeometry, dayLineGeometry } = useMemo(() => {
  49 |     const gridPoints: number[] = []
  50 |     const dayPoints: number[] = []
  51 |     const yTop = baseY + totalHeight
  52 |     const slotStep = (Math.PI * 2) / meta.totalSlots
  53 |     const gridRadius = radius - 0.03
  54 | 
  55 |     for (let layerIndex = 0; layerIndex < groupCount; layerIndex += 1) {
  56 |       const layerBottom = baseY + layerIndex * (LAYER_HEIGHT + LAYER_GAP)
  57 |       const layerTop = layerBottom + LAYER_HEIGHT
  58 |       pushCircle(gridPoints, layerBottom, gridRadius)
  59 |       pushCircle(gridPoints, layerTop, gridRadius)
  60 |     }
  61 | 
  62 |     for (let slotIndex = 0; slotIndex < meta.totalSlots; slotIndex += 1) {
  63 |       const boundaryAngle = slotAngle(slotIndex + 1, meta.totalSlots) - slotStep / 2
  64 |       pushMeridian(gridPoints, boundaryAngle, baseY, yTop, gridRadius)
  65 |     }
  66 | 
  67 |     for (let dayIndex = 1; dayIndex < meta.days.length; dayIndex += 1) {
  68 |       const dayBoundaryAngle =
  69 |         slotAngle(dayIndex * meta.periodsPerDay + 1, meta.totalSlots) - slotStep / 2
  70 |       pushMeridian(dayPoints, dayBoundaryAngle, baseY, yTop, gridRadius + 0.015)
  71 |     }
  72 | 
  73 |     const lineGeometry = new BufferGeometry()
  74 |     lineGeometry.setAttribute('position', new Float32BufferAttribute(gridPoints, 3))
  75 | 
  76 |     const dayLineGeometry = new BufferGeometry()
  77 |     dayLineGeometry.setAttribute('position', new Float32BufferAttribute(dayPoints, 3))
  78 | 
  79 |     return { lineGeometry, dayLineGeometry }
  80 |   }, [baseY, groupCount, meta.days.length, meta.periodsPerDay, meta.totalSlots, radius, totalHeight])
  81 | 
  82 |   return (
  83 |     <group>
  84 |       <lineSegments geometry={lineGeometry}>
  85 |         <lineBasicMaterial color="#5a718d" transparent opacity={0.42} />
  86 |       </lineSegments>
  87 |       <lineSegments geometry={dayLineGeometry}>
  88 |         <lineBasicMaterial color="#8ea8c4" transparent opacity={0.72} />
  89 |       </lineSegments>
  90 |     </group>
  91 |   )
  92 | }
  93 |

   1 | import type { ReactNode } from 'react'
   2 | import { TeacherCombobox } from './TeacherCombobox'
   3 | 
   4 | type Column<T> = {
   5 |   key: keyof T | string
   6 |   title: string
   7 |   width?: string
   8 |   className?: string
   9 |   render?: (row: T, index: number) => ReactNode
  10 |   editable?: boolean
  11 |   inputType?: 'text' | 'number' | 'select' | 'datalist'
  12 |   options?: { value: string; label: string }[]
  13 |   datalistOptions?: string[]
  14 |   comboboxPlaceholder?: string
  15 |   comboboxEmptyHint?: string
  16 |   comboboxSearchMode?: 'teacher' | 'text'
  17 | }
  18 | 
  19 | type DataTableProps<T extends { id: string }> = {
  20 |   rows: T[]
  21 |   columns: Column<T>[]
  22 |   onChange: (id: string, key: keyof T, value: string | number) => void
  23 |   onDelete?: (id: string) => void
  24 |   emptyText?: string
  25 |   tableClassName?: string
  26 | }
  27 | 
  28 | export function DataTable<T extends { id: string }>({
  29 |   rows,
  30 |   columns,
  31 |   onChange,
  32 |   onDelete,
  33 |   emptyText = 'Немає рядків',
  34 |   tableClassName,
  35 | }: DataTableProps<T>) {
  36 |   if (rows.length === 0) {
  37 |     return <p className="muted table-empty">{emptyText}</p>
  38 |   }
  39 | 
  40 |   return (
  41 |     <div className="table-wrap">
  42 |       <table className={tableClassName ? `data-table ${tableClassName}` : 'data-table'}>
  43 |         <thead>
  44 |           <tr>
  45 |             {columns.map((col) => (
  46 |               <th
  47 |                 key={String(col.key)}
  48 |                 className={col.className}
  49 |                 style={col.width ? { width: col.width, maxWidth: col.width } : undefined}
  50 |               >
  51 |                 {col.title}
  52 |               </th>
  53 |             ))}
  54 |             {onDelete ? <th style={{ width: 48 }} /> : null}
  55 |           </tr>
  56 |         </thead>
  57 |         <tbody>
  58 |           {rows.map((row, index) => (
  59 |             <tr key={row.id}>
  60 |               {columns.map((col) => {
  61 |                 const key = col.key as keyof T
  62 |                 const cellStyle = col.width ? { width: col.width, maxWidth: col.width } : undefined
  63 |                 if (col.render) {
  64 |                   return (
  65 |                     <td key={String(col.key)} className={col.className} style={cellStyle}>
  66 |                       {col.render(row, index)}
  67 |                     </td>
  68 |                   )
  69 |                 }
  70 |                 const value = row[key]
  71 |                 if (!col.editable) {
  72 |                   return (
  73 |                     <td key={String(col.key)} className={col.className} style={cellStyle}>
  74 |                       {String(value ?? '')}
  75 |                     </td>
  76 |                   )
  77 |                 }
  78 |                 if (col.inputType === 'select' && col.options) {
  79 |                   return (
  80 |                     <td key={String(col.key)} className={col.className} style={cellStyle}>
  81 |                       <select
  82 |                         value={String(value ?? '')}
  83 |                         onChange={(e) => onChange(row.id, key, e.target.value)}
  84 |                       >
  85 |                         {col.options.map((opt) => (
  86 |                           <option key={opt.value} value={opt.value}>
  87 |                             {opt.label}
  88 |                           </option>
  89 |                         ))}
  90 |                       </select>
  91 |                     </td>
  92 |                   )
  93 |                 }
  94 |                 if (col.inputType === 'datalist' && col.datalistOptions) {
  95 |                   return (
  96 |                     <td key={String(col.key)} className={col.className} style={cellStyle}>
  97 |                       <TeacherCombobox
  98 |                         value={value === undefined || value === null ? '' : String(value)}
  99 |                         options={col.datalistOptions}
 100 |                         placeholder={col.comboboxPlaceholder}
 101 |                         emptyHint={col.comboboxEmptyHint}
 102 |                         searchMode={col.comboboxSearchMode}
 103 |                         onChange={(next) => onChange(row.id, key, next)}
 104 |                       />
 105 |                     </td>
 106 |                   )
 107 |                 }
 108 |                 return (
 109 |                   <td key={String(col.key)} className={col.className} style={cellStyle}>
 110 |                     <input
 111 |                       type={col.inputType === 'number' ? 'number' : 'text'}
 112 |                       value={value === undefined || value === null ? '' : String(value)}
 113 |                       onChange={(e) =>
 114 |                         onChange(
 115 |                           row.id,
 116 |                           key,
 117 |                           col.inputType === 'number' ? Number(e.target.value) : e.target.value,
 118 |                         )
 119 |                       }
 120 |                     />
 121 |                   </td>
 122 |                 )
 123 |               })}
 124 |               {onDelete ? (
 125 |                 <td>
 126 |                   <button type="button" className="btn-icon" onClick={() => onDelete(row.id)} title="Видалити">
 127 |                     ×
 128 |                   </button>
 129 |                 </td>
 130 |               ) : null}
 131 |             </tr>
 132 |           ))}
 133 |         </tbody>
 134 |       </table>
 135 |     </div>
 136 |   )
 137 | }

  19 | export function DetailPanel({ selected, groups, compact = false, layout = 'panel' }: DetailPanelProps) {

   1 | import { useCallback, useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react'
   2 | import type { NavPlanSnapshot, PrintScheduleDocument, ScheduleDocument } from '../types/documents'
   3 | 
   4 | type SnapshotItem = NavPlanSnapshot
   5 | type ScheduleItem = ScheduleDocument
   6 | type PrintItem = PrintScheduleDocument
   7 | 
   8 | type DocumentVersionsPanelProps =
   9 |   | {
  10 |       kind: 'navPlan'
  11 |       items: SnapshotItem[]
  12 |       onRefresh: () => Promise<void>
  13 |       onSave: (label: string, note: string) => Promise<void>
  14 |       onRestore: (id: string) => Promise<void>
  15 |       onDelete: (id: string) => Promise<void>
  16 |       onExport: (item: SnapshotItem) => void
  17 |       onExportCurrent: (label: string, note: string) => void
  18 |       onImport: (file: File) => Promise<void>
  19 |       canExportCurrent?: boolean
  20 |     }
  21 |   | {
  22 |       kind: 'schedule'

  24 |       onRefresh: () => Promise<void>

  26 |       onLoad: (id: string) => Promise<void>
  27 |       onDelete: (id: string) => Promise<void>
  28 |       onExport: (item: ScheduleItem) => void
  29 |       onImport: (file: File) => Promise<void>
  30 |       onExportCurrent?: (label: string, note: string) => void
  31 |       canExportCurrent?: boolean

  33 |   | {

  40 |     }
  41 | 
  42 | export function DocumentVersionsPanel(props: DocumentVersionsPanelProps) {
  43 |   const [label, setLabel] = useState('')
  44 |   const [note, setNote] = useState('')
  45 |   const [busy, setBusy] = useState(false)
  46 |   const importRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null)
  47 | 
  48 |   useEffect(() => {
  49 |     void props.onRefresh()
  50 |   }, [props.kind])
  51 | 
  52 |   const titles = {
  53 |     navPlan: 'Версії навплану',
  54 |     schedule: 'Збережені розклади',
  55 |     print: 'Розклади для друку',
  56 |   }
  57 | 
  58 |   const handleSave = useCallback(async () => {
  59 |     if (props.kind === 'print') return
  60 |     setBusy(true)
  61 |     try {
  62 |       await props.onSave(label, note)
  63 |       setLabel('')
  64 |       setNote('')
  65 |       await props.onRefresh()
  66 |     } finally {
  67 |       setBusy(false)
  68 |     }
  69 |   }, [props, label, note])
  70 | 
  71 |   const handleImportFile = useCallback(
  72 |     async (file: File | undefined) => {
  73 |       if (!file || (props.kind !== 'navPlan' && props.kind !== 'schedule')) return
  74 |       setBusy(true)
  75 |       try {
  76 |         await props.onImport(file)
  77 |       } finally {
  78 |         setBusy(false)
  79 |         if (importRef.current) importRef.current.value = ''
  80 |       }
  81 |     },
  82 |     [props],
  83 |   )
  84 | 
  85 |   return (
  86 |     <section className="panel section-block document-versions document-versions-top">
  87 |       <div className="document-versions-head">
  88 |         <h2>{titles[props.kind]}</h2>
  89 |         {props.kind !== 'print' ? (
  90 |           <div className="document-versions-save">
  91 |             <input
  92 |               type="text"
  93 |               placeholder="Назва версії"
  94 |               value={label}
  95 |               onChange={(e) => setLabel(e.target.value)}
  96 |             />
  97 |             <input
  98 |               type="text"
  99 |               placeholder="Примітка (необовʼязково)"
 100 |               value={note}
 101 |               onChange={(e) => setNote(e.target.value)}
 102 |             />
 103 |             <button type="button" className="btn primary" disabled={busy} onClick={() => void handleSave()}>
 104 |               Зберегти версію
 105 |             </button>
 106 |             {props.kind === 'navPlan' ? (
 107 |               <>
 108 |                 <button
 109 |                   type="button"
 110 |                   className="btn"
 111 |                   disabled={busy || props.canExportCurrent === false}
 112 |                   onClick={() => props.onExportCurrent(label, note)}
 113 |                 >
 114 |                   Експорт JSON
 115 |                 </button>
 116 |                 <input
 117 |                   ref={importRef}
 118 |                   type="file"
 119 |                   accept=".json,application/json"
 120 |                   hidden
 121 |                   onChange={(e) => void handleImportFile(e.target.files?.[0])}
 122 |                 />
 123 |                 <button
 124 |                   type="button"
 125 |                   className="btn"
 126 |                   disabled={busy}
 127 |                   onClick={() => importRef.current?.click()}
 128 |                 >
 129 |                   Імпорт JSON
 130 |                 </button>
 131 |               </>
 132 |             ) : null}
 133 |             {props.kind === 'schedule' ? (
 134 |               <>
 135 |                 <button
 136 |                   type="button"
 137 |                   className="btn"
 138 |                   disabled={busy || props.canExportCurrent === false}
 139 |                   onClick={() => props.onExportCurrent?.(label, note)}
 140 |                 >

 142 |                 </button>

 155 |                 >
 156 |                   Імпорт JSON
 157 |                 </button>
 158 |               </>
 159 |             ) : null}
 160 |           </div>
 161 |         ) : null}
 162 |       </div>
 163 | 
 164 |       {props.kind === 'navPlan' ? (
 165 |         <p className="muted document-versions-hint">
 166 |           JSON містить <code>savedBy</code>, <code>savedAt</code>, назву та дані навплану. Імпорт завантажує файл у
 167 |           поточну таблицю.
 168 |         </p>
 169 |       ) : null}
 170 |       {props.kind === 'schedule' ? (

 173 |           розкладу. Після імпорту розклад одразу доступний у 3D і для друку.
 174 |         </p>
 175 |       ) : null}
 176 |

 178 |         <p className="muted">Поки немає збережених записів.</p>
 179 |       ) : (
 180 |         <ul className="document-versions-list">
 181 |           {props.items.map((item) => (
 182 |             <li key={item.id}>

 193 |                 </span>

 195 |               </div>
 196 |               <div className="document-versions-actions">
 197 |                 {props.kind === 'navPlan' ? (
 198 |                   <button type="button" className="btn" onClick={() => void props.onRestore(item.id)}>
 199 |                     Завантажити
 200 |                   </button>
 201 |                 ) : null}
 202 |                 {props.kind === 'schedule' ? (
 203 |                   <button type="button" className="btn" onClick={() => void props.onLoad(item.id)}>
 204 |                     Відкрити
 205 |                   </button>
 206 |                 ) : null}
 207 |                 {props.kind === 'print' ? (
 208 |                   <button type="button" className="btn primary" onClick={() => props.onPrint(item)}>
 209 |                     Друкувати
 210 |                   </button>
 211 |                 ) : null}
 212 |                 {props.kind !== 'print' ? (
 213 |                   <button type="button" className="btn" onClick={() => props.onExport(item as never)}>
 214 |                     Експорт

 216 |                 ) : (

 218 |                     JSON
 219 |                   </button>

 221 |                 <button
 222 |                   type="button"
 223 |                   className="btn btn-danger-text"
 224 |                   onClick={() => void props.onDelete(item.id).then(() => props.onRefresh())}

  49 | function numValue(value: number): string {
  50 |   return value === 0 ? '' : String(value)
  51 | }
  52 | 
  53 | function NumCell({
  54 |   rowId,
  55 |   field,
  56 |   value,
  57 |   tone,
  58 |   onChange,
  59 | }: {
  60 |   rowId: string
  61 |   field: keyof NavPlanRow
  62 |   value: number
  63 |   tone: 'shared' | 'fall' | 'spring' | 'year'
  64 |   onChange: NavPlanTableProps['onChange']
  65 | }) {
  66 |   return (
  67 |     <td className={`col-num col-tone-${tone}`}>
  68 |       <input
  69 |         type="number"
  70 |         min={0}
  71 |         inputMode="numeric"
  72 |         value={numValue(value)}
  73 |         onChange={(e) =>
  74 |           onChange(rowId, field, e.target.value === '' ? 0 : Number(e.target.value))
  75 |         }
  76 |       />
  77 |     </td>
  78 |   )
  79 | }

  81 | export function navPlanNeedsReimport(rows: NavPlanRow[]): boolean {
  82 |   return rows.some((row) => {
  83 |     const fallDetail =
  84 |       row.fallLectures +
  85 |       row.fallPractical +
  86 |       row.fallLab +
  87 |       row.fallCoursework +
  88 |       row.fallConsult +
  89 |       row.fallCredits +
  90 |       row.fallExams
  91 |     const springDetail =
  92 |       row.springLectures +
  93 |       row.springPractical +
  94 |       row.springLab +
  95 |       row.springCoursework +
  96 |       row.springConsult +
  97 |       row.springSupervised +
  98 |       row.springCredits +
  99 |       row.springExams +
 100 |       row.springDpa +
 101 |       row.springDkk
 102 | 
 103 |     if (row.hoursTotal > 0 && fallDetail === 0 && springDetail === 0 && row.hoursFall === 0 && row.hoursSpring === 0) {
 104 |       return false
 105 |     }
 106 | 
 107 |     if ((row.hoursFall > 0 || row.hoursSpring > 0) && row.hoursTotal === 0) return true
 108 |     if (row.hoursFall > 0 && fallDetail === 0) return true
 109 |     if (row.hoursSpring > 0 && springDetail === 0) return true
 110 |     return false
 111 |   })
 112 | }

 114 | export function NavPlanTable({
 115 |   rows,
 116 |   onChange,
 117 |   onDelete,
 118 |   emptyText = 'Немає рядків',
 119 | }: NavPlanTableProps) {
 120 |   if (rows.length === 0) {
 121 |     return <p className="muted table-empty">{emptyText}</p>
 122 |   }
 123 | 
 124 |   return (
 125 |     <div className="nav-plan-scroll">
 126 |       <table className="data-table nav-plan-table">
 127 |         <thead>
 128 |           <tr className="nav-plan-group-row">
 129 |             <th colSpan={3} className="sticky-col sticky-0 nav-plan-corner" />
 130 |             <th colSpan={SHARED_COLS.length} className="nav-plan-group shared-group">
 131 |               Кількість годин
 132 |             </th>
 133 |             <th colSpan={FALL_COLS.length} className="nav-plan-group fall-group">
 134 |               Осінній семестр
 135 |             </th>
 136 |             <th colSpan={SPRING_COLS.length} className="nav-plan-group spring-group">
 137 |               Весняний семестр
 138 |             </th>
 139 |             <th colSpan={YEAR_COLS.length} className="nav-plan-group year-group">
 140 |               За навч. рік
 141 |             </th>
 142 |             {onDelete ? <th className="col-delete" rowSpan={2} /> : null}
 143 |           </tr>
 144 |           <tr>
 145 |             <th className="sticky-col sticky-0 col-group">Група</th>
 146 |             <th className="sticky-col sticky-1 col-subject">Предмет</th>
 147 |             <th className="sticky-col sticky-2 col-teacher">Викладач</th>
 148 |             {SHARED_COLS.map((col) => (
 149 |               <th key={String(col.key)} className="col-vhead shared-group">
 150 |                 {col.title}
 151 |               </th>
 152 |             ))}
 153 |             {FALL_COLS.map((col) => (
 154 |               <th key={String(col.key)} className="col-vhead fall-group">
 155 |                 {col.title}
 156 |               </th>
 157 |             ))}
 158 |             {SPRING_COLS.map((col) => (
 159 |               <th key={String(col.key)} className="col-vhead spring-group">
 160 |                 {col.title}
 161 |               </th>
 162 |             ))}
 163 |             {YEAR_COLS.map((col) => (
 164 |               <th key={String(col.key)} className="col-vhead year-group">
 165 |                 {col.title}
 166 |               </th>
 167 |             ))}
 168 |           </tr>
 169 |         </thead>
 170 |         <tbody>
 171 |           {rows.map((row) => (
 172 |             <tr
 173 |               key={row.id}
 174 |               className={row.planKind !== 'schedule' ? 'nav-plan-row-excluded' : undefined}
 175 |             >
 176 |               <td className="sticky-col sticky-0 col-group">
 177 |                 <input
 178 |                   value={row.groupCode}
 179 |                   onChange={(e) => onChange(row.id, 'groupCode', e.target.value)}
 180 |                 />
 181 |               </td>
 182 |               <td className="sticky-col sticky-1 col-subject">
 183 |                 <input
 184 |                   title={row.subject}
 185 |                   value={row.subject}
 186 |                   onChange={(e) => onChange(row.id, 'subject', e.target.value)}
 187 |                 />
 188 |                 {row.planKind !== 'schedule' ? (
 189 |                   <span className="plan-kind-badge" title={row.planKindLabel}>
 190 |                     {row.planKindLabel}
 191 |                   </span>
 192 |                 ) : null}
 193 |               </td>
 194 |               <td className="sticky-col sticky-2 col-teacher">
 195 |                 <input
 196 |                   value={row.teacher}
 197 |                   onChange={(e) => onChange(row.id, 'teacher', e.target.value)}
 198 |                 />
 199 |               </td>
 200 |               {SHARED_COLS.map((col) => (
 201 |                 <NumCell
 202 |                   key={String(col.key)}
 203 |                   rowId={row.id}
 204 |                   field={col.key}
 205 |                   value={row[col.key] as number}
 206 |                   tone="shared"
 207 |                   onChange={onChange}
 208 |                 />
 209 |               ))}
 210 |               {FALL_COLS.map((col) => (
 211 |                 <NumCell
 212 |                   key={String(col.key)}
 213 |                   rowId={row.id}
 214 |                   field={col.key}
 215 |                   value={row[col.key] as number}
 216 |                   tone="fall"
 217 |                   onChange={onChange}
 218 |                 />
 219 |               ))}
 220 |               {SPRING_COLS.map((col) => (
 221 |                 <NumCell
 222 |                   key={String(col.key)}
 223 |                   rowId={row.id}
 224 |                   field={col.key}
 225 |                   value={row[col.key] as number}
 226 |                   tone="spring"
 227 |                   onChange={onChange}
 228 |                 />

 236 |                   tone="year"
 237 |                   onChange={onChange}

 240 |               {onDelete ? (

 252 |             </tr>
 253 |           ))}
 254 |         </tbody>
 255 |       </table>
 256 |     </div>

   1 | import type { ScheduleBuildState } from '../context/PlanningContext'
   2 | 
   3 | export function ScheduleBuildProgress({ build }: { build: ScheduleBuildState }) {
   4 |   if (!build.running && !build.lastResult && !build.error) return null
   5 | 
   6 |   return (
   7 |     <section
   8 |       className={`panel section-block schedule-build-panel${build.running ? ' is-running' : ''}${build.error ? ' has-error' : ''}`}

  10 |     >
  11 |       <div className="schedule-build-head">
  12 |         <h2>{build.running ? 'Збираємо розклад…' : build.error ? 'Помилка' : 'Збірку завершено'}</h2>
  13 |         <span className="schedule-build-percent">{build.progress}%</span>
  14 |       </div>
  15 | 
  16 |       <div className="progress-track" role="progressbar" aria-valuenow={build.progress} aria-valuemin={0} aria-valuemax={100}>
  17 |         <div className="progress-fill" style={{ width: `${build.progress}%` }} />
  18 |       </div>
  19 | 
  20 |       <p className="schedule-build-stage">
  21 |         <strong>{build.stage}</strong>
  22 |         {build.detail ? <span className="muted"> · {build.detail}</span> : null}
  23 |       </p>
  24 | 
  25 |       {build.error ? <p className="error-banner">{build.error}</p> : null}
  26 | 
  27 |       {build.lastResult && !build.running ? (
  28 |         <ul className="rules-list schedule-build-warnings">
  29 |           {build.lastResult.warnings.map((line) => (
  30 |             <li key={line}>{line}</li>
  31 |           ))}
  32 |         </ul>
  33 |       ) : null}
  34 |     </section>
  35 |   )
  36 | }

   1 | import { useMemo, useRef } from 'react'

   8 |   clusterEntries,
   9 |   shortDisplayText,
  10 |   type ScheduleEntryCluster,
  11 | } from '../utils/scheduleClusters'

  14 |   CELL_DEPTH,

  24 | type ScheduleCylinderProps = {
  25 |   groups: Group[]

  36 |   } | null

  38 | 
  39 | function worstConflict(entries: EnrichedEntry[]): ConflictKind {
  40 |   if (entries.some((entry) => entry.conflict === 'teacher')) return 'teacher'
  41 |   if (entries.some((entry) => entry.conflict === 'room')) return 'room'
  42 |   return 'none'
  43 | }
  44 | 
  45 | function clusterIsActive(cluster: ScheduleEntryCluster, entryId: string | null): boolean {
  46 |   if (!entryId) return false
  47 |   return cluster.entries.some((entry) => entry.id === entryId)
  48 | }
  49 | 
  50 | export function ScheduleCylinder({
  51 |   groups,
  52 |   entries,
  53 |   meta,
  54 |   selectedEntryId,
  55 |   hoveredEntryId,
  56 |   onSelect,
  57 |   onHover,
  58 |   teacherProjection,
  59 | }: ScheduleCylinderProps) {
  60 |   const clustersByGroup = useMemo(() => {
  61 |     const map = new Map<string, ScheduleEntryCluster[]>()
  62 |     for (const group of groups) map.set(group.id, [])
  63 |     for (const group of groups) {
  64 |       const groupEntries = entries.filter((entry) => entry.groupId === group.id)
  65 |       map.set(group.id, clusterEntries(groupEntries))
  66 |     }
  67 |     return map
  68 |   }, [groups, entries])
  69 | 
  70 |   const layout = useMemo(() => computeCylinderLayout(groups.length), [groups.length])
  71 |   const { baseY, totalHeight, orbitPivotY } = layout
  72 | 
  73 |   return (
  74 |     <group position={[0, -orbitPivotY, 0]}>
  75 |       <CylinderSurfaceGrid
  76 |         meta={meta}
  77 |         groupCount={groups.length}
  78 |         baseY={baseY}
  79 |         totalHeight={totalHeight}
  80 |         radius={CYLINDER_RADIUS}
  81 |       />
  82 | 
  83 |       {groups.map((group, groupIndex) => {
  84 |         const y = baseY + groupIndex * (LAYER_HEIGHT + LAYER_GAP) + LAYER_HEIGHT / 2
  85 |         const clusters = clustersByGroup.get(group.id) ?? []
  86 | 
  87 |         return (
  88 |           <group key={group.id} position={[0, y, 0]}>
  89 |             <Text
  90 |               position={[CYLINDER_RADIUS + 0.9, 0, 0]}
  91 |               fontSize={0.22}
  92 |               color="#d7e3ff"
  93 |               anchorX="left"
  94 |               anchorY="middle"
  95 |             >
  96 |               {group.code}
  97 |             </Text>
  98 | 
  99 |             {clusters.map((cluster) => {
 100 |               const angle = slotAngle(cluster.primary.slotId, meta.totalSlots)
 101 |               const ringRadius = CYLINDER_RADIUS + CELL_DEPTH / 2
 102 |               const x = Math.cos(angle) * ringRadius
 103 |               const z = Math.sin(angle) * ringRadius
 104 |               const selected = clusterIsActive(cluster, selectedEntryId)
 105 |               const hovered = clusterIsActive(cluster, hoveredEntryId)
 106 |               const color = conflictColor(worstConflict(cluster.entries), selected, hovered)
 107 |               const { day, period } = slotToDayPeriod(cluster.primary.slotId, meta)
 108 |               const slotLabel = cluster.parallel ? `${day}${period} · поділ` : `${day}${period}`
 109 | 
 110 |               return (
 111 |                 <ScheduleCell
 112 |                   key={cluster.key}
 113 |                   cluster={cluster}
 114 |                   position={[x, 0, z]}
 115 |                   rotation={[0, -angle + Math.PI / 2, 0]}
 116 |                   color={color}
 117 |                   slotLabel={slotLabel}
 118 |                   selected={selected}
 119 |                   onSelect={() => onSelect(cluster.primary.id)}
 120 |                   onHover={(value) => onHover(value ? cluster.primary.id : null)}
 121 |                 />
 122 |               )
 123 |             })}
 124 |           </group>
 125 |         )
 126 |       })}
 127 | 
 128 |       <TimeSlotRing
 129 |         meta={meta}
 130 |         baseY={baseY}
 131 |         cylinderRadius={CYLINDER_RADIUS}
 132 |         entries={entries}
 133 |         selectedEntryId={selectedEntryId}
 134 |         hoveredEntryId={hoveredEntryId}
 135 |         teacherProjection={teacherProjection}
 136 |       />
 137 |     </group>
 138 |   )
 139 | }
 140 | 
 141 | type ScheduleCellProps = {
 142 |   cluster: ScheduleEntryCluster

 144 |   rotation: [number, number, number]
 145 |   color: string
 146 |   slotLabel: string
 147 |   selected: boolean
 148 |   onSelect: () => void
 149 |   onHover: (active: boolean) => void

 152 | function ScheduleCell({
 153 |   cluster,
 154 |   position,
 155 |   rotation,
 156 |   color,
 157 |   slotLabel,
 158 |   selected,
 159 |   onSelect,
 160 |   onHover,
 161 | }: ScheduleCellProps) {
 162 |   const meshRef = useRef<Mesh>(null)
 163 |   const subjectLine = shortDisplayText(cluster.subject, cluster.parallel ? 18 : 24)
 164 |   const detailLine = cluster.parallel
 165 |     ? shortDisplayText(cluster.teachers.join(' · '), 28)
 166 |     : shortDisplayText(cluster.primary.teacher, 18)
 167 |   const widthScale = cluster.parallel ? 1.25 : 1
 168 |   const boxHeight = LAYER_HEIGHT * 0.72
 169 |   const faceZ = CELL_DEPTH / 2 + 0.02
 170 | 
 171 |   const handlePointerDown = (event: ThreeEvent<PointerEvent>) => {
 172 |     event.stopPropagation()
 173 |     onSelect()
 174 |   }
 175 | 
 176 |   return (
 177 |     <group position={position} rotation={rotation}>
 178 |       <mesh
 179 |         ref={meshRef}
 180 |         onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
 181 |         onPointerOver={(event) => {
 182 |           event.stopPropagation()
 183 |           onHover(true)
 184 |           document.body.style.cursor = 'pointer'
 185 |         }}
 186 |         onPointerOut={() => {
 187 |           onHover(false)
 188 |           document.body.style.cursor = 'default'
 189 |         }}
 190 |         scale={selected ? [widthScale * 1.12, 1.12, 1.12] : [widthScale, 1, 1]}
 191 |       >
 192 |         <boxGeometry args={[CELL_WIDTH, LAYER_HEIGHT * 0.72, CELL_DEPTH]} />
 193 |         <meshStandardMaterial color={color} emissive={color} emissiveIntensity={selected ? 0.35 : 0.12} />
 194 |       </mesh>
 195 |       <Text
 196 |         position={[0, boxHeight / 2 - 0.02, faceZ]}
 197 |         fontSize={0.095}
 198 |         color="#f8fbff"
 199 |         anchorX="center"
 200 |         anchorY="bottom"
 201 |         renderOrder={12}
 202 |         outlineWidth={0.008}
 203 |         outlineColor="#0b1220"
 204 |         material-depthTest={false}
 205 |       >
 206 |         {slotLabel}
 207 |       </Text>
 208 |       <Text
 209 |         position={[0, 0.02, faceZ]}
 210 |         fontSize={0.062}

   1 | import { OrbitControls, PerspectiveCamera } from '@react-three/drei'

   3 | import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react'
   4 | import type { OrbitControls as OrbitControlsImpl } from 'three-stdlib'
   5 | import { Vector3 } from 'three'
   6 | import { useTheme } from '../context/ThemeContext'
   7 | import type { EnrichedEntry, Group, ScheduleMeta } from '../types/schedule'
   8 | import { ScheduleCylinder } from './ScheduleCylinder'
   9 | 
  10 | type ScheduleSceneProps = {
  11 |   groups: Group[]
  12 |   entries: EnrichedEntry[]
  13 |   meta: ScheduleMeta
  14 |   selectedEntryId: string | null
  15 |   hoveredEntryId: string | null
  16 |   onSelect: (entryId: string) => void
  17 |   onHover: (entryId: string | null) => void
  18 |   teacherProjection?: {
  19 |     teacher: string
  20 |     entries: EnrichedEntry[]
  21 |     groups: Group[]
  22 |   } | null
  23 | }
  24 | 
  25 | const ORBIT_TARGET = new Vector3(0, 0, 0)
  26 | const DEFAULT_CAMERA = { position: [8, 6, 10] as const, fov: 50 }
  27 | 
  28 | function SceneControls({ groupCount }: { groupCount: number }) {
  29 |   const controlsRef = useRef<OrbitControlsImpl>(null)
  30 | 
  31 |   useEffect(() => {
  32 |     const controls = controlsRef.current
  33 |     if (!controls) return
  34 |     controls.target.copy(ORBIT_TARGET)
  35 |     controls.update()
  36 |   }, [groupCount])
  37 | 
  38 |   return (
  39 |     <OrbitControls
  40 |       ref={controlsRef}
  41 |       makeDefault
  42 |       enablePan
  43 |       enableZoom
  44 |       zoomSpeed={1.15}
  45 |       minDistance={3}
  46 |       maxDistance={72}
  47 |       maxPolarAngle={Math.PI / 1.7}
  48 |       screenSpacePanning={false}
  49 |       target={ORBIT_TARGET}
  50 |     />
  51 |   )
  52 | }
  53 | 
  54 | export function ScheduleScene(props: ScheduleSceneProps) {
  55 |   const { sceneBackground } = useTheme()
  56 |   const wrapRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  57 | 
  58 |   useEffect(() => {
  59 |     const root = wrapRef.current
  60 |     if (!root) return
  61 |     const canvas = root.querySelector('canvas')
  62 |     if (!canvas) return
  63 | 
  64 |     const blockPageScroll = (event: WheelEvent) => {
  65 |       event.preventDefault()
  66 |     }
  67 | 
  68 |     canvas.addEventListener('wheel', blockPageScroll, { passive: false })
  69 |     return () => canvas.removeEventListener('wheel', blockPageScroll)
  70 |   }, [])
  71 | 
  72 |   return (
  73 |     <div ref={wrapRef} className="scene-canvas-wrap">
  74 |       <Canvas className="scene-canvas" dpr={[1, 2]} gl={{ antialias: true }}>
  75 |         <color attach="background" args={[sceneBackground]} />
  76 |         <PerspectiveCamera makeDefault position={DEFAULT_CAMERA.position} fov={DEFAULT_CAMERA.fov} />
  77 |         <ambientLight intensity={0.55} />
  78 |         <directionalLight position={[8, 12, 6]} intensity={1.1} />
  79 |         <directionalLight position={[-6, 4, -8]} intensity={0.35} />
  80 |         <ScheduleCylinder {...props} />
  81 |         <SceneControls groupCount={props.groups.length} />
  82 |       </Canvas>
  83 |     </div>
  84 |   )
  85 | }

   1 | import type { EnrichedEntry, Group, ScheduleMeta } from '../types/schedule'
   2 | import { describeConflictsForEntry, type DescribedConflict } from '../utils/conflicts'
   3 | import { clusterEntries, clusterKeyForGroup } from '../utils/scheduleClusters'
   4 | import { parallelSubjectKey } from '../utils/parallelSubgroups'
   5 | import { slotLabel, slotToDayPeriod } from '../utils/slots'
   6 | 
   7 | type ScheduleWeekProjectionProps = {
   8 |   title: string
   9 |   entries: EnrichedEntry[]
  10 |   groups: Group[]
  11 |   meta: ScheduleMeta
  12 |   /** teacher — показувати групу; group — показувати викладача */
  13 |   mode: 'teacher' | 'group'
  14 |   /** Очікування з навплану (для порівняння) */
  15 |   expectedBySubject?: Array<{
  16 |     subject: string
  17 |     groups: Array<{ code: string; pairsPerWeek: number }>
  18 |   }>
  19 | }
  20 | 
  21 | function shortSubject(subject: string, max = 28): string {
  22 |   const trimmed = subject.trim()
  23 |   if (trimmed.length <= max) return trimmed
  24 |   return `${trimmed.slice(0, max - 1)}…`
  25 | }
  26 | 
  27 | function clusterKey(entry: EnrichedEntry): string {
  28 |   return `s|${entry.id}`
  29 | }
  30 | 
  31 | type WeekListItem = {
  32 |   key: string
  33 |   slot: string
  34 |   period: number
  35 |   group: string
  36 |   teachers: string[]
  37 |   subject: string
  38 |   fullSubject: string
  39 |   rooms: string[]
  40 |   hasConflict: boolean
  41 |   conflictWith: string[]
  42 |   parallel: boolean
  43 | }
  44 | 
  45 | function formatConflictLine(item: DescribedConflict): string {
  46 |   return `[${item.reasonLabel}] ${item.summary}`
  47 | }
  48 | 
  49 | function uniqueConflictLines(items: DescribedConflict[]): string[] {
  50 |   const seen = new Set<string>()
  51 |   const result: string[] = []
  52 |   for (const item of items) {
  53 |     const line = formatConflictLine(item)
  54 |     if (seen.has(line)) continue
  55 |     seen.add(line)
  56 |     result.push(line)
  57 |   }
  58 |   return result
  59 | }
  60 | 
  61 | function buildWeekListItems(
  62 |   dayEntries: EnrichedEntry[],
  63 |   meta: ScheduleMeta,
  64 |   groupById: Map<string, Group>,
  65 |   allEntries: EnrichedEntry[],
  66 | ): WeekListItem[] {
  67 |   return clusterEntries(dayEntries)
  68 |     .map((cluster) => {
  69 |       const { period } = slotToDayPeriod(cluster.primary.slotId, meta)
  70 |       const conflictWith = uniqueConflictLines(
  71 |         cluster.entries.flatMap((entry) => describeConflictsForEntry(entry, allEntries, groupById)),
  72 |       )
  73 |       return {
  74 |         key: cluster.key,
  75 |         slot: slotLabel(cluster.primary.slotId, meta),
  76 |         period,
  77 |         group: groupById.get(cluster.primary.groupId)?.code ?? '?',
  78 |         teachers: cluster.teachers,
  79 |         subject: shortSubject(cluster.subject),
  80 |         fullSubject: cluster.subject,
  81 |         rooms: cluster.rooms,
  82 |         hasConflict: cluster.entries.some((e) => e.conflict !== 'none'),
  83 |         conflictWith,
  84 |         parallel: cluster.parallel,
  85 |       }
  86 |     })
  87 |     .sort((a, b) => a.period - b.period)
  88 | }
  89 | 
  90 | export function ScheduleWeekProjection({
  91 |   title,
  92 |   entries,
  93 |   groups,
  94 |   meta,
  95 |   mode,
  96 |   expectedBySubject,
  97 | }: ScheduleWeekProjectionProps) {
  98 |   const groupById = new Map(groups.map((g) => [g.id, g]))
  99 | 
 100 |   const actualBySubject = [...(() => {
 101 |     const map = new Map<string, { label: string; groups: Map<string, Set<string>> }>()
 102 |     for (const entry of entries) {
 103 |       const group = groupById.get(entry.groupId)?.code ?? '?'
 104 |       const pKey = parallelSubjectKey(entry.subject)
 105 |       if (!map.has(pKey)) {
 106 |         map.set(pKey, { label: entry.subject, groups: new Map() })
 107 |       }
 108 |       const row = map.get(pKey)!
 109 |       const slots = row.groups.get(group) ?? new Set<string>()
 110 |       slots.add(mode === 'group' ? clusterKeyForGroup(entry) : clusterKey(entry))
 111 |       row.groups.set(group, slots)
 112 |     }
 113 |     return map.values()
 114 |   })()]
 115 |     .sort((a, b) => b.groups.size - a.groups.size || a.label.localeCompare(b.label, 'uk'))
 116 |     .map(({ label, groups }) => ({
 117 |       subject: shortSubject(label, 36),
 118 |       fullSubject: label,
 119 |       tags: [...groups.entries()]
 120 |         .sort((a, b) => a[0].localeCompare(b[0], 'uk'))
 121 |         .map(([code, slotKeys]) => ({ code, count: slotKeys.size })),
 122 |     }))
 123 | 
 124 |   const subjectSummary =
 125 |     mode === 'teacher' && expectedBySubject && expectedBySubject.length > 0
 126 |       ? expectedBySubject.map(({ subject, groups: expectedGroups }) => {
 127 |           const actual = actualBySubject.find(
 128 |             (item) =>
 129 |               item.fullSubject === subject ||
 130 |               item.fullSubject.replace(/\*+/g, '') === subject.replace(/\*+/g, ''),
 131 |           )
 132 |           const tags = expectedGroups.map(({ code, pairsPerWeek }) => {
 133 |             const actualCount = actual?.tags.find((t) => t.code === code)?.count ?? 0
 134 |             return {
 135 |               code,
 136 |               label: actualCount >= pairsPerWeek ? `${code}×${pairsPerWeek}` : `${code}×${actualCount}/${pairsPerWeek}`,
 137 |               missing: actualCount < pairsPerWeek,
 138 |             }
 139 |           })
 140 |           return {
 141 |             subject: shortSubject(subject, 36),
 142 |             fullSubject: subject,
 143 |             tags,
 144 |           }
 145 |         })
 146 |       : actualBySubject.map(({ subject, fullSubject, tags }) => ({
 147 |           subject,
 148 |           fullSubject,
 149 |           tags: tags.map(({ code, count }) => ({
 150 |             code,
 151 |             label: count > 1 ? `${code}×${count}` : code,
 152 |             missing: false,
 153 |           })),
 154 |         }))
 155 | 
 156 |   const missingFromNavPlan =
 157 |     mode === 'teacher' && expectedBySubject
 158 |       ? expectedBySubject.flatMap(({ subject, groups: expectedGroups }) =>
 159 |           expectedGroups.flatMap(({ code, pairsPerWeek }) => {
 160 |             const actual = actualBySubject.find(
 161 |               (item) =>
 162 |                 item.fullSubject === subject ||
 163 |                 item.fullSubject.replace(/\*+/g, '') === subject.replace(/\*+/g, ''),
 164 |             )
 165 |             const actualCount = actual?.tags.find((t) => t.code === code)?.count ?? 0
 166 |             const missing = pairsPerWeek - actualCount
 167 |             if (missing <= 0) return []
 168 |             return [{ subject, group: code, missing }]
 169 |           }),
 170 |         )
 171 |       : []
 172 | 
 173 |   const byDay = meta.days.map((day) => {
 174 |     const dayEntries = entries.filter(
 175 |       (entry) => slotToDayPeriod(entry.slotId, meta).day === day,
 176 |     )
 177 | 
 178 |     if (mode === 'group') {
 179 |       return { day, items: buildWeekListItems(dayEntries, meta, groupById, entries) }
 180 |     }
 181 | 
 182 |     const items = dayEntries
 183 |       .sort(
 184 |         (a, b) =>
 185 |           slotToDayPeriod(a.slotId, meta).period - slotToDayPeriod(b.slotId, meta).period,
 186 |       )
 187 |       .map((entry) => ({
 188 |         key: entry.id,
 189 |         slot: slotLabel(entry.slotId, meta),
 190 |         period: slotToDayPeriod(entry.slotId, meta).period,
 191 |         group: groupById.get(entry.groupId)?.code ?? '?',
 192 |         teachers: [entry.teacher],
 193 |         subject: shortSubject(entry.subject),
 194 |         fullSubject: entry.subject,
 195 |         rooms: [entry.room],
 196 |         hasConflict: entry.conflict !== 'none',
 197 |         conflictWith: describeConflictsForEntry(entry, entries, groupById).map(formatConflictLine),
 198 |         parallel: false,
 199 |       }))
 200 | 
 201 |     return { day, items }
 202 |   })
 203 | 
 204 |   const total =
 205 |     mode === 'group'
 206 |       ? new Set(entries.map((entry) => clusterKeyForGroup(entry))).size
 207 |       : entries.length
 208 | 
 209 |   return (
 210 |     <div className="schedule-week-projection" aria-label={`Розклад ${title}`}>
 211 |       <div className="schedule-week-head">
 212 |         <strong>{title}</strong>
 213 |         <span className="muted">
 214 |           {total} {total === 1 ? 'пара' : total < 5 ? 'пари' : 'пар'} на тиждень
 215 |         </span>
 216 |       </div>
 217 |       <div className="schedule-week-grid">
 218 |         {byDay.map(({ day, items }) => (
 219 |           <div key={day} className="schedule-week-col">
 220 |             <div className="schedule-week-day">{day}</div>
 221 |             {items.length === 0 ? (
 222 |               <p className="schedule-week-empty muted">—</p>
 223 |             ) : (
 224 |               <ul className="schedule-week-list">
 225 |                 {items.map((item) => (
 226 |                   <li
 227 |                     key={item.key}
 228 |                     className={
 229 |                       item.hasConflict
 230 |                         ? 'has-conflict'
 231 |                         : item.parallel
 232 |                           ? 'is-parallel'
 233 |                           : undefined
 234 |                     }
 235 |                   >
 236 |                     <span className="schedule-week-slot">{item.slot}</span>
 237 |                     {mode === 'teacher' ? (
 238 |                       <span className="schedule-week-tag group-tag">{item.group}</span>
 239 |                     ) : item.parallel ? (
 240 |                       <span className="schedule-week-parallel-badge" title="Паралельні підгрупи">
 241 |                         поділ
 242 |                       </span>
 243 |                     ) : (
 244 |                       <span className="schedule-week-tag teacher-tag" title={item.teachers[0]}>
 245 |                         {item.teachers[0]}
 246 |                       </span>
 247 |                     )}
 248 |                     <span className="schedule-week-subject" title={item.fullSubject}>
 249 |                       {item.subject}
 250 |                       {mode === 'group' && item.parallel ? (
 251 |                         <span className="schedule-week-teachers-inline" title={item.teachers.join(' · ')}>
 252 |                           {' '}
 253 |                           · {item.teachers.join(' · ')}
 254 |                         </span>
 255 |                       ) : null}
 256 |                     </span>
 257 |                     <span className="schedule-week-room" title={item.rooms.join(' · ')}>
 258 |                       {item.rooms.join(' · ')}
 259 |                     </span>
 260 |                     {item.conflictWith.length > 0 ? (
 261 |                       <span className="schedule-week-conflict-with" title={item.conflictWith.join('\n')}>
 262 |                         накладка з: {item.conflictWith.join(' · ')}
 263 |                       </span>
 264 |                     ) : null}
 265 |                   </li>
 266 |                 ))}
 267 |               </ul>
 268 |             )}
 269 |           </div>
 270 |         ))}
 271 |       </div>
 272 |       {subjectSummary.length > 0 && (
 273 |         <>
 274 |           <h3 className="schedule-week-subjects-title">Предмети</h3>
 275 |           <div className="schedule-week-summary schedule-week-summary-after-grid">
 276 |             {subjectSummary.map(({ subject, fullSubject, tags }) => (
 277 |               <div key={fullSubject} className="schedule-week-chip" title={fullSubject}>
 278 |                 <span className="schedule-week-chip-name">{subject}</span>
 279 |                 <span className="schedule-week-chip-tags">
 280 |                   {tags.map(({ code, label, missing }) => (
 281 |                     <span key={code} className={missing ? 'missing-pair' : undefined}>
 282 |                       {label}
 283 |                     </span>
 284 |                   ))}
 285 |                 </span>
 286 |               </div>
 287 |             ))}
 288 |           </div>
 289 |         </>
 290 |       )}
 291 |       {missingFromNavPlan.length > 0 && (
 292 |         <div className="schedule-week-missing" role="status">
 293 |           <strong>Не вмістилось у розклад ({missingFromNavPlan.length}):</strong>
 294 |           <ul className="schedule-week-missing-list">
 295 |             {missingFromNavPlan.map(({ subject, group, missing }) => (
 296 |               <li key={`${group}|${subject}`}>
 297 |                 <span className="schedule-week-tag group-tag">{group}</span>{' '}
 298 |                 {shortSubject(subject)} — ще {missing}{' '}
 299 |                 {missing === 1 ? 'пара' : missing < 5 ? 'пари' : 'пар'}
 300 |               </li>
 301 |             ))}
 302 |           </ul>
 303 |         </div>
 304 |       )}
 305 |     </div>
 306 |   )
 307 | }
