   1 | import { useEffect, useId, useLayoutEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState } from 'react'
   2 | import { createPortal } from 'react-dom'
   3 | import { filterTextOptions } from '../utils/filterTerms'
   4 | import { filterTeacherOptions } from '../utils/teacherOptions'
   5 | 
   6 | type TeacherComboboxProps = {
   7 |   value: string
   8 |   options: string[]
   9 |   onChange: (value: string) => void
  10 |   placeholder?: string
  11 |   className?: string
  12 |   emptyHint?: string
  13 |   searchMode?: 'teacher' | 'text'
  14 | }
  15 | 
  16 | type ListPosition = {
  17 |   top: number
  18 |   left: number
  19 |   width: number
  20 |   maxHeight: number
  21 | }
  22 | 
  23 | function computeListPosition(input: HTMLInputElement): ListPosition {
  24 |   const rect = input.getBoundingClientRect()
  25 |   const gap = 4
  26 |   const padding = 8
  27 |   const minWidth = Math.max(rect.width, 320)
  28 |   const left = Math.min(Math.max(padding, rect.left), window.innerWidth - minWidth - padding)
  29 |   const desiredMax = 320
  30 |   const spaceBelow = window.innerHeight - rect.bottom - gap - padding
  31 |   const spaceAbove = rect.top - gap - padding
  32 |   const openUp = spaceBelow < 160 && spaceAbove > spaceBelow
  33 |   const maxHeight = Math.max(140, Math.min(desiredMax, openUp ? spaceAbove : spaceBelow))
  34 |   const top = openUp ? Math.max(padding, rect.top - gap - maxHeight) : rect.bottom + gap
  35 | 
  36 |   return { top, left, width: minWidth, maxHeight }
  37 | }
  38 | 
  39 | export function TeacherCombobox({
  40 |   value,
  41 |   options,
  42 |   onChange,
  43 |   placeholder,
  44 |   className,
  45 |   emptyHint = 'Завантажте навплан на сторінці «Навплан» — тоді з’явиться список викладачів',
  46 |   searchMode = 'teacher',
  47 | }: TeacherComboboxProps) {
  48 |   const [open, setOpen] = useState(false)
  49 |   const [listPosition, setListPosition] = useState<ListPosition | null>(null)
  50 |   const rootRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  51 |   const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null)
  52 |   const listRef = useRef<HTMLUListElement>(null)
  53 |   const inputId = useId()
  54 | 
  55 |   const suggestions = useMemo(() => {
  56 |     const filter = searchMode === 'text' ? filterTextOptions : filterTeacherOptions
  57 |     return filter(options, value, 40)
  58 |   }, [options, value, searchMode])
  59 |   const query = value.trim()
  60 | 
  61 |   const updateListPosition = () => {
  62 |     if (!inputRef.current) return
  63 |     setListPosition(computeListPosition(inputRef.current))
  64 |   }
  65 | 
  66 |   useLayoutEffect(() => {
  67 |     if (!open) {
  68 |       setListPosition(null)
  69 |       return
  70 |     }
  71 |     updateListPosition()
  72 |   }, [open, value, suggestions.length, options.length])
  73 | 
  74 |   useEffect(() => {
  75 |     if (!open) return
  76 | 
  77 |     const onViewportChange = () => updateListPosition()
  78 |     window.addEventListener('resize', onViewportChange)
  79 |     window.addEventListener('scroll', onViewportChange, true)
  80 |     return () => {
  81 |       window.removeEventListener('resize', onViewportChange)
  82 |       window.removeEventListener('scroll', onViewportChange, true)
  83 |     }
  84 |   }, [open, value, suggestions.length, options.length])
  85 | 
  86 |   useEffect(() => {
  87 |     if (!open) return
  88 | 
  89 |     const close = (event: MouseEvent) => {
  90 |       const target = event.target as Node
  91 |       if (rootRef.current?.contains(target)) return
  92 |       if (listRef.current?.contains(target)) return
  93 |       setOpen(false)
  94 |     }
  95 | 
  96 |     document.addEventListener('mousedown', close)
  97 |     return () => document.removeEventListener('mousedown', close)
  98 |   }, [open])
  99 | 
 100 |   const showEmptyHint = open && options.length === 0
 101 |   const showNoMatches = open && query.length > 0 && options.length > 0 && suggestions.length === 0
 102 |   const showSuggestions = open && suggestions.length > 0
 103 |   const showList = showEmptyHint || showNoMatches || showSuggestions
 104 | 
 105 |   const list = showList && listPosition ? (
 106 |     <ul
 107 |       ref={listRef}
 108 |       className="teacher-combobox-list teacher-combobox-list-portal"
 109 |       role="listbox"
 110 |       aria-labelledby={inputId}
 111 |       style={{
 112 |         top: listPosition.top,
 113 |         left: listPosition.left,
 114 |         width: listPosition.width,
 115 |         maxHeight: listPosition.maxHeight,
 116 |       }}
 117 |     >
 118 |       {showSuggestions ? (
 119 |         <li className="teacher-combobox-head">
 120 |           {query ? `Знайдено: ${suggestions.length}` : `У списку: ${suggestions.length}`}
 121 |         </li>
 122 |       ) : null}
 123 |       {showEmptyHint ? <li className="teacher-combobox-empty">{emptyHint}</li> : null}
 124 |       {showNoMatches ? <li className="teacher-combobox-empty">Немає збігів для «{query}»</li> : null}
 125 |       {suggestions.map((opt) => (
 126 |         <li key={opt}>
 127 |           <button
 128 |             type="button"
 129 |             role="option"
 130 |             aria-selected={opt === value}
 131 |             onMouseDown={(e) => e.preventDefault()}
 132 |             onClick={() => {
 133 |               onChange(opt)
 134 |               setOpen(false)
 135 |             }}
 136 |           >
 137 |             {opt}
 138 |           </button>
 139 |         </li>
 140 |       ))}
 141 |     </ul>
 142 |   ) : null
 143 | 
 144 |   return (
 145 |     <div className={`teacher-combobox ${className ?? ''}`.trim()} ref={rootRef}>
 146 |       <input
 147 |         ref={inputRef}
 148 |         id={inputId}
 149 |         type="text"
 150 |         value={value}
 151 |         placeholder={placeholder}
 152 |         autoComplete="off"
 153 |         autoCorrect="off"
 154 |         spellCheck={false}
 155 |         data-lpignore="true"
 156 |         data-form-type="other"
 157 |         onChange={(e) => {
 158 |           onChange(e.target.value)
 159 |           setOpen(true)
 160 |         }}
 161 |         onFocus={() => setOpen(true)}
 162 |         onKeyDown={(e) => {
 163 |           if (e.key === 'Escape') setOpen(false)
 164 |           if (e.key === 'ArrowDown') setOpen(true)
 165 |         }}
 166 |       />
 167 |       {list ? createPortal(list, document.body) : null}
 168 |     </div>
 169 |   )
 170 | }
 171 |

Файл: src/components/TimeSlotRing.tsx

   1 | import { useMemo } from 'react'
   2 | import { Text } from '@react-three/drei'
   3 | import type { ConflictKind, EnrichedEntry, Group, ScheduleMeta } from '../types/schedule'
   4 | import { clusterEntries, shortDisplayText } from '../utils/scheduleClusters'
   5 | import { slotAngle, slotToDayPeriod } from '../utils/slots'
   6 | 
   7 | const DAY_COLORS = ['#065f46', '#047857', '#059669', '#10b981', '#34d399']
   8 | const TEACHER_SLOT_COLOR = '#2563eb'
   9 | const TEACHER_SLOT_EMISSIVE = '#60a5fa'
  10 | 
  11 | type SlotStat = {
  12 |   slotId: number
  13 |   count: number
  14 |   worstConflict: ConflictKind
  15 | }
  16 | 
  17 | type TimeSlotRingProps = {
  18 |   meta: ScheduleMeta
  19 |   baseY: number
  20 |   cylinderRadius: number
  21 |   entries: EnrichedEntry[]
  22 |   selectedEntryId: string | null
  23 |   hoveredEntryId: string | null
  24 |   teacherProjection?: {
  25 |     teacher: string
  26 |     entries: EnrichedEntry[]
  27 |     groups: Group[]
  28 |   } | null
  29 | }
  30 | 
  31 | function buildSlotStats(entries: EnrichedEntry[], totalSlots: number): SlotStat[] {
  32 |   const stats: SlotStat[] = Array.from({ length: totalSlots }, (_, index) => ({
  33 |     slotId: index + 1,
  34 |     count: 0,
  35 |     worstConflict: 'none' as ConflictKind,
  36 |   }))
  37 | 
  38 |   for (const entry of entries) {
  39 |     const stat = stats[entry.slotId - 1]
  40 |     if (!stat) continue
  41 |     stat.count += 1
  42 |     if (entry.conflict === 'teacher') stat.worstConflict = 'teacher'
  43 |     else if (entry.conflict === 'room' && stat.worstConflict !== 'teacher') stat.worstConflict = 'room'
  44 |   }
  45 | 
  46 |   return stats
  47 | }
  48 | 
  49 | function innerSegmentStyle(stat: SlotStat, maxCount: number, active: boolean, teacherSlot: boolean) {
  50 |   if (teacherSlot) {
  51 |     return {
  52 |       color: TEACHER_SLOT_COLOR,
  53 |       emissive: TEACHER_SLOT_EMISSIVE,
  54 |       emissiveIntensity: active ? 0.85 : 0.55,
  55 |       opacity: 0.95,
  56 |     }
  57 |   }
  58 |   if (stat.worstConflict === 'teacher') {
  59 |     return { color: '#d64545', emissive: '#ff5a5f', emissiveIntensity: active ? 0.75 : 0.45, opacity: 0.95 }
  60 |   }
  61 |   if (stat.worstConflict === 'room') {
  62 |     return { color: '#d8891d', emissive: '#ffb020', emissiveIntensity: active ? 0.65 : 0.38, opacity: 0.92 }
  63 |   }
  64 |   if (stat.count > 0) {
  65 |     const load = 0.25 + (stat.count / Math.max(maxCount, 1)) * 0.55
  66 |     return { color: '#2f5f93', emissive: '#4da3ff', emissiveIntensity: active ? load + 0.2 : load, opacity: 0.85 }
  67 |   }
  68 |   return { color: '#141c29', emissive: '#1f2937', emissiveIntensity: 0.05, opacity: 0.55 }
  69 | }
  70 | 
  71 | function shortText(value: string, max = 14): string {
  72 |   return shortDisplayText(value, max)
  73 | }
  74 | 
  75 | function buildTeacherSlotClusters(
  76 |   entries: EnrichedEntry[],
  77 |   groupById: Map<string, Group>,
  78 | ): Array<{ key: string; label: string }> {
  79 |   return clusterEntries(entries).map((cluster) => {
  80 |     const groupCode = groupById.get(cluster.primary.groupId)?.code ?? '?'
  81 |     const label = cluster.parallel
  82 |       ? `${groupCode} · поділ · ${shortText(cluster.subject, 16)} · ${shortText(cluster.teachers.join(' · '), 20)}`
  83 |       : `${groupCode} · ${shortText(cluster.subject)} · ${cluster.primary.room}`
  84 |     return { key: cluster.key, label }
  85 |   })
  86 | }
  87 | 
  88 | export function TimeSlotRing({
  89 |   meta,
  90 |   baseY,
  91 |   cylinderRadius,
  92 |   entries,
  93 |   selectedEntryId,
  94 |   hoveredEntryId,
  95 |   teacherProjection,
  96 | }: TimeSlotRingProps) {
  97 |   const ringY = baseY - 0.82
  98 |   const ringInner = cylinderRadius + 0.55
  99 |   const ringOuter = cylinderRadius + 1.85
 100 |   const pulseInner = cylinderRadius + 0.12
 101 |   const pulseOuter = ringInner - 0.08
 102 |   const pulseMid = (pulseInner + pulseOuter) / 2
 103 |   const ringThickness = ringOuter - ringInner
 104 |   const ringMid = (ringInner + ringOuter) / 2
 105 |   const slotAngleStep = (Math.PI * 2) / meta.totalSlots
 106 |   const segmentArc = ringMid * slotAngleStep * 0.9
 107 |   const pulseArc = pulseMid * slotAngleStep * 0.88
 108 | 
 109 |   const slotStats = useMemo(() => buildSlotStats(entries, meta.totalSlots), [entries, meta.totalSlots])
 110 |   const maxCount = useMemo(() => Math.max(1, ...slotStats.map((stat) => stat.count)), [slotStats])
 111 | 
 112 |   const groupById = useMemo(() => {
 113 |     const map = new Map<string, Group>()
 114 |     for (const group of teacherProjection?.groups ?? []) map.set(group.id, group)
 115 |     return map
 116 |   }, [teacherProjection?.groups])
 117 | 
 118 |   const teacherEntriesBySlot = useMemo(() => {
 119 |     const map = new Map<number, EnrichedEntry[]>()
 120 |     if (!teacherProjection) return map
 121 |     for (const entry of teacherProjection.entries) {
 122 |       const bucket = map.get(entry.slotId) ?? []
 123 |       bucket.push(entry)
 124 |       map.set(entry.slotId, bucket)
 125 |     }
 126 |     return map
 127 |   }, [teacherProjection])
 128 | 
 129 |   const activeSlotId = useMemo(() => {
 130 |     if (hoveredEntryId) {
 131 |       return entries.find((entry) => entry.id === hoveredEntryId)?.slotId ?? null
 132 |     }
 133 |     if (selectedEntryId) {
 134 |       return entries.find((entry) => entry.id === selectedEntryId)?.slotId ?? null
 135 |     }
 136 |     return null
 137 |   }, [entries, hoveredEntryId, selectedEntryId])
 138 | 
 139 |   return (
 140 |     <group position={[0, ringY, 0]}>
 141 |       {Array.from({ length: meta.totalSlots }).map((_, slotIndex) => {
 142 |         const slotId = slotIndex + 1
 143 |         const midAngle = slotAngle(slotId, meta.totalSlots)
 144 |         const stat = slotStats[slotIndex]
 145 |         const teacherSlot = teacherEntriesBySlot.has(slotId)
 146 |         const active = activeSlotId === slotId
 147 |         const pulseStyle = innerSegmentStyle(stat, maxCount, active, teacherSlot)
 148 |         const px = Math.cos(midAngle) * pulseMid
 149 |         const pz = Math.sin(midAngle) * pulseMid
 150 | 
 151 |         return (
 152 |           <group key={`pulse-${slotId}`}>
 153 |             <mesh position={[px, 0.03, pz]} rotation={[0, -midAngle + Math.PI / 2, 0]}>
 154 |               <boxGeometry args={[pulseArc, 0.08, pulseOuter - pulseInner]} />
 155 |               <meshStandardMaterial
 156 |                 color={pulseStyle.color}
 157 |                 emissive={pulseStyle.emissive}
 158 |                 emissiveIntensity={pulseStyle.emissiveIntensity}
 159 |                 transparent
 160 |                 opacity={pulseStyle.opacity}
 161 |               />
 162 |             </mesh>
 163 | 
 164 |             {(stat.worstConflict !== 'none' || active || teacherSlot) && (
 165 |               <mesh
 166 |                 position={[
 167 |                   Math.cos(midAngle) * ((pulseOuter + ringInner) / 2),
 168 |                   0.05 + (active ? 0.04 : 0),
 169 |                   Math.sin(midAngle) * ((pulseOuter + ringInner) / 2),
 170 |                 ]}
 171 |                 rotation={[0, -midAngle + Math.PI / 2, 0]}
 172 |               >
 173 |                 <boxGeometry args={[0.04, 0.06 + (active ? 0.05 : 0), ringInner - pulseOuter + 0.12]} />
 174 |                 <meshStandardMaterial
 175 |                   color={active ? '#eef4ff' : pulseStyle.emissive}
 176 |                   emissive={pulseStyle.emissive}
 177 |                   emissiveIntensity={active ? 0.8 : teacherSlot ? 0.55 : 0.35}
 178 |                   transparent
 179 |                   opacity={0.85}
 180 |                 />
 181 |               </mesh>
 182 |             )}
 183 |           </group>
 184 |         )
 185 |       })}
 186 | 
 187 |       {meta.days.map((day, dayIndex) => {
 188 |         const firstSlot = dayIndex * meta.periodsPerDay + 1
 189 |         const lastSlot = firstSlot + meta.periodsPerDay - 1
 190 |         const dayMidAngle = (slotAngle(firstSlot, meta.totalSlots) + slotAngle(lastSlot, meta.totalSlots)) / 2
 191 |         const dayLabelRadius = ringOuter + 0.95
 192 | 
 193 |         return (
 194 |           <Text
 195 |             key={day}
 196 |             position={[
 197 |               Math.cos(dayMidAngle) * dayLabelRadius,
 198 |               0.18,
 199 |               Math.sin(dayMidAngle) * dayLabelRadius,
 200 |             ]}
 201 |             rotation={[0, -dayMidAngle + Math.PI / 2, 0]}
 202 |             fontSize={0.28}
 203 |             color="#f3f7ff"
 204 |             anchorX="center"
 205 |             anchorY="middle"
 206 |             outlineWidth={0.015}
 207 |             outlineColor="#0b1220"
 208 |           >
 209 |             {day}
 210 |           </Text>
 211 |         )
 212 |       })}
 213 | 
 214 |       {Array.from({ length: meta.totalSlots }).map((_, slotIndex) => {
 215 |         const slotId = slotIndex + 1
 216 |         const midAngle = slotAngle(slotId, meta.totalSlots)
 217 |         const { period, dayIndex } = slotToDayPeriod(slotId, meta)
 218 |         const x = Math.cos(midAngle) * ringMid
 219 |         const z = Math.sin(midAngle) * ringMid
 220 |         const active = activeSlotId === slotId
 221 |         const teacherEntries = teacherEntriesBySlot.get(slotId) ?? []
 222 |         const teacherSlot = teacherEntries.length > 0
 223 |         const blockHeight = active ? 0.14 : teacherSlot ? 0.12 : 0.1
 224 |         const blockY = 0.08
 225 |         const blockTop = blockY + blockHeight / 2
 226 |         const labelRadius = ringMid - 0.05
 227 |         const labelX = Math.cos(midAngle) * labelRadius
 228 |         const labelZ = Math.sin(midAngle) * labelRadius
 229 | 
 230 |         return (
 231 |           <group key={`ring-slot-${slotId}`}>
 232 |             <mesh position={[x, blockY, z]} rotation={[0, -midAngle + Math.PI / 2, 0]}>
 233 |               <boxGeometry args={[segmentArc, blockHeight, ringThickness * 0.88]} />
 234 |               <meshStandardMaterial
 235 |                 color={teacherSlot ? TEACHER_SLOT_COLOR : DAY_COLORS[dayIndex] ?? '#334155'}
 236 |                 emissive={teacherSlot ? TEACHER_SLOT_EMISSIVE : DAY_COLORS[dayIndex] ?? '#334155'}
 237 |                 emissiveIntensity={teacherSlot ? (active ? 0.55 : 0.35) : active ? 0.35 : 0.18}
 238 |               />
 239 |             </mesh>
 240 | 
 241 |             <Text
 242 |               position={[labelX, blockTop + 0.04, labelZ]}
 243 |               rotation={[0, -midAngle + Math.PI / 2, 0]}
 244 |               fontSize={0.18}
 245 |               color="#ffffff"
 246 |               anchorX="center"
 247 |               anchorY="bottom"
 248 |               renderOrder={12}
 249 |               outlineWidth={0.014}
 250 |               outlineColor="#0b1220"
 251 |               material-depthTest={false}
 252 |             >
 253 |               {String(period)}
 254 |             </Text>
 255 | 
 256 |             {teacherSlot
 257 |               ? buildTeacherSlotClusters(teacherEntries, groupById).map(({ key, label }, entryIndex) => (
 258 |                   <Text
 259 |                     key={key}
 260 |                     position={[
 261 |                       Math.cos(midAngle) * (ringOuter + 0.42 + entryIndex * 0.06),
 262 |                       0.04,
 263 |                       Math.sin(midAngle) * (ringOuter + 0.42 + entryIndex * 0.06),
 264 |                     ]}
 265 |                     rotation={[0, -midAngle + Math.PI / 2, 0]}
 266 |                     fontSize={0.1}
 267 |                     color="#dbeafe"
 268 |                     anchorX="center"
 269 |                     anchorY="top"
 270 |                     maxWidth={0.85}
 271 |                     textAlign="center"
 272 |                     renderOrder={11}
 273 |                     outlineWidth={0.01}
 274 |                     outlineColor="#0b1220"
 275 |                     material-depthTest={false}
 276 |                   >
 277 |                     {label}
 278 |                   </Text>
 279 |                 ))
 280 |               : null}
 281 |           </group>
 282 |         )
 283 |       })}
 284 |     </group>
 285 |   )
 286 | }

 108 | const PlanningContext = createContext<PlanningContextValue | null>(null)

 110 | function scheduleStats(schedule: ScheduleData) {
 111 |   const enriched = enrichEntries(schedule.entries)
 112 |   return {
 113 |     groups: schedule.groups.length,
 114 |     entries: schedule.entries.length,
 115 |     conflicts: enriched.filter((entry) => entry.conflict !== 'none').length,
 116 |   }
 117 | }

 119 | export function PlanningProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
 120 |   const [store, setStore] = useState<PlanningStore>(() => loadPlanningStore())
 121 |   const [schedule, setSchedule] = useState<ScheduleData | null>(() => loadGeneratedSchedule())
 122 |   const [scheduleEdited, setScheduleEdited] = useState(false)
 123 |   const [scheduleBuild, setScheduleBuild] = useState<ScheduleBuildState>(idleBuildState)
 124 |   const [status, setStatus] = useState<string | null>(null)
 125 |   const skipAutoSave = useRef(true)
 126 | 
 127 |   useEffect(() => {
 128 |     if (skipAutoSave.current) {
 129 |       skipAutoSave.current = false
 130 |       return
 131 |     }
 132 |     const timer = window.setTimeout(() => {
 133 |       savePlanningStore(store)
 134 |     }, 500)
 135 |     return () => window.clearTimeout(timer)
 136 |   }, [store])
 137 | 
 138 |   const persistSchedule = useCallback((next: ScheduleData, edited: boolean) => {
 139 |     setSchedule(next)
 140 |     setScheduleEdited(edited)
 141 |     saveGeneratedSchedule(next)
 142 |   }, [])
 143 | 
 144 |   const generateSpringSchedule = useCallback(async () => {
 145 |     if (scheduleBuild.running) return null
 146 | 
 147 |     setScheduleBuild({
 148 |       running: true,
 149 |       progress: 0,
 150 |       stage: 'Запуск…',
 151 |       detail: null,
 152 |       lastResult: null,
 153 |       error: null,
 154 |     })
 155 |     setStatus('Збираємо весняний розклад…')
 156 | 
 157 |     const onProgress = (p: ScheduleBuildProgress) => {
 158 |       setScheduleBuild((current) => ({
 159 |         ...current,
 160 |         running: true,
 161 |         progress: p.percent,
 162 |         stage: p.stage,
 163 |         detail: p.detail ?? null,
 164 |       }))
 165 |       setStatus(p.detail ? `${p.stage} · ${p.detail}` : p.stage)
 166 |     }
 167 | 
 168 |     try {
 169 |       const syncedStore = syncPlanningGroupsFromNavPlan(store)
 170 |       const result = await buildSpringScheduleAsync(syncedStore, onProgress)
 171 |       setStore(syncedStore)
 172 |       savePlanningStore(syncedStore)
 173 |       persistSchedule(result.schedule, false)
 174 |       setScheduleBuild({
 175 |         running: false,
 176 |         progress: 100,
 177 |         stage: 'Готово',
 178 |         detail: `${result.placed} з ${result.requested} пар`,
 179 |         lastResult: result,
 180 |         error: null,
 181 |       })
 182 |       setStatus(
 183 |         result.unplaced.length
 184 |           ? `Готово: ${result.placed} з ${result.requested} пар · ${result.unplaced.length} не вмістилось`
 185 |           : `Готово: ${result.placed} пар · ${syncedStore.groups.length} груп`,
 186 |       )
 187 |       return result
 188 |     } catch (err) {
 189 |       const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Помилка збірки розкладу'
 190 |       setScheduleBuild({
 191 |         running: false,
 192 |         progress: 0,
 193 |         stage: 'Помилка',
 194 |         detail: message,
 195 |         lastResult: null,
 196 |         error: message,
 197 |       })
 198 |       setStatus(message)
 199 |       return null
 200 |     }
 201 |   }, [store, scheduleBuild.running, persistSchedule])
 202 | 
 203 |   const updateScheduleEntry = useCallback(
 204 |     (entryId: string, patch: Partial<ScheduleEntry>) => {
 205 |       setSchedule((current) => {
 206 |         if (!current) return current
 207 |         const next: ScheduleData = {
 208 |           ...current,
 209 |           entries: current.entries.map((entry) => (entry.id === entryId ? { ...entry, ...patch } : entry)),
 210 |         }
 211 |         saveGeneratedSchedule(next)
 212 |         setScheduleEdited(true)
 213 |         return next
 214 |       })
 215 |     },
 216 |     [],
 217 |   )
 218 | 
 219 |   const saveCurrentSchedule = useCallback(async (label?: string, note?: string) => {
 220 |     if (!schedule) return null
 221 |     const resolvedLabel =
 222 |       label?.trim() ||
 223 |       window.prompt('Назва збереженого розкладу:', `Розклад ${new Date().toLocaleDateString('uk-UA')}`)?.trim() ||
 224 |       `Розклад ${new Date().toLocaleDateString('uk-UA')}`
 225 |     const resolvedNote =
 226 |       note !== undefined
 227 |         ? note.trim() || undefined
 228 |         : window.prompt('Примітка (необовʼязково):', '')?.trim() || undefined
 229 |     const doc = await saveScheduleDocument(schedule, resolvedLabel, {
 230 |       note: resolvedNote,
 231 |       edited: scheduleEdited,
 232 |       stats: scheduleStats(schedule),
 233 |     })
 234 |     setStatus(`Розклад збережено: ${doc.label}`)
 235 |     return doc
 236 |   }, [schedule, scheduleEdited])
 237 | 
 238 |   const loadScheduleVersion = useCallback(
 239 |     async (id: string) => {
 240 |       const doc = await loadScheduleDocument(id)
 241 |       if (!doc) {
 242 |         setStatus('Версію розкладу не знайдено')
 243 |         return
 244 |       }
 245 |       persistSchedule(doc.schedule, doc.edited)
 246 |       setStatus(`Завантажено розклад «${doc.label}» · ${doc.savedBy}`)
 247 |     },
 248 |     [persistSchedule],
 249 |   )
 250 | 
 251 |   const saveNavPlanVersion = useCallback(
 252 |     async (label: string, note?: string) => {
 253 |       const snapshot = await saveNavPlanSnapshot(store, label, note)
 254 |       setStatus(`Навплан збережено: v${snapshot.version} · ${snapshot.label}`)
 255 |       return snapshot
 256 |     },
 257 |     [store],
 258 |   )
 259 | 
 260 |   const restoreNavPlanVersion = useCallback(async (id: string) => {
 261 |     const snapshot = await loadNavPlanSnapshot(id)
 262 |     if (!snapshot) {
 263 |       setStatus('Версію навплану не знайдено')
 264 |       return
 265 |     }
 266 |     const next: PlanningStore = {
 267 |       ...store,
 268 |       ...snapshot.payload,
 269 |       navPlan: snapshot.payload.navPlan.map((row) => ({ ...row })),
 270 |     }
 271 |     setStore(next)
 272 |     savePlanningStore(next)
 273 |     setStatus(`Завантажено навплан v${snapshot.version} · ${snapshot.label} (${snapshot.savedBy})`)
 274 |   }, [store])
 275 | 
 276 |   const exportCurrentNavPlanJson = useCallback(
 277 |     (label?: string, note?: string) => {
 278 |       if (store.navPlan.length === 0) {
 279 |         setStatus('Немає даних навплану для експорту')
 280 |         return
 281 |       }
 282 |       const doc = buildNavPlanExport(store, { label, note })
 283 |       exportNavPlanDocumentFile(doc)
 284 |       setStatus(
 285 |         `Експорт JSON · ${doc.rowCount} рядків · ${doc.savedBy} · ${new Date(doc.savedAt).toLocaleString('uk-UA')}`,
 286 |       )
 287 |     },
 288 |     [store],
 289 |   )
 290 | 
 291 |   const importNavPlanJson = useCallback(
 292 |     async (file: File) => {
 293 |       const text = await file.text()
 294 |       let parsed: unknown
 295 |       try {
 296 |         parsed = JSON.parse(text)
 297 |       } catch {
 298 |         throw new Error('Файл не є коректним JSON')
 299 |       }
 300 |       const doc = parseNavPlanImport(parsed)
 301 |       if (doc.payload.navPlan.length === 0) throw new Error('У JSON немає рядків навплану')
 302 |       const next = applyNavPlanImport(store, doc)
 303 |       setStore(next)
 304 |       savePlanningStore(next)
 305 |       setStatus(
 306 |         `Імпорт JSON · ${doc.rowCount} рядків · «${doc.label}» · ${doc.savedBy} · ${new Date(doc.savedAt).toLocaleString('uk-UA')}`,
 307 |       )
 308 |     },
 309 |     [store],
 310 |   )
 311 | 
 312 |   const importScheduleJson = useCallback(
 313 |     async (file: File) => {
 314 |       const text = await file.text()
 315 |       let parsed: unknown
 316 |       try {
 317 |         parsed = JSON.parse(text)
 318 |       } catch {
 319 |         throw new Error('Файл не є коректним JSON')
 320 |       }
 321 |       const doc = parseScheduleImport(parsed)
 322 |       if (doc.schedule.groups.length === 0) throw new Error('У JSON немає груп')
 323 |       persistSchedule(doc.schedule, doc.edited)
 324 |       setStatus(
 325 |         `Імпорт JSON · ${doc.schedule.groups.length} груп · ${doc.schedule.entries.length} пар · «${doc.label}» · ${doc.savedBy}`,
 326 |       )
 327 |     },
 328 |     [persistSchedule],
 329 |   )
 330 | 
 331 |   const exportCurrentScheduleJson = useCallback(
 332 |     (label?: string, note?: string) => {
 333 |       if (!schedule) {
 334 |         setStatus('Немає активного розкладу для експорту')
 335 |         return
 336 |       }
 337 |       exportCurrentScheduleJsonFile(schedule, { label, note })
 338 |       setStatus(
 339 |         `Експорт JSON · ${schedule.groups.length} груп · ${schedule.entries.length} пар · ${new Date().toLocaleString('uk-UA')}`,
 340 |       )
 341 |     },
 342 |     [schedule],
 343 |   )
 344 | 
 345 |   const savePrintScheduleView = useCallback(
 346 |     async (
 347 |       kind: 'group' | 'teacher',
 348 |       targetName: string,
 349 |       title: string,
 350 |       entries: ScheduleEntry[],
 351 |       note?: string,
 352 |     ) => {
 353 |       if (!schedule) throw new Error('Немає активного розкладу')
 354 |       const doc: PrintScheduleDocument = {
 355 |         ...createPrintScheduleDocument(
 356 |           schedule,
 357 |           kind,
 358 |           targetName,
 359 |           title,
 360 |           entries,
 361 |           ensureEditorName(),
 362 |           note,
 363 |         ),
 364 |         id: newId('prt'),
 365 |       }
 366 |       await savePrintSchedule(doc)
 367 |       setStatus(`Збережено для друку: ${title}`)
 368 |       return doc
 369 |     },
 370 |     [schedule],
 371 |   )
 372 | 
 373 |   const printSavedSchedule = useCallback(async (id: string) => {
 374 |     const doc = await loadPrintSchedule(id)
 375 |     if (!doc) {
 376 |       setStatus('Друковану версію не знайдено')
 377 |       return
 378 |     }
 379 |     printScheduleDocumentHtml(doc)
 380 |     setStatus(`Друк: ${doc.title}`)
 381 |   }, [])
 382 | 
 383 |   const printScheduleView = useCallback(
 384 |     (
 385 |       kind: 'group' | 'teacher',
 386 |       targetName: string,
 387 |       title: string,
 388 |       entries: ScheduleEntry[],
 389 |       note?: string,
 390 |     ) => {
 391 |       if (!schedule) {
 392 |         setStatus('Спочатку зберіть або згенеруйте розклад')
 393 |         return
 394 |       }

 396 |         schedule,
 397 |         kind,
 398 |         targetName,
 399 |         title,
 400 |         entries,
 401 |         ensureEditorName(),
 402 |         note,
 403 |       )
 404 |       printScheduleDocumentHtml(doc)
 405 |       setStatus(`Друк: ${title}`)
 406 |     },
 407 |     [schedule],
 408 |   )
 409 | 
 410 |   const saveLocal = useCallback(() => {
 411 |     savePlanningStore(store)
 412 |     setStatus('Збережено локально')
 413 |   }, [store])
 414 | 
 415 |   const value = useMemo(
 416 |     () => ({
 417 |       store,
 418 |       setStore,
 419 |       schedule,
 420 |       scheduleEdited,
 421 |       scheduleBuild,
 422 |       generateSpringSchedule,
 423 |       updateScheduleEntry,
 424 |       saveCurrentSchedule,
 425 |       loadScheduleVersion: loadScheduleVersion,
 426 |       listScheduleVersions: listScheduleDocuments,
 427 |       deleteScheduleVersion: deleteScheduleDocument,

 433 |       importNavPlanJson,
 434 |       importScheduleJson,
 435 |       exportCurrentScheduleJson,
 436 |       savePrintScheduleView,
 437 |       listPrintScheduleViews: listPrintSchedules,
 438 |       deletePrintScheduleView: deletePrintSchedule,
 439 |       printSavedSchedule,
 440 |       printScheduleView,
 441 |       saveLocal,
 442 |       status,
 443 |       setStatus,
 444 |     }),

 447 |       schedule,
 448 |       scheduleEdited,

 461 |       printSavedSchedule,
 462 |       printScheduleView,
 463 |       saveLocal,
 464 |       status,
 465 |     ],
 466 |   )
 467 | 
 468 |   return <PlanningContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</PlanningContext.Provider>
 469 | }

Рядків: 68

   1 | import {
   2 |   createContext,
   3 |   useContext,
   4 |   useEffect,
   5 |   useMemo,
   6 |   useState,
   7 |   type ReactNode,
   8 | } from 'react'
   9 | 
  10 | export type ThemeId = 'dark' | 'light'
  11 | 
  12 | const STORAGE_KEY = 'schedule3d-theme'
  13 | 
  14 | type ThemeContextValue = {
  15 |   theme: ThemeId
  16 |   setTheme: (theme: ThemeId) => void
  17 |   toggleTheme: () => void
  18 |   sceneBackground: string
  19 | }
  20 | 
  21 | const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextValue | null>(null)
  22 | 
  23 | function readStoredTheme(): ThemeId {
  24 |   try {
  25 |     return localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY) === 'light' ? 'light' : 'dark'
  26 |   } catch {
  27 |     return 'dark'
  28 |   }
  29 | }
  30 | 
  31 | export function ThemeProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  32 |   const [theme, setThemeState] = useState<ThemeId>(() => {
  33 |     const stored = readStoredTheme()
  34 |     document.documentElement.dataset.theme = stored
  35 |     return stored
  36 |   })
  37 | 
  38 |   useEffect(() => {
  39 |     document.documentElement.dataset.theme = theme
  40 |     try {
  41 |       localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, theme)
  42 |     } catch {
  43 |       /* ignore */
  44 |     }
  45 |   }, [theme])
  46 | 
  47 |   const setTheme = (next: ThemeId) => setThemeState(next)
  48 |   const toggleTheme = () => setThemeState((t) => (t === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark'))
  49 | 
  50 |   const value = useMemo(
  51 |     () => ({
  52 |       theme,
  53 |       setTheme,
  54 |       toggleTheme,
  55 |       sceneBackground: theme === 'light' ? '#dce8d4' : '#0f1724',
  56 |     }),
  57 |     [theme],
  58 |   )
  59 | 
  60 |   return <ThemeContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</ThemeContext.Provider>
  61 | }
  62 | 
  63 | export function useTheme() {
  64 |   const ctx = useContext(ThemeContext)
  65 |   if (!ctx) throw new Error('useTheme поза ThemeProvider')
  66 |   return ctx
  67 | }
  68 |

   1 | import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react'
   2 | import demoSchedule from '../data/schedule.json'
   3 | import { DetailPanel } from '../components/DetailPanel'
   4 | import { DocumentVersionsPanel } from '../components/DocumentVersionsPanel'
   5 | import { FilterPanel, defaultScheduleFilters } from '../components/FilterPanel'
   6 | import { Legend } from '../components/Legend'
   7 | import { ScheduleScene } from '../components/ScheduleScene'
   8 | import { ScheduleWeekProjection } from '../components/ScheduleWeekProjection'
   9 | import { exportPrintScheduleJson, usePlanning } from '../context/PlanningContext'
  10 | import {
  11 |   clearCylinderFilters,
  12 |   loadCylinderFilters,
  13 |   saveCylinderFilters,
  14 | } from '../storage/cylinderFilterStorage'
  15 | import type { PrintScheduleDocument } from '../types/documents'
  16 | import type { Filters, ScheduleData, SelectedCell } from '../types/schedule'
  17 | import { enrichEntries, findConflictsForEntry } from '../utils/conflicts'
  18 | import { slotLabel } from '../utils/slots'
  19 | import {
  20 |   navPlanExpectationsForTeacher,
  21 |   summarizeExpectationsBySubject,
  22 | } from '../utils/navPlanExpectations'
  23 | import { normalizeGroupCode } from '../utils/normalize'
  24 | import {
  25 |   filterEntries,
  26 |   filterGroups,
  27 |   resolveSingleGroup,
  28 |   resolveTeachers,
  29 |   teacherMatchesFilter,
  30 | } from '../utils/scheduleFilters'
  31 | 
  32 | export function CylinderPage() {
  33 |   const {
  34 |     schedule: generatedSchedule,
  35 |     store,
  36 |     savePrintScheduleView,
  37 |     listPrintScheduleViews,
  38 |     deletePrintScheduleView,
  39 |     printSavedSchedule,
  40 |     printScheduleView,
  41 |   } = usePlanning()
  42 |   const data = (generatedSchedule ?? demoSchedule) as ScheduleData
  43 |   const isGenerated = Boolean(generatedSchedule)
  44 | 
  45 |   const [filters, setFilters] = useState<Filters>(() => loadCylinderFilters())
  46 |   const [selectedEntryId, setSelectedEntryId] = useState<string | null>(null)
  47 |   const [hoveredEntryId, setHoveredEntryId] = useState<string | null>(null)
  48 |   const [printDocs, setPrintDocs] = useState<PrintScheduleDocument[]>([])
  49 | 
  50 |   useEffect(() => {
  51 |     saveCylinderFilters(filters)
  52 |   }, [filters])
  53 | 
  54 |   const refreshPrintDocs = async () => {
  55 |     setPrintDocs(await listPrintScheduleViews())
  56 |   }
  57 | 
  58 |   useEffect(() => {
  59 |     void refreshPrintDocs()
  60 |   }, [])
  61 | 
  62 |   const enrichedEntries = useMemo(() => enrichEntries(data.entries), [data.entries])
  63 | 
  64 |   const visibleGroups = useMemo(() => filterGroups(data.groups, filters), [data.groups, filters])
  65 | 
  66 |   const visibleGroupIds = useMemo(() => new Set(visibleGroups.map((group) => group.id)), [visibleGroups])
  67 | 
  68 |   const visibleEntries = useMemo(
  69 |     () => filterEntries(enrichedEntries, data.meta, visibleGroupIds, filters),
  70 |     [data.meta, enrichedEntries, filters, visibleGroupIds],
  71 |   )
  72 | 
  73 |   const conflictCount = visibleEntries.filter((entry) => entry.conflict !== 'none').length
  74 | 
  75 |   const matchedTeachers = useMemo(
  76 |     () => resolveTeachers(filters.teacher, data.teachers),
  77 |     [data.teachers, filters.teacher],
  78 |   )
  79 | 
  80 |   const teacherProjection = useMemo(() => {
  81 |     const q = filters.teacher.trim()
  82 |     if (!q) return null
  83 |     const entries = enrichedEntries.filter((entry) => teacherMatchesFilter(entry.teacher, q))
  84 |     if (entries.length === 0) return null
  85 |     const title = matchedTeachers.length === 1 ? matchedTeachers[0]! : q
  86 |     return { teacher: title, entries }
  87 |   }, [enrichedEntries, filters.teacher, matchedTeachers])
  88 | 
  89 |   const weeksByGroup = useMemo(() => {
  90 |     const map = new Map<string, number>()
  91 |     for (const group of store.groups) map.set(normalizeGroupCode(group.code), group.weeksSpring)
  92 |     return map
  93 |   }, [store.groups])
  94 | 
  95 |   const teacherNavPlanExpectations = useMemo(() => {
  96 |     if (!filters.teacher.trim()) return undefined
  97 |     const teachers = matchedTeachers.length > 0 ? matchedTeachers : [filters.teacher.trim()]
  98 |     const rows = teachers.flatMap((teacher) =>
  99 |       navPlanExpectationsForTeacher(store.navPlan, teacher, weeksByGroup),
 100 |     )
 101 |     return summarizeExpectationsBySubject(rows)
 102 |   }, [filters.teacher, matchedTeachers, store.navPlan, weeksByGroup])
 103 | 
 104 |   const groupProjection = useMemo(() => {
 105 |     const group = resolveSingleGroup(data.groups, filters.groupCode)
 106 |     if (!group) return null
 107 |     return {
 108 |       group,
 109 |       entries: enrichedEntries.filter((entry) => entry.groupId === group.id),
 110 |     }
 111 |   }, [data.groups, enrichedEntries, filters.groupCode])
 112 | 
 113 |   const teacherProjectionForScene =
 114 |     teacherProjection === null
 115 |       ? null
 116 |       : {
 117 |           teacher: teacherProjection.teacher,
 118 |           entries: teacherProjection.entries,
 119 |           groups: data.groups,
 120 |         }
 121 | 
 122 |   const selectedCell = useMemo<SelectedCell | null>(() => {
 123 |     if (!selectedEntryId) return null
 124 |     const entry = data.entries.find((item) => item.id === selectedEntryId)
 125 |     if (!entry) return null
 126 |     const group = data.groups.find((item) => item.id === entry.groupId)
 127 |     if (!group) return null
 128 | 
 129 |     return {
 130 |       entry,
 131 |       group,
 132 |       slotLabel: slotLabel(entry.slotId, data.meta),
 133 |       conflicts: findConflictsForEntry(entry, data.entries),
 134 |     }
 135 |   }, [data.entries, data.groups, data.meta, selectedEntryId])
 136 | 
 137 |   const showSidebarHint = !teacherProjection && !groupProjection
 138 | 
 139 |   const saveCurrentPrintView = async () => {
 140 |     if (teacherProjection) {
 141 |       await savePrintScheduleView(
 142 |         'teacher',
 143 |         teacherProjection.teacher,
 144 |         teacherProjection.teacher,
 145 |         teacherProjection.entries,
 146 |       )
 147 |     } else if (groupProjection) {
 148 |       await savePrintScheduleView(
 149 |         'group',
 150 |         groupProjection.group.code,
 151 |         `Група ${groupProjection.group.code}`,
 152 |         groupProjection.entries,
 153 |       )
 154 |     }
 155 |     await refreshPrintDocs()
 156 |   }
 157 | 
 158 |   const printCurrentView = () => {
 159 |     if (teacherProjection) {
 160 |       printScheduleView(
 161 |         'teacher',
 162 |         teacherProjection.teacher,
 163 |         teacherProjection.teacher,
 164 |         teacherProjection.entries,
 165 |       )
 166 |       return
 167 |     }
 168 |     if (groupProjection) {
 169 |       printScheduleView(
 170 |         'group',
 171 |         groupProjection.group.code,
 172 |         `Група ${groupProjection.group.code}`,
 173 |         groupProjection.entries,
 174 |       )
 175 |     }
 176 |   }
 177 | 
 178 |   return (
 179 |     <div className="cylinder-layout">
 180 |       <header className="app-header cylinder-header">
 181 |         <div className="cylinder-header-top">
 182 |           <div>
 183 |             <p className="eyebrow">3D-інтерфейс</p>
 184 |             <h1>Циліндр занять</h1>
 185 |             <p className="subtitle">
 186 |               {isGenerated
 187 |                 ? `Весняний розклад · ${data.groups.length} груп · ${data.entries.length} пар`
 188 |                 : 'Демо-розклад. Зберіть весняний розклад на вкладці «Розклад».'}
 189 |             </p>
 190 |           </div>
 191 |           <Legend />
 192 |         </div>
 193 | 
 194 |         <FilterPanel
 195 |           filters={filters}
 196 |           visibleGroups={visibleGroups}
 197 |           visibleEntriesCount={visibleEntries.length}
 198 |           conflictCount={conflictCount}
 199 |           onChange={(patch) => setFilters((current) => ({ ...current, ...patch }))}
 200 |           onReset={() => {
 201 |             clearCylinderFilters()
 202 |             setFilters(defaultScheduleFilters)
 203 |           }}
 204 |         />
 205 | 
 206 |         <DetailPanel selected={selectedCell} layout="bar" groups={data.groups} />
 207 |       </header>
 208 | 
 209 |       <main className="layout cylinder-main">
 210 |         <section className="viewport cylinder-viewport">
 211 |           <ScheduleScene
 212 |             groups={visibleGroups}
 213 |             entries={visibleEntries}
 214 |             meta={data.meta}
 215 |             selectedEntryId={selectedEntryId}
 216 |             hoveredEntryId={hoveredEntryId}
 217 |             onSelect={setSelectedEntryId}
 218 |             onHover={setHoveredEntryId}
 219 |             teacherProjection={teacherProjectionForScene}
 220 |           />

 222 |         </section>

 227 |             <p className="muted cylinder-sidebar-hint">

 229 |             </p>
 230 |           ) : null}
 231 |           {teacherProjection ? (
 232 |             <ScheduleWeekProjection
 233 |               title={teacherProjection.teacher}
 234 |               entries={teacherProjection.entries}
 235 |               groups={data.groups}
 236 |               meta={data.meta}
 237 |               mode="teacher"

 239 |             />
 240 |           ) : null}
 241 |           {groupProjection ? (
 242 |             <ScheduleWeekProjection
 243 |               title={`Група ${groupProjection.group.code}`}
 244 |               entries={groupProjection.entries}
 245 |               groups={data.groups}
 246 |               meta={data.meta}
 247 |               mode="group"
 248 |             />
 249 |           ) : null}

 255 |               </button>
 256 |               <button type="button" className="btn" onClick={() => void saveCurrentPrintView()}>
 257 |                 Зберегти для друку
 258 |               </button>
 259 |             </div>
 260 |           ) : null}
 261 | 
 262 |           <DocumentVersionsPanel
 263 |             kind="print"
 264 |             items={printDocs}
 265 |             onRefresh={refreshPrintDocs}
 266 |             onDelete={deletePrintScheduleView}
 267 |             onPrint={(item) => void printSavedSchedule(item.id)}
 268 |             onExport={exportPrintScheduleJson}
 269 |           />
 270 |         </aside>
 271 |       </main>
 272 |     </div>
 273 |   )
 274 | }

   1 | import { useMemo, useState } from 'react'
   2 | import { AppLayout, SaveToolbar, type AppPage } from '../components/AppLayout'
   3 | import { DataTable } from '../components/DataTable'
   4 | import { TableTextFilters } from '../components/TableTextFilters'
   5 | import { usePlanning } from '../context/PlanningContext'
   6 | import type { GroupRow } from '../types/planning'
   7 | import { newId, normalizeGroupCode } from '../utils/normalize'
   8 | import { filterTableRows } from '../utils/tableRowFilters'
   9 | 
  10 | type PageProps = { page: AppPage; onPageChange: (page: AppPage) => void }
  11 | 
  12 | const emptyGroupFilters = { code: '', room: '', shift: '', query: '' }
  13 | 
  14 | export function GroupsPage({ page, onPageChange }: PageProps) {
  15 |   const { store, setStore, saveLocal, status } = usePlanning()
  16 |   const [filters, setFilters] = useState(emptyGroupFilters)
  17 | 
  18 |   const filteredRows = useMemo(
  19 |     () => filterTableRows(store.groups, filters, ['code', 'room', 'shift']),
  20 |     [store.groups, filters],
  21 |   )
  22 | 
  23 |   const updateRow = (id: string, key: keyof GroupRow, value: string | number) => {
  24 |     setStore((current) => ({
  25 |       ...current,
  26 |       groups: current.groups.map((row) => {
  27 |         if (row.id !== id) return row
  28 |         if (key === 'code') return { ...row, code: normalizeGroupCode(String(value)) }
  29 |         if (key === 'shift') return { ...row, shift: Number(value) === 2 ? 2 : 1 }
  30 |         return { ...row, [key]: value }
  31 |       }),
  32 |     }))
  33 |   }
  34 | 
  35 |   const deleteRow = (id: string) => {
  36 |     setStore((current) => ({
  37 |       ...current,

   1 | import { useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState } from 'react'
   2 | import { AppLayout, SaveToolbar, type AppPage } from '../components/AppLayout'
   3 | import { DocumentVersionsPanel } from '../components/DocumentVersionsPanel'
   4 | import { NavPlanFiltersPanel } from '../components/NavPlanFiltersPanel'
   5 | import { NavPlanClassifyBar } from '../components/NavPlanClassifyBar'
   6 | import { NavPlanTable, navPlanNeedsReimport } from '../components/NavPlanTable'
   7 | import { exportNavPlanSnapshotJson, usePlanning } from '../context/PlanningContext'
   8 | import type { NavPlanSnapshot } from '../types/documents'
   9 | import { reparseNavPlanFromStoredFile, saveNavPlanSourceFile } from '../storage/navPlanFileStorage'
  10 | import { savePlanningStore } from '../storage/planningStorage'
  11 | import type { NavPlanRow } from '../types/planning'
  12 | import { newId, normalizeGroupCode, normalizeSubjectKey, normalizeTeacherField } from '../utils/normalize'
  13 | import { defaultNavPlanFilters, filterNavPlanRows } from '../utils/navPlanFilters'
  14 | import { classifyNavPlanRow } from '../utils/navPlanClassify'
  15 | import { parseNavPlanFile } from '../utils/parseNavPlan'
  16 | 
  17 | type PageProps = { page: AppPage; onPageChange: (page: AppPage) => void }
  18 | 
  19 | export function NavPlanPage({ page, onPageChange }: PageProps) {
  20 |   const {
  21 |     store,
  22 |     setStore,
  23 |     saveLocal,
  24 |     status,
  25 |     setStatus,
  26 |     saveNavPlanVersion,
  27 |     restoreNavPlanVersion,
  28 |     listNavPlanVersions,
  29 |     deleteNavPlanVersion,
  30 |     exportCurrentNavPlanJson,
  31 |     importNavPlanJson,
  32 |   } = usePlanning()
  33 |   const [filters, setFilters] = useState(defaultNavPlanFilters)
  34 |   const [importError, setImportError] = useState<string | null>(null)
  35 |   const [navSnapshots, setNavSnapshots] = useState<NavPlanSnapshot[]>([])
  36 |   const fileRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null)
  37 | 
  38 |   const refreshSnapshots = async () => {
  39 |     setNavSnapshots(await listNavPlanVersions())
  40 |   }
  41 | 
  42 |   const filteredRows = useMemo(
  43 |     () => filterNavPlanRows(store.navPlan, filters),
  44 |     [store.navPlan, filters],
  45 |   )
  46 | 
  47 |   const groupOptions = useMemo(() => {
  48 |     const codes = [...new Set(store.navPlan.map((r) => r.groupCode))].sort()
  49 |     return codes
  50 |   }, [store.navPlan])
  51 | 
  52 |   const needsReimport =
  53 |     store.navPlan.length > 0 &&
  54 |     (store.navPlanColumnsVersion !== 2 || navPlanNeedsReimport(store.navPlan))
  55 | 
  56 |   const applyImportedRows = (rows: NavPlanRow[], source: string) => {
  57 |     setStore((current) => {
  58 |       const next = {
  59 |         ...current,
  60 |         navPlan: rows,
  61 |         navPlanSource: source,
  62 |         navPlanColumnsVersion: 2,
  63 |       }
  64 |       savePlanningStore(next)
  65 |       return next
  66 |     })
  67 |   }
  68 | 
  69 |   useEffect(() => {
  70 |     if (!needsReimport) return
  71 |     let cancelled = false
  72 |     reparseNavPlanFromStoredFile().then((parsed) => {
  73 |       if (cancelled || !parsed?.rows.length) return
  74 |       applyImportedRows(parsed.rows, parsed.source)
  75 |       setStatus(`Години оновлено з ${parsed.source}`)
  76 |     })
  77 |     return () => {
  78 |       cancelled = true
  79 |     }
  80 |   }, [])
  81 | 
  82 |   const refreshFromStoredExcel = async () => {
  83 |     setImportError(null)
  84 |     const parsed = await reparseNavPlanFromStoredFile()
  85 |     if (!parsed?.rows.length) {
  86 |       fileRef.current?.click()
  87 |       return
  88 |     }
  89 |     applyImportedRows(parsed.rows, parsed.source)
  90 |     setStatus(`Оновлено ${parsed.rows.length} рядків · ${parsed.source}`)
  91 |   }
  92 | 
  93 |   const updateRow = (id: string, key: keyof NavPlanRow, value: string | number) => {
  94 |     setStore((current) => ({
  95 |       ...current,
  96 |       navPlan: current.navPlan.map((row) => {
  97 |         if (row.id !== id) return row
  98 |         const next = { ...row, [key]: value }
  99 |         if (key === 'subject') {
 100 |           next.subjectNorm = normalizeSubjectKey(String(value))
 101 |           const classified = classifyNavPlanRow(next)
 102 |           next.planKind = classified.kind
 103 |           next.planKindLabel = classified.label
 104 |         }
 105 |         if (key === 'teacher') next.teacher = normalizeTeacherField(String(value))
 106 |         if (key === 'groupCode') next.groupCode = normalizeGroupCode(String(value))
 107 |         return next
 108 |       }),
 109 |     }))
 110 |   }
 111 | 
 112 |   const deleteRow = (id: string) => {
 113 |     setStore((current) => ({
 114 |       ...current,
 115 |       navPlan: current.navPlan.filter((row) => row.id !== id),
 116 |     }))
 117 |   }
 118 | 
 119 |   const addRow = () => {
 120 |     setStore((current) => ({
 121 |       ...current,
 122 |       navPlan: [
 123 |         ...current.navPlan,
 124 |         {
 125 |           id: newId('np'),
 126 |           subject: '',
 127 |           subjectNorm: '',
 128 |           teacher: '',
 129 |           hoursTotal: 0,
 130 |           hoursCourse: 0,
 131 |           hoursSelf: 0,
 132 |           fallLectures: 0,
 133 |           fallPractical: 0,
 134 |           fallLab: 0,
 135 |           fallCoursework: 0,
 136 |           fallConsult: 0,
 137 |           fallCredits: 0,
 138 |           fallExams: 0,
 139 |           hoursFall: 0,
 140 |           springLectures: 0,
 141 |           springPractical: 0,
 142 |           springLab: 0,
 143 |           springCoursework: 0,
 144 |           springConsult: 0,
 145 |           springSupervised: 0,
 146 |           springCredits: 0,
 147 |           springExams: 0,
 148 |           springDpa: 0,
 149 |           springDkk: 0,
 150 |           hoursSpring: 0,
 151 |           groupCode: groupOptions[0] ?? '',
 152 |           budget: 0,
 153 |           extraBudget: 0,
 154 |           planKind: 'schedule',
 155 |           planKindLabel: 'У тижневий розклад',
 156 |         },
 157 |       ],
 158 |     }))
 159 |   }
 160 | 
 161 |   const onFile = async (file: File | undefined) => {
 162 |     if (!file) return
 163 |     setImportError(null)
 164 |     try {
 165 |       const rows = await parseNavPlanFile(file)
 166 |       if (rows.length === 0) throw new Error('Не знайдено рядків навплану')
 167 |       await saveNavPlanSourceFile(file)
 168 |       applyImportedRows(rows, file.name)
 169 |       setStatus(`Завантажено ${rows.length} рядків · збережено локально`)
 170 |     } catch (err) {
 171 |       setImportError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Помилка імпорту')
 172 |     } finally {
 173 |       if (fileRef.current) fileRef.current.value = ''
 174 |     }
 175 |   }
 176 | 
 177 |   const toolbar = (
 178 |     <SaveToolbar
 179 |       onSaveLocal={saveLocal}
 180 |       extra={
 181 |         <>
 182 |           <input
 183 |             ref={fileRef}
 184 |             type="file"
 185 |             accept=".xlsx,.xls"
 186 |             hidden
 187 |             onChange={(e) => onFile(e.target.files?.[0])}
 188 |           />
 189 |           <button type="button" className="btn" onClick={() => fileRef.current?.click()}>
 190 |             Завантажити Excel
 191 |           </button>
 192 |           {store.navPlan.length > 0 ? (
 193 |             <button type="button" className="btn" onClick={refreshFromStoredExcel}>
 194 |               Оновити години
 195 |             </button>
 196 |           ) : null}
 197 |           <button type="button" className="btn" onClick={addRow}>
 198 |             + Рядок
 199 |           </button>
 200 |         </>
 201 |       }
 202 |     />
 203 |   )
 204 | 
 205 |   return (
 206 |     <AppLayout
 207 |       page={page}
 208 |       onPageChange={onPageChange}
 209 |       title="Навчальний план"
 210 |       subtitle={
 211 |         store.navPlanSource
 212 |           ? `Джерело: ${store.navPlanSource}. Показано ${filteredRows.length} з ${store.navPlan.length}. За замовчуванням — лише пари для розкладу; КР/КП/практики — у «Виключені».`
 213 |           : 'Завантажте Excel. Рядки автоматично класифікуються: пари, КР, КП, практики…'
 214 |       }
 215 |       toolbar={toolbar}
 216 |       status={status}
 217 |     >
 218 |       {importError ? <p className="error-banner">{importError}</p> : null}
 219 |       {needsReimport ? (
 220 |         <p className="warn-banner">
 221 |           У таблиці лише старі дані (без лекцій, практичних, заліків). Натисніть{' '}
 222 |           <strong>Оновити години</strong> або завантажте Excel знову — тоді з’являться всі колонки
 223 |           годин, як у файлі.
 224 |         </p>
 225 |       ) : null}
 226 | 
 227 |       <DocumentVersionsPanel
 228 |         kind="navPlan"
 229 |         items={navSnapshots}
 230 |         onRefresh={refreshSnapshots}
 231 |         canExportCurrent={store.navPlan.length > 0}
 232 |         onSave={async (label, note) => {
 233 |           await saveNavPlanVersion(label, note)
 234 |         }}
 235 |         onRestore={restoreNavPlanVersion}
 236 |         onDelete={deleteNavPlanVersion}
 237 |         onExport={exportNavPlanSnapshotJson}
 238 |         onExportCurrent={(label, note) => exportCurrentNavPlanJson(label, note)}
 239 |         onImport={async (file) => {
 240 |           setImportError(null)
 241 |           try {
 242 |             await importNavPlanJson(file)
 243 |             await refreshSnapshots()
 244 |           } catch (err) {
 245 |             setImportError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Помилка імпорту JSON')
 246 |           }
 247 |         }}
 248 |       />
 249 | 
 250 |       {store.navPlan.length > 0 ? (
 251 |         <>
 252 |           <NavPlanClassifyBar
 253 |             rows={store.navPlan}
 254 |             active={filters.planKind}
 255 |             onSelect={(planKind) => setFilters((current) => ({ ...current, planKind }))}
 256 |           />
 257 |           <NavPlanFiltersPanel filters={filters} onChange={setFilters} />
 258 |         </>
 259 |       ) : null}
 260 |       <NavPlanTable
 261 |         rows={filteredRows}
 262 |         onChange={updateRow}
 263 |         onDelete={deleteRow}
 264 |         emptyText="Завантажте навплан з Excel (.xlsx)"
 265 |       />
 266 |     </AppLayout>
 267 |   )
 268 | }

 117 |       {!schedule && !scheduleBuild.running ? (
 118 |         <p className="muted table-empty">
 119 |           Розклад ще не зібрано. Завантажте навплан і натисніть «Зібрати весняний розклад».
 120 |         </p>
 121 |       ) : null}
 122 | 
 123 |       {schedule && !scheduleBuild.running ? (
 124 |         <section className="panel section-block">
 125 |           <h2>Результат</h2>
 126 |           <p>
 127 |             Груп: <strong>{preview?.groups}</strong> · Пар на тиждень:{' '}
 128 |             <strong>{preview?.entries}</strong> · Конфліктів:{' '}
 129 |             <strong className={preview?.conflicts ? 'warn-text' : ''}>{preview?.conflicts ?? 0}</strong>
 130 |             {scheduleEdited ? (
 131 |               <>
 132 |                 {' '}
 133 |                 · <span className="warn-text">є незбережені правки</span>
 134 |               </>
 135 |             ) : null}
 136 |           </p>
 137 |           <p className="muted">
 138 |             Джерело: {schedule.meta.sourceFile} ·{' '}
 139 |             {new Date(schedule.meta.generatedAt).toLocaleString('uk-UA')}
 140 |           </p>
 141 |         </section>
 142 |       ) : null}
 143 | 
 144 |       {schedule && !scheduleBuild.running ? (
 145 |         <BatchExportPanel schedule={schedule} onStatus={setStatus} />
 146 |       ) : null}
 147 | 
 148 |       <DocumentVersionsPanel
 149 |         kind="schedule"
 150 |         items={scheduleDocs}
 151 |         onRefresh={refreshScheduleDocs}
 152 |         onSave={async (label, note) => {
 153 |           await saveCurrentSchedule(label, note)
 154 |         }}
 155 |         onLoad={loadScheduleVersion}
 156 |         onDelete={deleteScheduleVersion}
 157 |         onExport={exportScheduleDocumentJson}
 158 |         onImport={async (file) => {
 159 |           try {
 160 |             await importScheduleJson(file)
 161 |           } catch (err) {
 162 |             setStatus(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Помилка імпорту')
 163 |           }
 164 |         }}
 165 |         onExportCurrent={exportCurrentScheduleJson}
 166 |         canExportCurrent={Boolean(schedule)}
 167 |       />
 168 | 
 169 |       {store.navPlan.length === 0 ? (
 170 |         <p className="warn-banner">Спочатку завантажте навчальний план на вкладці «Навплан».</p>
 171 |       ) : null}
 172 |     </AppLayout>
 173 |   )
 174 | }
