  77 | function findTeacherPref(prefs: TeacherPrefRow[], teacher: string): string | undefined {
  78 |   return prefs.find((p) => p.teacher === teacher)?.rule
  79 | }
  80 | 
  81 | function findSubjectPref(
  82 |   prefs: SubjectPrefRow[],
  83 |   groupCode: string,
  84 |   subject: string,
  85 | ): string | undefined {
  86 |   const code = normalizeGroupCode(groupCode)
  87 |   const subjKey = normalizeSubjectKey(subject)
  88 |   return prefs.find(
  89 |     (p) =>
  90 |       normalizeGroupCode(p.groupCode) === code &&
  91 |       normalizeSubjectKey(p.subject) === subjKey,
  92 |   )?.rule
  93 | }
  94 | 
  95 | function resolveRoom(
  96 |   row: NavPlanRow,
  97 |   groupRow: GroupRow,
  98 |   remote: boolean,
  99 |   roomRules: RoomRuleRow[],
 100 | ): string {
 101 |   if (remote) return 'Дист'
 102 |   const subjKey = normalizeSubjectKey(row.subject)
 103 |   const rule = roomRules.find((r) => {
 104 |     const subjMatch =
 105 |       normalizeSubjectKey(r.subject) === subjKey ||
 106 |       row.subject.toLowerCase().includes(r.subject.toLowerCase())
 107 |     if (!subjMatch) return false
 108 |     if (!r.teacher) return true
 109 |     return row.teacher === r.teacher
 110 |   })
 111 |   if (rule) {
 112 |     if (rule.room === 'своя') return groupRow.room.startsWith('~') ? placeholderRoom(groupRow.code) : groupRow.room
 113 |     return rule.room
 114 |   }
 115 |   return groupRow.room
 116 | }
 117 | 
 118 | function buildDemands(store: PlanningStore, groupsMap: Map<string, GroupRow>): {
 119 |   demands: LessonDemand[]
 120 |   duplicateKeys: string[]
 121 | } {
 122 |   const buckets = new Map<
 123 |     string,
 124 |     { row: NavPlanRow; contact: number; groupRow: GroupRow; duplicate: boolean; teacher: string }
 125 |   >()
 126 | 
 127 |   for (const row of store.navPlan) {
 128 |     if (!row.groupCode || !row.subject) continue
 129 |     if (row.planKind !== 'schedule') continue
 130 |     const groupRow = ensureGroupRow(row.groupCode, groupsMap)
 131 |     const contact = springContactHours(row)
 132 |     if (contact <= 0) continue
 133 |     if (!row.teacher) continue
 134 | 
 135 |     const teacher = normalizeTeacherField(row.teacher)
 136 |     if (!teacher) continue
 137 | 
 138 |     const key = `${normalizeGroupCode(row.groupCode)}|${row.subject}|${teacher}`
 139 |     const existing = buckets.get(key)
 140 |     if (existing) {
 141 |       existing.duplicate = true
 142 |       existing.contact = Math.max(existing.contact, contact)
 143 |     } else {
 144 |       buckets.set(key, { row, contact, groupRow, duplicate: false, teacher })
 145 |     }
 146 |   }
 147 | 
 148 |   const demands: LessonDemand[] = []
 149 |   const duplicateKeys: string[] = []
 150 | 
 151 |   for (const [key, bucket] of buckets) {
 152 |     if (bucket.duplicate) duplicateKeys.push(key)
 153 |     const { row, contact, groupRow, teacher } = bucket
 154 |     const parsed = parseGroupCode(row.groupCode)
 155 |     const shift = effectiveShift(parsed.course, groupRow.shift)
 156 |     const remote = isRemoteGroup(row.groupCode, parsed.course)
 157 |     const weekly = pairsPerWeek(contact, groupRow.weeksSpring)
 158 |     if (weekly <= 0) continue
 159 | 
 160 |     demands.push({
 161 |       key,
 162 |       navRowId: row.id,
 163 |       groupCode: normalizeGroupCode(row.groupCode),
 164 |       groupId: groupRow.id,
 165 |       subject: row.subject,
 166 |       teacher,
 167 |       pairsPerWeek: weekly,
 168 |       shift,
 169 |       remote,
 170 |       room: resolveRoom(row, groupRow, remote, store.roomRules),
 171 |       isPE: isPhysicalEducation(row.subject),
 172 |       teacherPref: findTeacherPref(store.teacherPrefs, teacher),
 173 |       subjectPref: findSubjectPref(store.subjectPrefs, row.groupCode, row.subject),
 174 |     })
 175 |   }
 176 | 
 177 |   return {
 178 |     demands: demands.sort((a, b) => {
 179 |       if (a.isPE !== b.isPE) return a.isPE ? 1 : -1
 180 |       return b.pairsPerWeek - a.pairsPerWeek
 181 |     }),
 182 |     duplicateKeys,
 183 |   }
 184 | }
 185 | 
 186 | function createOccupancy(): Occupancy {
 187 |   return {
 188 |     teacher: new Map(),
 189 |     room: new Map(),
 190 |     group: new Map(),
 191 |     subjectDay: new Map(),
 192 |     subjectDays: new Map(),
 193 |   }
 194 | }
 195 | 
 196 | function occupy(setMap: Map<string, Set<number>>, key: string, slotId: number) {
 197 |   if (!setMap.has(key)) setMap.set(key, new Set())
 198 |   setMap.get(key)!.add(slotId)
 199 | }
 200 | 
 201 | function isOccupied(setMap: Map<string, Set<number>>, key: string, slotId: number): boolean {
 202 |   return setMap.get(key)?.has(slotId) ?? false
 203 | }
 204 | 
 205 | function teacherSlotsOnDay(
 206 |   occ: Occupancy,
 207 |   teacher: string,
 208 |   dayIndex: number,
 209 |   meta: { days: string[]; periodsPerDay: number; totalSlots: number; sourceFile: string; generatedAt: string; note: string },
 210 | ): number {
 211 |   const slots = occ.teacher.get(teacher)
 212 |   if (!slots) return 0
 213 |   let count = 0
 214 |   for (const slotId of slots) {
 215 |     if (slotContext(slotId, meta).dayIndex === dayIndex) count += 1
 216 |   }
 217 |   return count
 218 | }
 219 | 
 220 | function teacherActiveDayCount(
 221 |   occ: Occupancy,
 222 |   teacher: string,
 223 |   meta: { days: string[]; periodsPerDay: number; totalSlots: number; sourceFile: string; generatedAt: string; note: string },
 224 | ): number {
 225 |   const slots = occ.teacher.get(teacher)
 226 |   if (!slots) return 0
 227 |   const days = new Set<number>()
 228 |   for (const slotId of slots) {
 229 |     days.add(slotContext(slotId, meta).dayIndex)
 230 |   }
 231 |   return days.size
 232 | }
 233 | 
 234 | function teacherMaxDailyLoad(
 235 |   occ: Occupancy,
 236 |   teacher: string,
 237 |   meta: { days: string[]; periodsPerDay: number; totalSlots: number; sourceFile: string; generatedAt: string; note: string },
 238 | ): number {
 239 |   let max = 0
 240 |   for (let dayIndex = 0; dayIndex < meta.days.length; dayIndex += 1) {
 241 |     max = Math.max(max, teacherSlotsOnDay(occ, teacher, dayIndex, meta))
 242 |   }
 243 |   return max
 244 | }
 245 | 
 246 | function scoreSlot(
 247 |   demand: LessonDemand,
 248 |   ctx: ReturnType<typeof slotContext>,
 249 |   occ: Occupancy,
 250 |   options?: { skipGroupCheck?: boolean; relaxSpacing?: boolean; ignoreRoom?: boolean },
 251 | ): number | null {
 252 |   if (!teacherAllowsSlot(demand.teacherPref, ctx)) return null
 253 |   if (!subjectAllowsDay(demand.subjectPref, ctx.dayIndex)) return null
 254 | 
 255 |   const dayKey = demand.subjectDayKey ?? demand.key
 256 |   const dayCount = occ.subjectDay.get(dayKey)?.get(ctx.dayIndex) ?? 0
 257 |   const dayLimit = subjectDayLimit(demand.subjectPref)
 258 |   if (dayCount >= dayLimit) return null
 259 | 
 260 |   if (!options?.relaxSpacing && demand.subjectPref?.includes('min_1_день_між')) {
 261 |     const usedDays = occ.subjectDays.get(dayKey) ?? new Set()
 262 |     for (const d of usedDays) {
 263 |       if (Math.abs(d - ctx.dayIndex) <= 1) return null
 264 |     }
 265 |   }
 266 | 
 267 |   if (isOccupied(occ.teacher, demand.teacher, ctx.slotId)) return null
 268 |   if (!options?.skipGroupCheck && isOccupied(occ.group, demand.groupId, ctx.slotId)) return null
 269 |   if (!options?.ignoreRoom && !demand.remote && isOccupied(occ.room, demand.room, ctx.slotId)) return null
 270 | 
 271 |   const meta = { ...META, sourceFile: '', generatedAt: '', note: '' }
 272 |   const teacherDayLoad = teacherSlotsOnDay(occ, demand.teacher, ctx.dayIndex, meta)
 273 |   const teacherLoadScore = scoreTeacherDailyLoad(teacherDayLoad, demand.teacherPref)
 274 |   if (teacherLoadScore === null) return null
 275 | 
 276 |   let score = dayCount * 100
 277 |   score += ctx.period
 278 |   score += teacherLoadScore
 279 | 
 280 |   const teacherActiveDays = teacherActiveDayCount(occ, demand.teacher, meta)
 281 |   if (teacherDayLoad === 0 && teacherActiveDays > 0) {
 282 |     score += 90 + teacherActiveDays * 20
 283 |   }
 284 | 
 285 |   const busiestDayLoad = teacherMaxDailyLoad(occ, demand.teacher, meta)
 286 |   if (teacherDayLoad > 0 && teacherDayLoad === busiestDayLoad && busiestDayLoad >= 2) {
 287 |     score -= 40
 288 |   }
 289 | 
 290 |   if (demand.isPE) {
 291 |     score += pePeriodScore(ctx, demand.shift) * 40
 292 |   } else {
 293 |     score += dayCount * 50
 294 |   }
 295 | 
 296 |   const usedDays = occ.subjectDays.get(dayKey)?.size ?? 0
 297 |   if (usedDays > 0 && !occ.subjectDays.get(dayKey)?.has(ctx.dayIndex)) {
 298 |     if (teacherDayLoad === 0) score -= 10
 299 |     else score += 25
 300 |   }
 301 | 
 302 |   return score
 303 | }
 304 | 
 305 | function scoreParallelSlot(demands: LessonDemand[], ctx: ReturnType<typeof slotContext>, occ: Occupancy): number | null {
 306 |   if (demands.length === 0) return null
 307 |   if (isOccupied(occ.group, demands[0].groupId, ctx.slotId)) return null
 308 | 
 309 |   let totalScore = 0
 310 |   for (const demand of demands) {
 311 |     const score = scoreSlot(demand, ctx, occ, { skipGroupCheck: true })
 312 |     if (score === null) return null
 313 |     totalScore += score
 314 |   }
 315 | 
 316 |   return totalScore / demands.length
 317 | }
 318 | 
 319 | function pickSlot(
 320 |   demand: LessonDemand,
 321 |   occ: Occupancy,
 322 |   options?: { relaxSpacing?: boolean; ignoreRoom?: boolean },
 323 | ): number | null {
 324 |   const meta = { ...META, sourceFile: '', generatedAt: '', note: '' }
 325 |   const candidates = allowedSlotIds(meta, demand.shift)
 326 |   let best: { slotId: number; score: number } | null = null
 327 | 
 328 |   for (const slotId of candidates) {
 329 |     const ctx = slotContext(slotId, meta)
 330 |     const score = scoreSlot(demand, ctx, occ, options)
 331 |     if (score === null) continue
 332 |     if (!best || score < best.score) best = { slotId, score }
 333 |   }
 334 | 
 335 |   return best?.slotId ?? null
 336 | }
 337 | 
 338 | function pickParallelSlot(demands: LessonDemand[], occ: Occupancy): number | null {
 339 |   const meta = { ...META, sourceFile: '', generatedAt: '', note: '' }
 340 |   const candidates = allowedSlotIds(meta, demands[0].shift)
 341 |   let best: { slotId: number; score: number } | null = null
 342 | 
 343 |   for (const slotId of candidates) {
 344 |     const ctx = slotContext(slotId, meta)
 345 |     const score = scoreParallelSlot(demands, ctx, occ)
 346 |     if (score === null) continue
 347 |     if (!best || score < best.score) best = { slotId, score }
 348 |   }
 349 | 
 350 |   return best?.slotId ?? null
 351 | }
 352 | 
 353 | function placeEntry(
 354 |   demand: LessonDemand,
 355 |   slotId: number,
 356 |   occ: Occupancy,
 357 |   entries: ScheduleEntry[],
 358 |   options?: { skipGroupOccupy?: boolean; skipRoomOccupy?: boolean },
 359 | ) {
 360 |   const entry: ScheduleEntry = {
 361 |     id: newId('e'),
 362 |     groupId: demand.groupId,
 363 |     slotId,
 364 |     subject: demand.subject,
 365 |     teacher: demand.teacher,
 366 |     room: demand.room,
 367 |     parallelBundleId: demand.parallelBundleId,
 368 |   }
 369 |   entries.push(entry)
 370 |   occupy(occ.teacher, demand.teacher, slotId)
 371 |   if (!options?.skipGroupOccupy) occupy(occ.group, demand.groupId, slotId)
 372 |   if (!demand.remote && !options?.skipRoomOccupy) occupy(occ.room, demand.room, slotId)
 373 | 
 374 |   const dayKey = demand.subjectDayKey ?? demand.key
 375 |   if (!occ.subjectDay.has(dayKey)) occ.subjectDay.set(dayKey, new Map())
 376 |   const dayMap = occ.subjectDay.get(dayKey)!
 377 |   const { dayIndex } = slotContext(slotId, { ...META, sourceFile: '', generatedAt: '', note: '' })
 378 |   dayMap.set(dayIndex, (dayMap.get(dayIndex) ?? 0) + 1)
 379 | 
 380 |   if (!occ.subjectDays.has(dayKey)) occ.subjectDays.set(dayKey, new Set())
 381 |   occ.subjectDays.get(dayKey)!.add(dayIndex)
 382 | }
 383 | 
 384 | function placeParallelBundle(
 385 |   demands: LessonDemand[],
 386 |   slotId: number,
 387 |   occ: Occupancy,
 388 |   entries: ScheduleEntry[],
 389 | ) {
 390 |   demands.forEach((demand, index) => {
 391 |     placeEntry(demand, slotId, occ, entries, { skipGroupOccupy: index > 0 })
 392 |   })
 393 | }
 394 | 
 395 | function unitPairsPerWeek(unit: ReturnType<typeof buildScheduleUnits<LessonDemand>>[number]): number {
 396 |   return unit.type === 'single' ? unit.demand.pairsPerWeek : unit.demands[0]?.pairsPerWeek ?? 0
 397 | }
 398 | 
 399 | type ScheduleUnit = ReturnType<typeof buildScheduleUnits<LessonDemand>>[number]
 400 | 
 401 | function unitGroupCode(unit: ScheduleUnit): string {
 402 |   return unit.type === 'single' ? unit.demand.groupCode : unit.demands[0]?.groupCode ?? ''
 403 | }
 404 | 
 405 | function unitTeacherKey(unit: ScheduleUnit): string {
 406 |   return unit.type === 'single'
 407 |     ? unit.demand.teacher
 408 |     : unit.demands.map((d) => d.teacher).sort().join('|')
 409 | }
 410 | 
 411 | /** Чергує предмети в межах групи (алгоритми ↔ технології), а не всі пари одного предмета підряд. */
 412 | function interleaveUnitsByGroup(units: ScheduleUnit[]): ScheduleUnit[] {
 413 |   const byGroup = new Map<string, ScheduleUnit[]>()
 414 |   for (const unit of units) {
 415 |     const group = unitGroupCode(unit)
 416 |     const list = byGroup.get(group) ?? []
 417 |     list.push(unit)
 418 |     byGroup.set(group, list)
 419 |   }
 420 | 
 421 |   for (const list of byGroup.values()) {
 422 |     list.sort((a, b) => {
 423 |       const subjA =
 424 |         a.type === 'single' ? a.demand.subject : a.demands.map((d) => d.subject).join('|')
 425 |       const subjB =
 426 |         b.type === 'single' ? b.demand.subject : b.demands.map((d) => d.subject).join('|')
 427 |       return subjA.localeCompare(subjB, 'uk') || unitSortWeight(b) - unitSortWeight(a)
 428 |     })
 429 |   }
 430 | 
 431 |   const groups = [...byGroup.keys()].sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, 'uk'))
 432 |   const maxDepth = Math.max(...[...byGroup.values()].map((list) => list.length), 0)
 433 |   const result: ScheduleUnit[] = []
 434 |   for (let depth = 0; depth < maxDepth; depth += 1) {
 435 |     for (const group of groups) {
 436 |       const unit = byGroup.get(group)?.[depth]
 437 |       if (unit) result.push(unit)
 438 |     }
 439 |   }
 440 |   return result
 441 | }
 442 | 
 443 | /** Черга розміщення: по одній парі, чергуючи викладачів, групи та предмети. */
 444 | function buildFairPairQueue(units: ScheduleUnit[]): ScheduleUnit[] {
 445 |   const byTeacher = new Map<string, ScheduleUnit[]>()
 446 |   for (const unit of units) {
 447 |     const key = unitTeacherKey(unit)
 448 |     const list = byTeacher.get(key) ?? []
 449 |     list.push(unit)
 450 |     byTeacher.set(key, list)
 451 |   }
 452 | 
 453 |   const maxPairs = Math.max(...units.map((u) => unitPairsPerWeek(u)), 0)
 454 |   const queue: ScheduleUnit[] = []
 455 | 
 456 |   for (let pairIdx = 0; pairIdx < maxPairs; pairIdx += 1) {
 457 |     for (const teacherUnits of byTeacher.values()) {
 458 |       for (const unit of interleaveUnitsByGroup(teacherUnits)) {
 459 |         if (pairIdx < unitPairsPerWeek(unit)) queue.push(unit)
 460 |       }
 461 |     }
 462 |   }
 463 | 
 464 |   return queue
 465 | }
 466 | 
 467 | function unitSortWeight(unit: ReturnType<typeof buildScheduleUnits<LessonDemand>>[number]): number {
 468 |   if (unit.type === 'single') {
 469 |     return unit.demand.isPE ? -1 : unit.demand.pairsPerWeek
 470 |   }
 471 |   const isPE = unit.demands.some((d) => d.isPE)
 472 |   return isPE ? -1 : unitPairsPerWeek(unit)
 473 | }
 474 | 
 475 | function buildScheduleGroups(
 476 |   demands: LessonDemand[],
 477 |   groupsMap: Map<string, GroupRow>,
 478 | ): Group[] {
 479 |   const ids = new Set(demands.map((d) => d.groupId))
 480 |   const groups: Group[] = []
 481 |   for (const row of groupsMap.values()) {
 482 |     if (!ids.has(row.id)) continue
 483 |     const parsed = parseGroupCode(row.code)
 484 |     groups.push({
 485 |       id: row.id,
 486 |       code: row.code,
 487 |       name: `Група ${row.code}`,
 488 |       specialty: parsed.specialty,
 489 |       course: parsed.course,
 490 |       room: row.room,
 491 |     })
 492 |   }
 493 |   return groups.sort((a, b) => a.code.localeCompare(b.code, 'uk'))
 494 | }
 495 | 
 496 | function buildLookups(entries: ScheduleEntry[]): { teachers: Teacher[]; rooms: Room[] } {
 497 |   const teacherNames = [...new Set(entries.map((e) => e.teacher).filter(Boolean))]
 498 |   const roomCodes = [...new Set(entries.map((e) => e.room).filter(Boolean))]
 499 |   return {
 500 |     teachers: teacherNames.map((name, i) => ({ id: `t${i + 1}`, name })),
 501 |     rooms: roomCodes.map((code, i) => ({ id: `r${i + 1}`, code })),
 502 |   }
 503 | }
 504 | 
 505 | async function reportProgress(
 506 |   onProgress: ((p: ScheduleBuildProgress) => void) | undefined,
 507 |   stage: string,
 508 |   percent: number,
 509 |   detail?: string,
 510 | ) {
 511 |   onProgress?.({ stage, percent, detail })
 512 |   await yieldUi()
 513 | }
 514 | 
 515 | function buildSpringScheduleResult(
 516 |   store: PlanningStore,
 517 |   groupsMap: Map<string, GroupRow>,
 518 |   demands: LessonDemand[],
 519 |   warnings: string[],
 520 |   entries: ScheduleEntry[],
 521 |   unplaced: LessonDemand[],
 522 |   placed: number,
 523 |   requested: number,
 524 | ): SpringScheduleResult {
 525 |   const { teachers, rooms } = buildLookups(entries)
 526 |   const schedule: ScheduleData = {
 527 |     meta: {
 528 |       sourceFile: store.navPlanSource ?? 'навплан',
 529 |       generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
 530 |       note: 'Автозбірка весняного семестру',
 531 |       days: META.days,
 532 |       periodsPerDay: META.periodsPerDay,
 533 |       totalSlots: META.totalSlots,
 534 |     },
 535 |     groups: buildScheduleGroups(demands, groupsMap),
 536 |     teachers,
 537 |     rooms,
 538 |     entries,
 539 |   }
 540 |   return { schedule, placed, requested, unplaced, warnings }
 541 | }
 542 | 
 543 | export async function buildSpringScheduleAsync(
 544 |   store: PlanningStore,
 545 |   onProgress?: (progress: ScheduleBuildProgress) => void,
 546 | ): Promise<SpringScheduleResult> {
 547 |   const warnings: string[] = []
 548 | 
 549 |   await reportProgress(
 550 |     onProgress,
 551 |     'Підготовка',
 552 |     5,
 553 |     `Навплан: ${store.navPlan.length} рядків`,
 554 |   )
 555 | 
 556 |   await reportProgress(onProgress, 'Синхронізація груп', 12)
 557 |   const groupsMap = buildGroupsMapFromStore(store)
 558 |   const totalGroups = groupsMap.size
 559 | 
 560 |   await reportProgress(onProgress, 'Відбір предметів', 20)
 561 |   const { demands: rawDemands, duplicateKeys } = buildDemands(store, groupsMap)
 562 |   const { demands, warnings: parallelWarnings, bundleCount } = assignParallelBundles(rawDemands)
 563 |   warnings.push(...parallelWarnings)
 564 | 
 565 |   if (duplicateKeys.length > 0) {
 566 |     warnings.push(
 567 |       `Дублікати в навплані (група+предмет+викладач): ${duplicateKeys.length} — перевірте Excel.`,
 568 |     )
 569 |   }
 570 | 
 571 |   if (bundleCount > 0) {
 572 |     warnings.push(
 573 |       `Паралельні підгрупи: ${bundleCount} наборів (різні викладачі, один слот — напр. іноземна 13/9 студ.).`,
 574 |     )
 575 |   }
 576 | 
 577 |   const scheduleUnits = buildScheduleUnits(demands)
 578 |   const pairQueue = buildFairPairQueue(scheduleUnits)
 579 | 
 580 |   const totalPairs = pairQueue.length
 581 | 
 582 |   if (demands.length === 0) {
 583 |     warnings.push('Немає рядків навплану з годинами весняного семестру.')
 584 |   }
 585 | 
 586 |   warnings.push(`Груп у навплані: ${totalGroups} (усі спеціальності, не лише КН).`)
 587 |   warnings.push('Без розкладу: практики, курсові, керівництво, КП/КР/ДП, ДПА/ДКК.')
 588 |   warnings.push('Викладач: за замовчуванням 3–4 пари на день (max 4); преференції на вкладці «Правила».')
 589 | 
 590 |   const remoteGroups = demands.filter((d) => d.remote).length
 591 |   const shift2Groups = new Set(demands.filter((d) => d.shift === 2).map((d) => d.groupCode)).size
 592 |   if (remoteGroups > 0) {
 593 |     warnings.push(
 594 |       `Дистанційний режим (2–3 курс, непарна підгрупа): ${remoteGroups} предметів — аудиторія «Дист».`,
 595 |     )
 596 |   }
 597 |   warnings.push(`2–3 курс → зміна 2 (пари 5–8): ${shift2Groups} груп.`)
 598 | 
 599 |   await reportProgress(
 600 |     onProgress,
 601 |     'Відбір предметів',
 602 |     28,
 603 |     `${demands.length} рядків · ${scheduleUnits.length} блоків · ${totalPairs} пар на тиждень`,
 604 |   )
 605 | 
 606 |   const occ = createOccupancy()
 607 |   const entries: ScheduleEntry[] = []
 608 |   const unplaced: LessonDemand[] = []
 609 |   let requested = 0
 610 |   let placed = 0
 611 |   let donePairs = 0
 612 | 
 613 |   await reportProgress(onProgress, 'Розміщення пар', 30)
 614 | 
 615 |   for (const unit of pairQueue) {
 616 |     requested += unit.type === 'parallel' ? unit.demands.length : 1
 617 |     donePairs += 1
 618 | 
 619 |     if (unit.type === 'parallel') {
 620 |       const slotId = pickParallelSlot(unit.demands, occ)
 621 |       if (slotId === null) {
 622 |         for (const demand of unit.demands) unplaced.push({ ...demand, pairsPerWeek: 1 })
 623 |       } else {
 624 |         placeParallelBundle(unit.demands, slotId, occ, entries)
 625 |         placed += unit.demands.length
 626 |       }
 627 |     } else {
 628 |       const slotId = pickSlot(unit.demand, occ)
 629 |       if (slotId === null) {
 630 |         unplaced.push({ ...unit.demand, pairsPerWeek: 1 })
 631 |       } else {
 632 |         placeEntry(unit.demand, slotId, occ, entries)
 633 |         placed += 1
 634 |       }
 635 |     }
 636 | 
 637 |     if (
 638 |       totalPairs > 0 &&
 639 |       (donePairs === 1 || donePairs === totalPairs || donePairs % 20 === 0)
 640 |     ) {
 641 |       const percent = 30 + Math.round((donePairs / totalPairs) * 58)
 642 |       await reportProgress(
 643 |         onProgress,
 644 |         'Розміщення пар',
 645 |         percent,
 646 |         `${donePairs} / ${totalPairs} · розміщено ${placed}`,
 647 |       )
 648 |     }
 649 |   }
 650 | 
 651 |   if (unplaced.length > 0) {
 652 |     await reportProgress(onProgress, 'Дорозміщення', 88, `${unplaced.length} пар`)
 653 |     const retry = [...unplaced]
 654 |     unplaced.length = 0
 655 |     for (const demand of retry) {
 656 |       const strictSlot = pickSlot(demand, occ, { relaxSpacing: true })
 657 |       const slotId =
 658 |         strictSlot ?? pickSlot(demand, occ, { relaxSpacing: true, ignoreRoom: true })
 659 |       if (slotId === null) {
 660 |         unplaced.push(demand)
 661 |         continue
 662 |       }
 663 |       placeEntry(demand, slotId, occ, entries, {
 664 |         skipRoomOccupy: strictSlot === null,
 665 |       })
 666 |       placed += 1
 667 |     }
 668 |   }
 669 | 
 670 |   if (unplaced.length > 0) {
 671 |     warnings.push(`Не вдалось розмістити ${unplaced.length} пар — перевірте конфлікти.`)
 672 |     const sample = unplaced.slice(0, 8).map((d) => `${d.groupCode} · ${d.subject} · ${d.teacher}`)
 673 |     warnings.push(`Приклади: ${sample.join('; ')}${unplaced.length > 8 ? '…' : ''}`)
 674 |   }
 675 | 
 676 |   await reportProgress(onProgress, 'Збереження результату', 92)
 677 | 
 678 |   const result = buildSpringScheduleResult(
 679 |     store,
 680 |     groupsMap,
 681 |     demands,
 682 |     warnings,
 683 |     entries,
 684 |     unplaced,
 685 |     placed,
 686 |     requested,
 687 |   )
 688 | 
 689 |   await reportProgress(
 690 |     onProgress,
 691 |     'Готово',
 692 |     100,
 693 |     `${placed} з ${requested} пар · ${totalGroups} груп`,
 694 |   )
 695 | 
 696 |   return result
 697 | }

Файл: src/storage/cylinderFilterStorage.ts
Рядків: 46

   1 | import type { Filters } from '../types/schedule'
   2 | import { defaultScheduleFilters } from '../utils/scheduleFilters'
   3 | 
   4 | const STORAGE_KEY = 'schedule3d-cylinder-filters-v1'
   5 | 
   6 | function isFilters(value: unknown): value is Filters {
   7 |   if (!value || typeof value !== 'object') return false
   8 |   const v = value as Record<string, unknown>
   9 |   return (
  10 |     typeof v.specialty === 'string' &&
  11 |     typeof v.course === 'string' &&
  12 |     typeof v.groupCode === 'string' &&
  13 |     typeof v.teacher === 'string' &&
  14 |     typeof v.day === 'string' &&
  15 |     typeof v.conflictsOnly === 'boolean'
  16 |   )
  17 | }
  18 | 
  19 | export function loadCylinderFilters(): Filters {
  20 |   try {
  21 |     const raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY)
  22 |     if (!raw) return defaultScheduleFilters
  23 |     const parsed: unknown = JSON.parse(raw)
  24 |     if (!isFilters(parsed)) return defaultScheduleFilters
  25 |     return { ...defaultScheduleFilters, ...parsed }
  26 |   } catch {
  27 |     return defaultScheduleFilters
  28 |   }
  29 | }
  30 | 
  31 | export function saveCylinderFilters(filters: Filters): void {
  32 |   try {
  33 |     localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(filters))
  34 |   } catch {
  35 |     // ignore quota / private mode
  36 |   }
  37 | }
  38 | 
  39 | export function clearCylinderFilters(): void {

   1 | import type { NavPlanSnapshot, PrintScheduleDocument, ScheduleDocument } from '../types/documents'
   2 | import type { PlanningStore } from '../types/planning'
   3 | import type { ScheduleData } from '../types/schedule'
   4 | import { normalizeNavPlanRow } from '../utils/parseNavPlan'
   5 | import { newId } from '../utils/normalize'
   6 | import { ensureEditorName } from './editorIdentity'
   7 | 
   8 | const DB_NAME = 'schedule3d-files-v1'
   9 | const DB_VERSION = 2
  10 | const STORE_FILES = 'files'
  11 | const STORE_NAV_SNAPSHOTS = 'navPlanSnapshots'
  12 | const STORE_SCHEDULE_DOCS = 'scheduleDocuments'
  13 | const STORE_PRINT = 'printSchedules'
  14 | 
  15 | function openDb(): Promise<IDBDatabase> {
  16 |   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
  17 |     const request = indexedDB.open(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION)
  18 |     request.onupgradeneeded = () => {
  19 |       const db = request.result
  20 |       if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(STORE_FILES)) {
  21 |         db.createObjectStore(STORE_FILES)
  22 |       }
  23 |       if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(STORE_NAV_SNAPSHOTS)) {
  24 |         db.createObjectStore(STORE_NAV_SNAPSHOTS, { keyPath: 'id' })
  25 |       }
  26 |       if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(STORE_SCHEDULE_DOCS)) {
  27 |         db.createObjectStore(STORE_SCHEDULE_DOCS, { keyPath: 'id' })
  28 |       }
  29 |       if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(STORE_PRINT)) {
  30 |         db.createObjectStore(STORE_PRINT, { keyPath: 'id' })
  31 |       }
  32 |     }
  33 |     request.onsuccess = () => resolve(request.result)
  34 |     request.onerror = () => reject(request.error ?? new Error('IndexedDB'))
  35 |   })
  36 | }
  37 | 
  38 | function idbGet<T>(storeName: string, key: string): Promise<T | null> {
  39 |   return openDb().then(
  40 |     (db) =>
  41 |       new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
  42 |         const tx = db.transaction(storeName, 'readonly')
  43 |         const req = tx.objectStore(storeName).get(key)
  44 |         req.onsuccess = () => resolve((req.result as T | undefined) ?? null)
  45 |         req.onerror = () => reject(req.error ?? new Error('IndexedDB read'))
  46 |       }),
  47 |   )
  48 | }
  49 | 
  50 | function idbGetAll<T>(storeName: string): Promise<T[]> {
  51 |   return openDb().then(
  52 |     (db) =>
  53 |       new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
  54 |         const tx = db.transaction(storeName, 'readonly')
  55 |         const req = tx.objectStore(storeName).getAll()
  56 |         req.onsuccess = () => resolve((req.result as T[]) ?? [])
  57 |         req.onerror = () => reject(req.error ?? new Error('IndexedDB readAll'))
  58 |       }),
  59 |   )
  60 | }
  61 | 
  62 | function idbPutKey(storeName: string, key: string, value: unknown): Promise<void> {
  63 |   return openDb().then(
  64 |     (db) =>
  65 |       new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
  66 |         const tx = db.transaction(storeName, 'readwrite')
  67 |         tx.oncomplete = () => resolve()
  68 |         tx.onerror = () => reject(tx.error ?? new Error('IndexedDB write'))
  69 |         tx.objectStore(storeName).put(value, key)
  70 |       }),
  71 |   )
  72 | }
  73 | 
  74 | function idbPut<T>(storeName: string, value: T): Promise<void> {
  75 |   return openDb().then(
  76 |     (db) =>
  77 |       new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
  78 |         const tx = db.transaction(storeName, 'readwrite')
  79 |         tx.oncomplete = () => resolve()
  80 |         tx.onerror = () => reject(tx.error ?? new Error('IndexedDB write'))
  81 |         tx.objectStore(storeName).put(value)
  82 |       }),
  83 |   )
  84 | }
  85 | 
  86 | function idbDelete(storeName: string, key: string): Promise<void> {
  87 |   return openDb().then(
  88 |     (db) =>
  89 |       new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
  90 |         const tx = db.transaction(storeName, 'readwrite')
  91 |         tx.oncomplete = () => resolve()
  92 |         tx.onerror = () => reject(tx.error ?? new Error('IndexedDB delete'))
  93 |         tx.objectStore(storeName).delete(key)
  94 |       }),
  95 |   )
  96 | }
  97 | 
  98 | export async function idbGetFile<T>(key: string): Promise<T | null> {
  99 |   return idbGet<T>(STORE_FILES, key)
 100 | }
 101 | 
 102 | export async function idbSetFile(key: string, value: unknown): Promise<void> {
 103 |   return idbPutKey(STORE_FILES, key, value)
 104 | }

 106 | export async function listNavPlanSnapshots(): Promise<NavPlanSnapshot[]> {
 107 |   const rows = await idbGetAll<NavPlanSnapshot>(STORE_NAV_SNAPSHOTS)
 108 |   return rows.sort((a, b) => b.savedAt.localeCompare(a.savedAt))
 109 | }

 115 |   savedBy?: string,
 116 | ): Promise<NavPlanSnapshot> {
 117 |   const existing = await listNavPlanSnapshots()
 118 |   const version = (existing[0]?.version ?? 0) + 1
 119 |   const snapshot: NavPlanSnapshot = {

 121 |     version,
 122 |     label: label.trim() || `Версія ${version}`,
 123 |     savedAt: new Date().toISOString(),

 126 |     sourceFileName: store.navPlanSource,

 129 |     payload: {

 131 |       groups: structuredClone(store.groups),
 132 |       roomRules: structuredClone(store.roomRules),
 133 |       teacherPrefs: structuredClone(store.teacherPrefs),
 134 |       subjectPrefs: structuredClone(store.subjectPrefs),
 135 |       navPlanSource: store.navPlanSource,
 136 |       navPlanColumnsVersion: store.navPlanColumnsVersion ?? 2,
 137 |     },
 138 |   }
 139 |   await idbPut(STORE_NAV_SNAPSHOTS, snapshot)
 140 |   return snapshot
 141 | }

   8 |   }

  13 |     localStorage.setItem(EDITOR_KEY, name.trim())
  14 |   } catch {
  15 |     // ignore
  16 |   }
  17 | }

  19 | /** Запитує ПІБ один раз і зберігає для подальших версій. */
  20 | export function ensureEditorName(): string {
  21 |   const existing = getEditorName()
  22 |   if (existing) return existing
  23 |   const entered = window.prompt('Ваше прізвище або ПІБ (для журналу змін):', '')?.trim()
  24 |   if (!entered) return 'Невідомий'
  25 |   setEditorName(entered)
  26 |   return entered
  27 | }

   1 | import { idbGetFile, idbSetFile } from './documentStorage'
   2 | 
   3 | export type ExportLocationMode = 'downloads' | 'folder'
   4 | 
   5 | export type ExportLocationPrefs = {
   6 |   mode: ExportLocationMode
   7 |   folderLabel?: string
   8 | }
   9 | 
  10 | const PREFS_KEY = 'schedule3d-export-location-v1'
  11 | const HANDLE_KEY = 'exportDirectoryHandle'
  12 | 
  13 | export function loadExportLocationPrefs(): ExportLocationPrefs {
  14 |   try {
  15 |     const raw = localStorage.getItem(PREFS_KEY)
  16 |     if (!raw) return { mode: 'downloads' }
  17 |     const parsed = JSON.parse(raw) as ExportLocationPrefs
  18 |     return {
  19 |       mode: parsed.mode === 'folder' ? 'folder' : 'downloads',
  20 |       folderLabel: parsed.folderLabel,
  21 |     }
  22 |   } catch {
  23 |     return { mode: 'downloads' }
  24 |   }
  25 | }
  26 | 
  27 | export function saveExportLocationPrefs(prefs: ExportLocationPrefs): void {
  28 |   localStorage.setItem(PREFS_KEY, JSON.stringify(prefs))
  29 | }
  30 | 
  31 | export function isFolderExportSupported(): boolean {
  32 |   return typeof window !== 'undefined' && 'showDirectoryPicker' in window
  33 | }
  34 | 
  35 | export async function getStoredExportFolderHandle(): Promise<FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null> {
  36 |   if (!isFolderExportSupported()) return null
  37 |   const handle = await idbGetFile<FileSystemDirectoryHandle>(HANDLE_KEY)
  38 |   return handle ?? null
  39 | }
  40 | 
  41 | async function verifyFolderPermission(handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle): Promise<boolean> {
  42 |   const opts = { mode: 'readwrite' as const }
  43 |   if ((await handle.queryPermission(opts)) === 'granted') return true
  44 |   return (await handle.requestPermission(opts)) === 'granted'
  45 | }
  46 | 
  47 | export async function pickExportFolder(): Promise<ExportLocationPrefs | null> {
  48 |   if (!isFolderExportSupported()) return null
  49 |   const handle = await window.showDirectoryPicker({ mode: 'readwrite' })
  50 |   const allowed = await verifyFolderPermission(handle)
  51 |   if (!allowed) return null
  52 |   await idbSetFile(HANDLE_KEY, handle)
  53 |   const prefs: ExportLocationPrefs = { mode: 'folder', folderLabel: handle.name }
  54 |   saveExportLocationPrefs(prefs)
  55 |   return prefs
  56 | }
  57 | 
  58 | export async function resolveExportFolderHandle(): Promise<FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null> {
  59 |   const prefs = loadExportLocationPrefs()
  60 |   if (prefs.mode !== 'folder') return null
  61 |   const handle = await getStoredExportFolderHandle()
  62 |   if (!handle) return null
  63 |   const allowed = await verifyFolderPermission(handle)
  64 |   return allowed ? handle : null
  65 | }
  66 | 
  67 | export async function clearExportFolder(): Promise<void> {
  68 |   saveExportLocationPrefs({ mode: 'downloads' })
  69 |   await idbSetFile(HANDLE_KEY, null)
  70 | }
  71 |

  16 |     const parsed = JSON.parse(raw) as PlanningStore

  22 |       roomRules: parsed.roomRules?.length ? parsed.roomRules : DEFAULT_ROOM_RULES,

  24 |       subjectPrefs: parsed.subjectPrefs ?? DEFAULT_SUBJECT_PREFS,
  25 |     }
  26 |   } catch {
  27 |     return createDefaultStore()
  28 |   }
  29 | }

  18 |   return APP_PAGES.includes(value as AppPage)

  20 | 
  21 | export function readAppPageFromHash(): AppPage {
  22 |   const raw = window.location.hash.replace(/^#\/?/, '').split('?')[0]?.trim() ?? ''
  23 |   if (isAppPage(raw)) return raw
  24 |   const legacy = LEGACY_PAGE_ALIASES[raw]
  25 |   if (legacy) return legacy
  26 |   return 'nav'
  27 | }
  28 | 
  29 | export function writeAppPageToHash(page: AppPage) {
  30 |   const next = `#/${page}`
  31 |   if (window.location.hash !== next) {
  32 |     window.location.hash = next
  33 |   }

  16 |   scope: BatchExportScope

  20 |   includeGroupJson: boolean

  37 | function resolveTargetGroups(schedule: ScheduleData, options: BatchExportOptions): Group[] {
  38 |   const sorted = [...schedule.groups].sort((a, b) => a.code.localeCompare(b.code, 'uk'))
  39 |   if (options.scope === 'all') return sorted
  40 |   const selected = new Set(options.groupCodes.map((code) => code.trim().toUpperCase()))
  41 |   return sorted.filter((group) => selected.has(group.code.toUpperCase()))
  42 | }
  43 | 
  44 | export function buildGroupPrintDocument(schedule: ScheduleData, group: Group): PrintScheduleDocument {
  45 |   const entries = schedule.entries.filter((entry) => entry.groupId === group.id)
  46 |   return createPrintScheduleDocument(
  47 |     schedule,
  48 |     'group',
  49 |     group.code,
  50 |     `Група ${group.code}`,
  51 |     entries,
  52 |     ensureEditorName(),
  53 |   )
  54 | }
  55 | 
  56 | function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {
  57 |   return new Promise((resolve) => window.setTimeout(resolve, ms))
  58 | }
  59 | 
  60 | function countFiles(groups: Group[], options: BatchExportOptions): number {
  61 |   let total = 1
  62 |   if (options.includeFullScheduleJson) total += 1
  63 |   const perGroup = Number(options.includeGroupHtml) + Number(options.includeGroupJson)
  64 |   total += groups.length * perGroup
  65 |   return total
  66 | }
  67 | 
  68 | export async function exportScheduleBatch(
  69 |   schedule: ScheduleData,
  70 |   options: BatchExportOptions,
  71 |   onProgress?: (progress: BatchExportProgress) => void,
  72 | ): Promise<BatchExportResult> {
  73 |   const groups = resolveTargetGroups(schedule, options)
  74 |   if (groups.length === 0) {
  75 |     throw new Error('Не обрано жодної групи для експорту')
  76 |   }
  77 | 
  78 |   const sessionName = exportSessionFolderName()
  79 |   const sessionDir = await createExportSessionDirectory()
  80 |   const sessionFolder = sessionDir ? sessionName : undefined
  81 |   let method: 'folder' | 'downloads' = sessionDir ? 'folder' : 'downloads'
  82 | 
  83 |   const total = countFiles(groups, options)
  84 |   let done = 0
  85 |   const report = (label: string) => {
  86 |     done += 1
  87 |     onProgress?.({ done, total, label })
  88 |   }
  89 | 
  90 |   const manifest = {
  91 |     exportedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  92 |     exportedBy: ensureEditorName(),
  93 |     scope: options.scope,
  94 |     groups: groups.map((group) => group.code),
  95 |     source: schedule.meta.sourceFile,
  96 |     generatedAt: schedule.meta.generatedAt,
  97 |     sessionFolder,
  98 |   }
  99 | 
 100 |   const manifestResult = await writeExportFile(
 101 |     sessionDir ? 'manifest.json' : `${sessionName}_manifest.json`,
 102 |     JSON.stringify(manifest, null, 2),
 103 |     'application/json;charset=utf-8',
 104 |     sessionDir,
 105 |   )
 106 |   method = manifestResult.method
 107 |   report('manifest.json')
 108 |   if (!sessionDir) await sleep(180)
 109 | 
 110 |   if (options.includeFullScheduleJson) {
 111 |     const fullResult = await writeExportFile(
 112 |       sessionDir ? 'schedule-full.json' : `${sessionName}_schedule-full.json`,
 113 |       JSON.stringify(schedule, null, 2),
 114 |       'application/json;charset=utf-8',
 115 |       sessionDir,
 116 |     )
 117 |     method = fullResult.method
 118 |     report('schedule-full.json')
 119 |     if (!sessionDir) await sleep(180)
 120 |   }
 121 | 
 122 |   for (const group of groups) {
 123 |     const safeCode = safeExportFileName(group.code)
 124 |     const doc = buildGroupPrintDocument(schedule, group)
 125 |     const basePath = sessionDir ? `groups/${safeCode}` : `${sessionName}_${safeCode}`
 126 | 
 127 |     if (options.includeGroupJson) {
 128 |       const jsonResult = await writeExportFile(
 129 |         sessionDir ? `${basePath}.json` : `${basePath}.json`,
 130 |         JSON.stringify(doc, null, 2),
 131 |         'application/json;charset=utf-8',
 132 |         sessionDir,
 133 |       )
 134 |       method = jsonResult.method
 135 |       report(`${group.code}.json`)
 136 |       if (!sessionDir) await sleep(180)
 137 |     }
 138 | 
 139 |     if (options.includeGroupHtml) {
 140 |       const htmlResult = await writeExportFile(
 141 |         sessionDir ? `${basePath}.html` : `${basePath}.html`,
 142 |         buildPrintScheduleHtml(doc),
 143 |         'text/html;charset=utf-8',
 144 |         sessionDir,
 145 |       )
 146 |       method = htmlResult.method
 147 |       report(`${group.code}.html`)
 148 |       if (!sessionDir) await sleep(180)
 149 |     }
 150 |   }
 151 | 
 152 |   const rootFolder = loadExportLocationPrefs().folderLabel
 153 | 
 154 |   return {
 155 |     groups: groups.length,
 156 |     files: done,
 157 |     method,
 158 |     sessionFolder,
 159 |     folderLabel: method === 'folder' ? `${rootFolder ?? 'папка'}/${sessionFolder}` : undefined,
 160 |   }
 161 | }

   1 | import type { ConflictKind, Group, ScheduleEntry } from '../types/schedule'
   2 | import { parallelSubjectKey } from './parallelSubgroups'
   3 | 
   4 | /** Паралельні підгрупи однієї групи в один слот — не накладка одна на одну. */
   5 | export function isParallelPeer(a: ScheduleEntry, b: ScheduleEntry): boolean {
   6 |   if (a.id === b.id) return false
   7 |   if (a.slotId !== b.slotId) return false
   8 | 
   9 |   if (a.parallelBundleId && b.parallelBundleId && a.parallelBundleId === b.parallelBundleId) {
  10 |     return true
  11 |   }
  12 | 
  13 |   return (
  14 |     a.groupId === b.groupId &&
  15 |     parallelSubjectKey(a.subject) === parallelSubjectKey(b.subject)
  16 |   )
  17 | }
  18 | 
  19 | export function detectEntryConflict(entry: ScheduleEntry, allEntries: ScheduleEntry[]): ConflictKind {
  20 |   const teacherConflict = allEntries.some(
  21 |     (other) =>
  22 |       other.id !== entry.id &&
  23 |       !isParallelPeer(entry, other) &&
  24 |       other.slotId === entry.slotId &&
  25 |       other.teacher === entry.teacher,
  26 |   )
  27 | 
  28 |   if (teacherConflict) return 'teacher'
  29 | 
  30 |   const roomConflict = allEntries.some(
  31 |     (other) =>
  32 |       other.id !== entry.id &&
  33 |       !isParallelPeer(entry, other) &&
  34 |       other.slotId === entry.slotId &&
  35 |       other.room === entry.room &&
  36 |       entry.room !== 'Дист' &&
  37 |       other.room !== 'Дист',
  38 |   )
  39 | 
  40 |   if (roomConflict) return 'room'
  41 | 
  42 |   return 'none'
  43 | }
  44 | 
  45 | export function enrichEntries(entries: ScheduleEntry[]) {
  46 |   return entries.map((entry) => ({
  47 |     ...entry,
  48 |     conflict: detectEntryConflict(entry, entries),
  49 |   }))
  50 | }
  51 | 
  52 | export function findConflictsForEntry(entry: ScheduleEntry, allEntries: ScheduleEntry[]) {
  53 |   return allEntries.filter(
  54 |     (other) =>
  55 |       other.id !== entry.id &&
  56 |       !isParallelPeer(entry, other) &&
  57 |       other.slotId === entry.slotId &&
  58 |       (other.teacher === entry.teacher ||
  59 |         (other.room === entry.room && entry.room !== 'Дист' && other.room !== 'Дист')),
  60 |   )
  61 | }
  62 | 
  63 | export type ConflictReason = 'teacher' | 'room' | 'both'
  64 | 
  65 | export function conflictReasonBetween(entry: ScheduleEntry, other: ScheduleEntry): ConflictReason {
  66 |   const teacher = entry.teacher === other.teacher
  67 |   const room =
  68 |     entry.room === other.room && entry.room !== 'Дист' && other.room !== 'Дист'
  69 | 
  70 |   if (teacher && room) return 'both'
  71 |   if (teacher) return 'teacher'
  72 |   return 'room'
  73 | }
  74 | 
  75 | export function conflictReasonLabel(reason: ConflictReason): string {
  76 |   if (reason === 'teacher') return 'викладач'
  77 |   if (reason === 'room') return 'аудиторія'
  78 |   return 'викладач і аудиторія'
  79 | }
  80 | 
  81 | export function describeConflictEntry(other: ScheduleEntry, groupById: Map<string, Group>): string {
  82 |   const code = groupById.get(other.groupId)?.code ?? '?'
  83 |   return `${code} · ${other.subject} · ${other.teacher} · ауд. ${other.room}`
  84 | }
  85 | 
  86 | export type DescribedConflict = {
  87 |   entry: ScheduleEntry
  88 |   reason: ConflictReason
  89 |   reasonLabel: string
  90 |   summary: string
  91 | }
  92 | 
  93 | export function describeConflictWithReason(
  94 |   entry: ScheduleEntry,
  95 |   other: ScheduleEntry,
  96 |   groupById: Map<string, Group>,
  97 | ): DescribedConflict {
  98 |   const reason = conflictReasonBetween(entry, other)
  99 |   return {
 100 |     entry: other,
 101 |     reason,
 102 |     reasonLabel: conflictReasonLabel(reason),
 103 |     summary: describeConflictEntry(other, groupById),
 104 |   }
 105 | }
 106 | 
 107 | export function describeConflictsForEntry(
 108 |   entry: ScheduleEntry,
 109 |   allEntries: ScheduleEntry[],
 110 |   groupById: Map<string, Group>,
 111 | ): DescribedConflict[] {
 112 |   return findConflictsForEntry(entry, allEntries).map((other) =>
 113 |     describeConflictWithReason(entry, other, groupById),
 114 |   )
 115 | }
 116 | 
 117 | export function conflictColor(conflict: ConflictKind, selected: boolean, hovered: boolean) {
 118 |   if (conflict === 'teacher') return selected ? '#ff5a5f' : hovered ? '#ff7b7f' : '#d64545'
 119 |   if (conflict === 'room') return selected ? '#ffb020' : hovered ? '#ffc857' : '#d8891d'
 120 |   return selected ? '#4da3ff' : hovered ? '#66b2ff' : '#3b82c4'

   7 | export function safeExportFileName(value: string): string {
   8 |   return (
   9 |     String(value ?? '')
  10 |       .trim()
  11 |       .replace(/[<>:"/\\|?*\u0000-\u001f]/g, '_')
  12 |       .replace(/\s+/g, '_')
  13 |       .replace(/_+/g, '_')
  14 |       .slice(0, 80) || 'export'
  15 |   )
  16 | }
  17 | 
  18 | export function exportSessionFolderName(prefix = 'schedule-export'): string {
  19 |   const now = new Date()
  20 |   const date = now.toISOString().slice(0, 10)
  21 |   const time = now.toTimeString().slice(0, 8).replace(/:/g, '-')
  22 |   return `${prefix}_${date}_${time}`
  23 | }
  24 | 
  25 | function triggerBrowserDownload(filename: string, content: string, mimeType: string): void {
  26 |   const blob = new Blob([content], { type: mimeType })
  27 |   const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob)
  28 |   const link = document.createElement('a')
  29 |   link.href = url
  30 |   link.download = filename
  31 |   link.click()
  32 |   URL.revokeObjectURL(url)
  33 | }
  34 | 
  35 | async function getOrCreateSubdirectory(
  36 |   root: FileSystemDirectoryHandle,
  37 |   pathParts: string[],
  38 | ): Promise<FileSystemDirectoryHandle> {
  39 |   let current = root
  40 |   for (const part of pathParts) {
  41 |     if (!part) continue
  42 |     current = await current.getDirectoryHandle(part, { create: true })
  43 |   }
  44 |   return current
  45 | }
  46 | 
  47 | async function writeToFolder(
  48 |   root: FileSystemDirectoryHandle,
  49 |   relativePath: string,
  50 |   content: string,
  51 | ): Promise<void> {
  52 |   const normalized = relativePath.replace(/\\/g, '/').replace(/^\/+/, '')
  53 |   const parts = normalized.split('/')
  54 |   const fileName = parts.pop()
  55 |   if (!fileName) throw new Error('Invalid export path')
  56 | 
  57 |   const dir = parts.length > 0 ? await getOrCreateSubdirectory(root, parts) : root
  58 |   const fileHandle = await dir.getFileHandle(fileName, { create: true })
  59 |   const writable = await fileHandle.createWritable()
  60 |   await writable.write(content)
  61 |   await writable.close()
  62 | }
  63 | 
  64 | export type WriteExportFileResult = {
  65 |   method: ExportLocationMode
  66 |   path: string
  67 | }
  68 | 
  69 | export async function writeExportFile(
  70 |   relativePath: string,
  71 |   content: string,
  72 |   mimeType = 'text/plain;charset=utf-8',
  73 |   folderRoot?: FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null,
  74 | ): Promise<WriteExportFileResult> {
  75 |   const prefs = loadExportLocationPrefs()
  76 |   const handle = folderRoot ?? (prefs.mode === 'folder' ? await resolveExportFolderHandle() : null)
  77 | 
  78 |   if (handle) {
  79 |     await writeToFolder(handle, relativePath, content)
  80 |     return { method: 'folder', path: relativePath }
  81 |   }
  82 | 
  83 |   const fileName = relativePath.replace(/\\/g, '/').split('/').pop() ?? relativePath
  84 |   triggerBrowserDownload(fileName, content, mimeType)
  85 |   return { method: 'downloads', path: fileName }
  86 | }
  87 | 
  88 | export async function createExportSessionDirectory(): Promise<FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null> {
  89 |   const root = await resolveExportFolderHandle()
  90 |   if (!root) return null
  91 |   return root.getDirectoryHandle(exportSessionFolderName(), { create: true })
  92 | }

   1 | /** Розбиває фільтр на частини через кому або крапку з комою. */
   2 | export function splitFilterTerms(filter: string): string[] {
   3 |   return filter
   4 |     .split(/[,;]+/)
   5 |     .map((part) => part.trim())
   6 |     .filter(Boolean)
   7 | }
   8 | 
   9 | export function hasFilterTerms(filter: string): boolean {
  10 |   return splitFilterTerms(filter).length > 0
  11 | }
  12 | 
  13 | function matchesSingleText(haystack: string, term: string): boolean {
  14 |   const q = term.trim().toLowerCase()
  15 |   if (!q) return true
  16 |   return haystack.toLowerCase().includes(q)
  17 | }
  18 | 
  19 | /** Будь-який термін збігається (OR). Порожній фільтр = усі. */
  20 | export function matchesAnyText(haystack: string, filter: string): boolean {
  21 |   const terms = splitFilterTerms(filter)
  22 |   if (terms.length === 0) return true
  23 |   return terms.some((term) => matchesSingleText(haystack, term))
  24 | }
  25 | 
  26 | export function matchesAnyTerm<T>(
  27 |   filter: string,
  28 |   matcher: (item: T, term: string) => boolean,
  29 |   item: T,
  30 | ): boolean {
  31 |   const terms = splitFilterTerms(filter)
  32 |   if (terms.length === 0) return true
  33 |   return terms.some((term) => matcher(item, term))
  34 | }
  35 | 
  36 | export function filterTextOptions(options: string[], query: string, limit = 40): string[] {
  37 |   const q = query.trim()
  38 |   const filtered = q ? options.filter((opt) => matchesAnyText(opt, q)) : options
  39 |   return filtered.slice(0, limit)
  40 | }

Файл: src/utils/groupCode.ts
Рядків: 53
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   1 | import { normalizeGroupCode } from './normalize'
   2 | 
   3 | export type ParsedGroupCode = {
   4 |   code: string
   5 |   specialty: string
   6 |   course: number
   7 |   subgroup: number
   8 | }
   9 | 
  10 | export function parseGroupCode(raw: string): ParsedGroupCode {
  11 |   const code = normalizeGroupCode(raw)
  12 | 
  13 |   const tailMatch = code.match(/^(.+?)[-]?(\d)(\d)$/)
  14 |   if (tailMatch) {
  15 |     return {
  16 |       code,
  17 |       specialty: tailMatch[1].replace(/-/g, ''),
  18 |       course: Number.parseInt(tailMatch[2], 10),
  19 |       subgroup: Number.parseInt(tailMatch[3], 10),
  20 |     }
  21 |   }
  22 | 
  23 |   const knMatch = code.match(/^([A-ZА-ЯІЇЄҐ]{1,6})(\d)(\d)$/)
  24 |   if (knMatch) {
  25 |     return {
  26 |       code,
  27 |       specialty: knMatch[1],
  28 |       course: Number.parseInt(knMatch[2], 10),
  29 |       subgroup: Number.parseInt(knMatch[3], 10),
  30 |     }
  31 |   }
  32 | 
  33 |   const digit = code.match(/\d/)?.[0]
  34 |   return {
  35 |     code,
  36 |     specialty: code.replace(/[\d-]/g, '').slice(0, 6) || code.slice(0, 2),
  37 |     course: digit ? Number.parseInt(digit, 10) : 1,
  38 |     subgroup: 1,
  39 |   }
  40 | }
  41 | 
  42 | /** 2–3 курс: непарна підгрупа — дистанційно, парна — очно (аудиторії не перетинаються). */
  43 | export function isRemoteGroup(code: string, course: number): boolean {
  44 |   if (course !== 2 && course !== 3) return false
  45 |   const { subgroup } = parseGroupCode(code)
  46 |   return subgroup % 2 === 1
  47 | }
  48 | 
  49 | export function effectiveShift(course: number, groupShift: 1 | 2): 1 | 2 {
  50 |   if (course === 2 || course === 3) return 2
  51 |   return groupShift
  52 | }
  53 |

   4 | 
   5 | /** Умовна аудиторія для групи без явного призначення. */
   6 | export function placeholderRoom(code: string, parsed?: ParsedGroupCode): string {
   7 |   const p = parsed ?? parseGroupCode(code)
   8 |   let hash = 0
   9 |   for (const ch of code) hash = (hash * 31 + ch.charCodeAt(0)) >>> 0
  10 |   const num = 200 + (hash % 350)
  11 |   return `~${p.specialty}${p.course}${p.subgroup}.${num}`
  12 | }
  13 | 
  14 | export function defaultWeeksSpring(parsed: ParsedGroupCode): number {
  15 |   if (parsed.course >= 4) return 9
  16 |   if (parsed.course === 3) return 16
  17 |   return 18
  18 | }
  19 | 
  20 | export function createGroupRowFromCode(code: string, existing?: GroupRow): GroupRow {
  21 |   const normalized = normalizeGroupCode(code)
  22 |   const parsed = parseGroupCode(normalized)
  23 |   return {
  24 |     id: existing?.id ?? newId('g'),
  25 |     code: normalized,
  26 |     weeksFall: existing?.weeksFall ?? 14,
  27 |     weeksSpring: existing?.weeksSpring ?? defaultWeeksSpring(parsed),
  28 |     room:
  29 |       existing?.room && !existing.room.startsWith('~') ? existing.room : placeholderRoom(normalized, parsed),
  30 |     shift: existing?.shift ?? (parsed.course === 2 || parsed.course === 3 ? 2 : 1),
  31 |   }
  32 | }
  33 | 
  34 | /** Додає в store усі групи з навплану (не лише КН з defaults). */
  35 | export function syncPlanningGroupsFromNavPlan(store: PlanningStore): PlanningStore {
  36 |   const map = new Map<string, GroupRow>()
  37 |   for (const g of store.groups) {
  38 |     map.set(normalizeGroupCode(g.code), g)
  39 |   }
  40 | 
  41 |   for (const row of store.navPlan) {
  42 |     if (!row.groupCode) continue
  43 |     const code = normalizeGroupCode(row.groupCode)
  44 |     if (map.has(code)) continue
  45 |     map.set(code, createGroupRowFromCode(code))
  46 |   }
  47 | 
  48 |   const groups = [...map.values()].sort((a, b) => a.code.localeCompare(b.code, 'uk'))
  49 |   return { ...store, groups }
  50 | }
  51 | 
  52 | export function buildGroupsMapFromStore(store: PlanningStore): Map<string, GroupRow> {
  53 |   const synced = syncPlanningGroupsFromNavPlan(store)
  54 |   const map = new Map<string, GroupRow>()
  55 |   for (const g of synced.groups) {
  56 |     map.set(normalizeGroupCode(g.code), g)
  57 |   }
  58 |   return map
  59 | }
  60 | 
  61 | export function ensureGroupRow(code: string, groupsMap: Map<string, GroupRow>): GroupRow {
  62 |   const normalized = normalizeGroupCode(code)
  63 |   const existing = groupsMap.get(normalized)
  64 |   if (existing) return existing
  65 |   const row = createGroupRowFromCode(normalized)
  66 |   groupsMap.set(normalized, row)
  67 |   return row
  68 | }
  69 |

Рядків: 125

   1 | import type { NavPlanRow, NavPlanRowKind } from '../types/planning'
   2 | import { springTeachingContactHours } from './subjectSchedule'
   3 | 
   4 | export type NavPlanClassification = {
   5 |   kind: NavPlanRowKind
   6 |   label: string
   7 | }
   8 | 
   9 | export type { NavPlanRowKind }
  10 | 
  11 | export const NAV_PLAN_KIND_LABELS: Record<NavPlanRowKind, string> = {
  12 |   schedule: 'У тижневий розклад',
  13 |   practice: 'Практика',
  14 |   coursework: 'Курсова (КР)',
  15 |   course_project: 'Курсовий проект (КП)',
  16 |   supervision: 'Керівництво',
  17 |   diploma: 'Диплом / ДПА / ДКК',
  18 |   consultation: 'Консультації',
  19 |   unknown: 'Без назви',
  20 | }
  21 | 
  22 | const PRACTICE_RE =
  23 |   /навчальн.*практик|виробнич.*практик|педагогічн.*практик|ознайомлювальн.*практик|переддипломн.*практик|демонтажно.*практик|слюсарн.*практик|професійн.*практик|\bpractic(?:e|um)\b/i
  24 | 
  25 | const SUPERVISION_RE = /керівництв|кер\.?\s*п|\bsupervis/i
  26 | 
  27 | const DIPLOMA_RE = /диплом|дпа|дкк|\bdiploma\b|\bthesis\b|\bdpa\b|\bdkk\b/i
  28 | 
  29 | const COURSE_PROJECT_RE =
  30 |   /курсов(?:ий|ого)?\s*проект|\([^)]*\b(кп|cp|kp)\b[^)]*\)|(?:^|[\s(])(?:кп|cp|kp)(?:[\s,)])/i
  31 | 
  32 | const COURSEWORK_RE =
  33 |   /курсов(?:а|і|ий|ого)?(?:\s|$)|\([^)]*\b(кр|cr|cw|kr)\b[^)]*\)|(?:^|[\s(])(?:кр|cr|cw|kr)(?:[\s,)])/i
  34 | 
  35 | const CONSULTATION_RE = /консульт|\bconsult/i
  36 | 
  37 | /** Латиниця + кирилиця в дужках і як окремі позначки. */
  38 | const PAREN_EXCLUDE_RE = /\([^)]*\b(кп|кр|дп|cp|cr|cw|kr|kp|dp)\b[^)]*\)/i
  39 | 
  40 | function isCourseProject(subject: string): boolean {
  41 |   return COURSE_PROJECT_RE.test(subject) || /\(\s*кп\b/i.test(subject)
  42 | }
  43 | 
  44 | function isCoursework(subject: string): boolean {
  45 |   if (isCourseProject(subject)) return false
  46 |   return COURSEWORK_RE.test(subject) || PAREN_EXCLUDE_RE.test(subject)
  47 | }
  48 | 
  49 | export function classifyNavPlanSubject(subject: string): NavPlanClassification {
  50 |   const s = subject.trim()
  51 |   if (!s) return { kind: 'unknown', label: NAV_PLAN_KIND_LABELS.unknown }
  52 | 
  53 |   if (PRACTICE_RE.test(s)) return { kind: 'practice', label: NAV_PLAN_KIND_LABELS.practice }
  54 |   if (SUPERVISION_RE.test(s)) return { kind: 'supervision', label: NAV_PLAN_KIND_LABELS.supervision }
  55 |   if (DIPLOMA_RE.test(s)) return { kind: 'diploma', label: NAV_PLAN_KIND_LABELS.diploma }
  56 |   if (isCourseProject(s)) return { kind: 'course_project', label: NAV_PLAN_KIND_LABELS.course_project }
  57 |   if (isCoursework(s)) return { kind: 'coursework', label: NAV_PLAN_KIND_LABELS.coursework }
  58 |   if (CONSULTATION_RE.test(s) && !/\b(лекці|практ|лаб)\b/i.test(s)) {
  59 |     return { kind: 'consultation', label: NAV_PLAN_KIND_LABELS.consultation }
  60 |   }
  61 | 
  62 |   return { kind: 'schedule', label: NAV_PLAN_KIND_LABELS.schedule }
  63 | }
  64 | 
  65 | /** Класифікація з урахуванням назви та колонок годин. */
  66 | export function classifyNavPlanRow(row: NavPlanRow): NavPlanClassification {
  67 |   const bySubject = classifyNavPlanSubject(row.subject)
  68 |   if (bySubject.kind !== 'schedule') return bySubject
  69 | 
  70 |   const springTeaching = springTeachingContactHours(row)
  71 |   if (row.springCoursework > 0 && springTeaching === 0) {
  72 |     return { kind: 'coursework', label: 'КР (лише колонка курсових)' }
  73 |   }
  74 |   if (row.springSupervised > 0 && springTeaching === 0 && row.springCoursework === 0) {
  75 |     return { kind: 'supervision', label: 'Керівництво (колонка)' }
  76 |   }
  77 |   if ((row.springDpa > 0 || row.springDkk > 0) && springTeaching === 0) {
  78 |     return { kind: 'diploma', label: 'ДПА/ДКК (колонка)' }
  79 |   }
  80 |   if (row.springConsult > 0 && springTeaching === 0 && row.hoursSpring <= row.springConsult) {
  81 |     return { kind: 'consultation', label: 'Консультації (колонка)' }
  82 |   }
  83 | 
  84 |   return bySubject
  85 | }
  86 | 
  87 | export function isSchedulableNavPlanRow(row: NavPlanRow): boolean {
  88 |   return classifyNavPlanRow(row).kind === 'schedule'
  89 | }
  90 | 
  91 | export function isSchedulableSubject(subject: string): boolean {
  92 |   return classifyNavPlanSubject(subject).kind === 'schedule'
  93 | }
  94 | 
  95 | export function summarizeNavPlanByKind(rows: NavPlanRow[]): Record<NavPlanRowKind, number> {
  96 |   const counts: Record<NavPlanRowKind, number> = {
  97 |     schedule: 0,
  98 |     practice: 0,
  99 |     coursework: 0,
 100 |     course_project: 0,
 101 |     supervision: 0,
 102 |     diploma: 0,
 103 |     consultation: 0,
 104 |     unknown: 0,
 105 |   }
 106 |   for (const row of rows) {
 107 |     counts[row.planKind ?? classifyNavPlanRow(row).kind] += 1
 108 |   }
 109 |   return counts
 110 | }
 111 | 
 112 | export const EXCLUDED_NAV_PLAN_KINDS: NavPlanRowKind[] = [
 113 |   'practice',
 114 |   'coursework',
 115 |   'course_project',
 116 |   'supervision',
 117 |   'diploma',
 118 |   'consultation',
 119 |   'unknown',
 120 | ]
 121 | 
 122 | export function isExcludedNavPlanKind(kind: NavPlanRowKind): boolean {
 123 |   return kind !== 'schedule'
 124 | }

   1 | import type { NavPlanRow } from '../types/planning'
   2 | import { normalizeGroupCode, normalizeTeacherField } from './normalize'
   3 | import { pairsPerWeek, springSchedulableHours } from './subjectSchedule'
   4 | 
   5 | export type NavPlanSubjectExpectation = {
   6 |   subject: string
   7 |   groupCode: string
   8 |   pairsPerWeek: number
   9 |   hours: number
  10 | }
  11 | 
  12 | export function teachersMatch(a: string, b: string): boolean {
  13 |   return normalizeTeacherField(a) === normalizeTeacherField(b)
  14 | }
  15 | 
  16 | /** Скільки пар/тиж очікується з навплану для викладача (лише planKind=schedule). */
  17 | export function navPlanExpectationsForTeacher(
  18 |   rows: NavPlanRow[],
  19 |   teacher: string,
  20 |   weeksByGroup: Map<string, number>,
  21 | ): NavPlanSubjectExpectation[] {
  22 |   const map = new Map<string, NavPlanSubjectExpectation>()
  23 | 
  24 |   for (const row of rows) {
  25 |     if (row.planKind !== 'schedule') continue
  26 |     if (!teachersMatch(row.teacher, teacher)) continue
  27 |     const hours = springSchedulableHours(row)
  28 |     if (hours <= 0) continue
  29 |     const weeks = weeksByGroup.get(normalizeGroupCode(row.groupCode)) ?? 16
  30 |     const weekly = pairsPerWeek(hours, weeks)
  31 |     if (weekly <= 0) continue
  32 | 
  33 |     const key = `${normalizeGroupCode(row.groupCode)}|${row.subject}`
  34 |     const existing = map.get(key)
  35 |     if (existing) {
  36 |       existing.pairsPerWeek = Math.max(existing.pairsPerWeek, weekly)
  37 |       existing.hours = Math.max(existing.hours, hours)
  38 |     } else {
  39 |       map.set(key, {
  40 |         subject: row.subject,
  41 |         groupCode: normalizeGroupCode(row.groupCode),
  42 |         pairsPerWeek: weekly,
  43 |         hours,
  44 |       })
  45 |     }
  46 |   }
  47 | 
  48 |   return [...map.values()].sort(
  49 |     (a, b) => a.subject.localeCompare(b.subject, 'uk') || a.groupCode.localeCompare(b.groupCode, 'uk'),
  50 |   )
  51 | }
  52 | 
  53 | export function summarizeExpectationsBySubject(
  54 |   expectations: NavPlanSubjectExpectation[],
  55 | ): Array<{ subject: string; groups: Array<{ code: string; pairsPerWeek: number }> }> {
  56 |   const bySubject = new Map<string, Map<string, number>>()
  57 |   for (const item of expectations) {
  58 |     if (!bySubject.has(item.subject)) bySubject.set(item.subject, new Map())
  59 |     const groups = bySubject.get(item.subject)!
  60 |     groups.set(item.groupCode, Math.max(groups.get(item.groupCode) ?? 0, item.pairsPerWeek))
  61 |   }
  62 |   return [...bySubject.entries()]
  63 |     .sort((a, b) => a[0].localeCompare(b[0], 'uk'))
  64 |     .map(([subject, groupsMap]) => ({
  65 |       subject,
  66 |       groups: [...groupsMap.entries()]
  67 |         .sort((a, b) => a[0].localeCompare(b[0], 'uk'))
  68 |         .map(([code, pairsPerWeek]) => ({ code, pairsPerWeek })),
  69 |     }))
  70 | }

   1 | import type { NavPlanFilters, NavPlanRow } from '../types/planning'
   2 | import { normalizeGroupCode, normalizeSubjectKey, normalizeTeacherField } from './normalize'
   3 | import { isExcludedNavPlanKind } from './navPlanClassify'
   4 | 
   5 | export const defaultNavPlanFilters: NavPlanFilters = {
   6 |   query: '',
   7 |   groupCode: '',
   8 |   subject: '',
   9 |   teacher: '',
  10 |   onlyWithTeacher: false,
  11 |   planKind: 'schedule',
  12 |   exams: '',
  13 |   credits: '',
  14 |   lectures: '',
  15 |   hoursTotalMin: '',
  16 |   hoursTotalMax: '',
  17 | }
  18 | 
  19 | export function totalExams(row: NavPlanRow): number {
  20 |   return row.fallExams + row.springExams
  21 | }
  22 | 
  23 | export function totalCredits(row: NavPlanRow): number {
  24 |   return row.fallCredits + row.springCredits
  25 | }
  26 | 
  27 | export function totalLectures(row: NavPlanRow): number {
  28 |   return row.fallLectures + row.springLectures
  29 | }
  30 | 
  31 | function parseBound(value: string): number | null {
  32 |   const trimmed = value.trim()
  33 |   if (!trimmed) return null
  34 |   const n = Number(trimmed.replace(',', '.'))
  35 |   return Number.isFinite(n) ? n : null
  36 | }
  37 | 
  38 | function matchesText(haystack: string, needle: string): boolean {
  39 |   const q = needle.trim().toLowerCase()
  40 |   if (!q) return true
  41 |   return haystack.toLowerCase().includes(q)
  42 | }
  43 | 
  44 | function matchesGroup(rowCode: string, filter: string): boolean {
  45 |   const q = filter.trim()
  46 |   if (!q) return true
  47 |   const code = normalizeGroupCode(rowCode)
  48 |   const query = normalizeGroupCode(q)
  49 |   return code.includes(query) || matchesText(rowCode, q)
  50 | }
  51 | 
  52 | function matchesSubject(row: NavPlanRow, filter: string): boolean {
  53 |   const q = filter.trim()
  54 |   if (!q) return true
  55 |   return (
  56 |     matchesText(row.subject, q) ||
  57 |     row.subjectNorm.includes(normalizeSubjectKey(q))
  58 |   )
  59 | }
  60 | 
  61 | function matchesTeacher(rowTeacher: string, filter: string): boolean {
  62 |   const q = filter.trim()
  63 |   if (!q) return true
  64 |   const normalizedRow = normalizeTeacherField(rowTeacher).toLowerCase()
  65 |   const normalizedQuery = normalizeTeacherField(q).toLowerCase()
  66 |   if (normalizedQuery && normalizedRow.includes(normalizedQuery)) return true
  67 |   return matchesText(rowTeacher, q)
  68 | }
  69 | 
  70 | /** Порожньо = усі; «є»/«немає» або число годин/кількості. */
  71 | function matchesTriSearch(value: number, filter: string): boolean {
  72 |   const f = filter.trim().toLowerCase()
  73 |   if (!f) return true
  74 |   if (['є', 'yes', 'так', '1', '+', 'y'].includes(f)) return value > 0
  75 |   if (['немає', 'нема', 'no', 'ні', '0', '-', 'n'].includes(f)) return value === 0
  76 |   const n = Number(f.replace(',', '.'))
  77 |   if (Number.isFinite(n)) return value === n
  78 |   return String(value).includes(f)
  79 | }
  80 | 
  81 | export function filterNavPlanRows(rows: NavPlanRow[], filters: NavPlanFilters): NavPlanRow[] {
  82 |   const q = filters.query.trim().toLowerCase()
  83 |   const minTotal = parseBound(filters.hoursTotalMin)
  84 |   const maxTotal = parseBound(filters.hoursTotalMax)
  85 | 
  86 |   return rows.filter((row) => {
  87 |     if (filters.planKind === 'schedule' && row.planKind !== 'schedule') return false
  88 |     if (filters.planKind === 'excluded' && !isExcludedNavPlanKind(row.planKind)) return false
  89 |     if (
  90 |       filters.planKind !== 'all' &&
  91 |       filters.planKind !== 'schedule' &&
  92 |       filters.planKind !== 'excluded' &&
  93 |       row.planKind !== filters.planKind
  94 |     ) {
  95 |       return false
  96 |     }
  97 |     if (!matchesGroup(row.groupCode, filters.groupCode)) return false
  98 |     if (!matchesSubject(row, filters.subject)) return false
  99 |     if (!matchesTeacher(row.teacher, filters.teacher)) return false
 100 |     if (filters.onlyWithTeacher && !row.teacher) return false
 101 |     if (!matchesTriSearch(totalExams(row), filters.exams)) return false
 102 |     if (!matchesTriSearch(totalCredits(row), filters.credits)) return false
 103 |     if (!matchesTriSearch(totalLectures(row), filters.lectures)) return false
 104 |     if (minTotal !== null && row.hoursTotal < minTotal) return false
 105 |     if (maxTotal !== null && row.hoursTotal > maxTotal) return false
 106 |     if (!q) return true
 107 |     return (
 108 |       row.subject.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
 109 |       row.subjectNorm.includes(q) ||
 110 |       row.teacher.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
 111 |       row.groupCode.toLowerCase().includes(q)
 112 |     )
 113 |   })
 114 | }
 115 |

 119 |     filters.groupCode.trim() !== '' ||
 120 |     filters.subject.trim() !== '' ||
 121 |     filters.teacher.trim() !== '' ||
 122 |     filters.onlyWithTeacher ||
 123 |     filters.planKind !== 'schedule' ||
 124 |     filters.exams.trim() !== '' ||
 125 |     filters.credits.trim() !== '' ||
 126 |     filters.lectures.trim() !== '' ||
 127 |     filters.hoursTotalMin.trim() !== '' ||
 128 |     filters.hoursTotalMax.trim() !== ''
 129 |   )
 130 | }

   1 | import type { NavPlanSnapshot } from '../types/documents'
   2 | import type { PlanningStore } from '../types/planning'

   4 | import { normalizeNavPlanRow } from './parseNavPlan'
   5 | import { downloadJsonFile } from './schedulePrintExport'
   6 | 
   7 | export const NAV_PLAN_JSON_TYPE = 'schedule3d-navplan-v1'
   8 | 
   9 | export type NavPlanExportDocument = {
  10 |   type: typeof NAV_PLAN_JSON_TYPE
  11 |   label: string
  12 |   savedAt: string
  13 |   savedBy: string
  14 |   note?: string
  15 |   sourceFileName?: string
  16 |   columnsVersion: number
  17 |   rowCount: number
  18 |   payload: NavPlanSnapshot['payload']
  19 | }
  20 | 
  21 | function isRecord(value: unknown): value is Record<string, unknown> {
  22 |   return typeof value === 'object' && value !== null
  23 | }
  24 | 
  25 | export function buildNavPlanExport(
  26 |   store: PlanningStore,
  27 |   options?: { label?: string; note?: string; savedBy?: string },
  28 | ): NavPlanExportDocument {
  29 |   return {
  30 |     type: NAV_PLAN_JSON_TYPE,
  31 |     label: options?.label?.trim() || `Навплан ${new Date().toLocaleString('uk-UA')}`,
  32 |     savedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  33 |     savedBy: options?.savedBy?.trim() || ensureEditorName(),
  34 |     note: options?.note?.trim() || undefined,
  35 |     sourceFileName: store.navPlanSource,
  36 |     columnsVersion: store.navPlanColumnsVersion ?? 2,
  37 |     rowCount: store.navPlan.length,
  38 |     payload: {
  39 |       navPlan: store.navPlan.map((row) => ({ ...row })),
  40 |       groups: structuredClone(store.groups),
  41 |       roomRules: structuredClone(store.roomRules),
  42 |       teacherPrefs: structuredClone(store.teacherPrefs),
  43 |       subjectPrefs: structuredClone(store.subjectPrefs),
  44 |       navPlanSource: store.navPlanSource,
  45 |       navPlanColumnsVersion: store.navPlanColumnsVersion ?? 2,
  46 |     },
  47 |   }
  48 | }
  49 | 
  50 | export function snapshotToExportDocument(snapshot: NavPlanSnapshot): NavPlanExportDocument {
  51 |   return {
  52 |     type: NAV_PLAN_JSON_TYPE,
  53 |     label: snapshot.label,
  54 |     savedAt: snapshot.savedAt,
  55 |     savedBy: snapshot.savedBy,
  56 |     note: snapshot.note,
  57 |     sourceFileName: snapshot.sourceFileName,
  58 |     columnsVersion: snapshot.columnsVersion,
  59 |     rowCount: snapshot.rowCount,
  60 |     payload: snapshot.payload,
  61 |   }
  62 | }
  63 | 
  64 | export function parseNavPlanImport(raw: unknown): NavPlanExportDocument {
  65 |   if (!isRecord(raw)) throw new Error('Некоректний JSON')
  66 | 
  67 |   const payload = raw.payload
  68 |   if (isRecord(payload) && Array.isArray(payload.navPlan)) {
  69 |     return {
  70 |       type: NAV_PLAN_JSON_TYPE,
  71 |       label: String(raw.label ?? 'Імпорт'),
  72 |       savedAt: String(raw.savedAt ?? new Date().toISOString()),
  73 |       savedBy: String(raw.savedBy ?? 'невідомо'),
  74 |       note: raw.note ? String(raw.note) : undefined,
  75 |       sourceFileName: raw.sourceFileName ? String(raw.sourceFileName) : undefined,
  76 |       columnsVersion: Number(raw.columnsVersion ?? payload.navPlanColumnsVersion ?? 2),
  77 |       rowCount: Number(raw.rowCount ?? payload.navPlan.length),
  78 |       payload: payload as NavPlanExportDocument['payload'],
  79 |     }
  80 |   }
  81 | 
  82 |   if ('id' in raw && isRecord(raw.payload) && Array.isArray(raw.payload.navPlan)) {
  83 |     return snapshotToExportDocument(raw as NavPlanSnapshot)
  84 |   }
  85 | 
  86 |   throw new Error('У файлі немає даних навплану (очікується payload.navPlan)')
  87 | }
  88 | 
  89 | export function applyNavPlanImport(store: PlanningStore, doc: NavPlanExportDocument): PlanningStore {
  90 |   return {
  91 |     ...store,
  92 |     ...doc.payload,
  93 |     navPlan: doc.payload.navPlan.map((row) => normalizeNavPlanRow(row)),
  94 |     groups: structuredClone(doc.payload.groups ?? store.groups),
  95 |     roomRules: structuredClone(doc.payload.roomRules ?? store.roomRules),
  96 |     teacherPrefs: structuredClone(doc.payload.teacherPrefs ?? store.teacherPrefs),
  97 |     subjectPrefs: structuredClone(doc.payload.subjectPrefs ?? store.subjectPrefs),
  98 |   }
  99 | }
 100 | 
 101 | export function exportNavPlanDocumentFile(doc: NavPlanExportDocument, filename?: string): void {
 102 |   const safe = doc.label.replace(/[^\w\u0400-\u04FF-]+/g, '_').slice(0, 40) || 'navplan'
 103 |   const datePart = doc.savedAt.slice(0, 10)
 104 |   downloadJsonFile(doc, filename ?? `navplan-${safe}-${datePart}.json`)
 105 | }

Файл: src/utils/normalize.ts

   1 | export function normalizeGroupCode(value: string): string {
   2 |   return String(value ?? '')
   3 |     .trim()
   4 |     .toUpperCase()
   5 |     .replace(/\s+/g, '')
   6 | }
   7 | 
   8 | export function normalizeSubjectKey(value: string): string {
   9 |   return String(value ?? '')
  10 |     .toLowerCase()
  11 |     .replace(/\*+/g, '')
  12 |     .replace(/\([^)]*\)/g, ' ')
  13 |     .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')
  14 |     .trim()
  15 | }
  16 | 
  17 | /** «О.О.» → «О. О.», «Є.М» → «Є. М» */
  18 | export function formatTeacherInitials(value: string): string {
  19 |   return String(value ?? '')
  20 |     .trim()
  21 |     .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')
  22 |     .replace(/\.(?=[A-ZА-ЯІЇЄҐ])/gi, '. ')
  23 |     .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')
  24 |     .trim()
  25 | }
  26 | 
  27 | export function normalizeTeacher(value: string): string | null {
  28 |   let teacher = formatTeacherInitials(String(value ?? ''))
  29 |   if (!teacher || teacher === 'В' || teacher.length < 3) return null
  30 |   if (teacher.toLowerCase().includes('прізвище') || teacher.toLowerCase().includes('викладач')) return null
  31 |   teacher = formatTeacherInitials(teacher.replace(/^В\s+/, '').trim())
  32 |   return teacher || null
  33 | }
  34 | 
  35 | /** Для поля навплану: завжди форматує ініціали, навіть якщо рядок короткий. */
  36 | export function normalizeTeacherField(value: string): string {
  37 |   const trimmed = String(value ?? '').trim()
  38 |   if (!trimmed || trimmed === 'В') return ''
  39 |   const normalized = normalizeTeacher(trimmed)
  40 |   if (normalized) return normalized
  41 |   return formatTeacherInitials(trimmed.replace(/^В\s+/, '').trim())
  42 | }
  43 | 
  44 | export function parseNumber(value: unknown): number {
  45 |   if (value === null || value === undefined || value === '') return 0
  46 |   const n = Number(String(value).replace(',', '.').replace(/\s/g, ''))
  47 |   return Number.isFinite(n) ? n : 0
  48 | }
  49 | 
  50 | export function newId(prefix: string): string {
  51 |   return `${prefix}_${Date.now().toString(36)}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7)}`
  52 | }
  53 |

   1 | import { normalizeGroupCode } from './normalize'
   2 | 
   3 | export type DemandLike = {
   4 |   key: string
   5 |   groupCode: string
   6 |   groupId: string
   7 |   subject: string
   8 |   teacher: string
   9 |   pairsPerWeek: number
  10 |   parallelBundleId?: string
  11 |   subjectDayKey?: string
  12 | }
  13 | 
  14 | /** Ключ предмета без «13 студ», «9 студентів» тощо — для паралельних підгруп. */
  15 | export function parallelSubjectKey(subject: string): string {
  16 |   let s = String(subject ?? '').toLowerCase().replace(/\*+/g, '')
  17 |   s = s.replace(/\d+\s*ст(?:уд(?:ент(?:ів|и|а)?)?)?\.?/gi, ' ')
  18 |   s = s.replace(/ст(?:уд(?:ент(?:ів|и|a)?)?)?\.?\s*\d+/gi, ' ')
  19 |   s = s.replace(/\(\s*\d+\s*ст[^)]*\)/gi, ' ')
  20 |   s = s.replace(/\([^)]*\)/g, ' ')
  21 |   return s.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim()
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | export function parallelBundleDayKey(groupCode: string, subject: string): string {
  25 |   return `${normalizeGroupCode(groupCode)}|${parallelSubjectKey(subject)}`
  26 | }
  27 | 
  28 | export function assignParallelBundles<T extends DemandLike>(demands: T[]): {
  29 |   demands: T[]
  30 |   warnings: string[]
  31 |   bundleCount: number
  32 | } {
  33 |   const warnings: string[] = []
  34 |   const clusters = new Map<string, T[]>()
  35 | 
  36 |   for (const demand of demands) {
  37 |     const clusterKey = `${demand.groupCode}|${parallelSubjectKey(demand.subject)}`
  38 |     const bucket = clusters.get(clusterKey) ?? []
  39 |     bucket.push(demand)
  40 |     clusters.set(clusterKey, bucket)
  41 |   }
  42 | 
  43 |   let bundleCount = 0
  44 | 
  45 |   for (const [clusterKey, cluster] of clusters) {
  46 |     if (cluster.length < 2) continue
  47 | 
  48 |     const teachers = new Set(cluster.map((d) => d.teacher))
  49 |     if (teachers.size < 2) continue
  50 | 
  51 |     bundleCount += 1
  52 |     const bundleId = `pb|${clusterKey}`
  53 |     const dayKey = parallelBundleDayKey(cluster[0].groupCode, cluster[0].subject)
  54 |     const pairCounts = cluster.map((d) => d.pairsPerWeek)
  55 |     const minPairs = Math.min(...pairCounts)
  56 |     const maxPairs = Math.max(...pairCounts)
  57 | 
  58 |     if (minPairs !== maxPairs) {
  59 |       warnings.push(
  60 |         `Підгрупи «${cluster[0].subject}» (${cluster[0].groupCode}): ${minPairs}–${maxPairs} пар/тиж — синхронізовано до ${minPairs}.`,
  61 |       )
  62 |     }
  63 | 
  64 |     for (const demand of cluster) {
  65 |       demand.parallelBundleId = bundleId
  66 |       demand.subjectDayKey = dayKey
  67 |       demand.pairsPerWeek = minPairs
  68 |     }
  69 |   }
  70 | 
  71 |   for (const demand of demands) {
  72 |     if (!demand.subjectDayKey) demand.subjectDayKey = demand.key
  73 |   }
  74 | 
  75 |   return { demands, warnings, bundleCount }
  76 | }
  77 | 
  78 | export function buildScheduleUnits<T extends DemandLike>(demands: T[]): Array<
  79 |   | { type: 'single'; demand: T }
  80 |   | { type: 'parallel'; bundleId: string; demands: T[] }
  81 | > {
  82 |   const usedKeys = new Set<string>()
  83 |   const units: Array<
  84 |     | { type: 'single'; demand: T }
  85 |     | { type: 'parallel'; bundleId: string; demands: T[] }
  86 |   > = []
  87 | 
  88 |   for (const demand of demands) {
  89 |     if (usedKeys.has(demand.key)) continue
  90 | 
  91 |     if (demand.parallelBundleId) {
  92 |       const peers = demands.filter((d) => d.parallelBundleId === demand.parallelBundleId)
  93 |       for (const peer of peers) usedKeys.add(peer.key)
  94 |       units.push({ type: 'parallel', bundleId: demand.parallelBundleId, demands: peers })
  95 |       continue
  96 |     }
  97 | 
  98 |     usedKeys.add(demand.key)
  99 |     units.push({ type: 'single', demand })
 100 |   }
 101 | 
 102 |   return units
 103 | }

  78 | function normalizeSubject(value: unknown): string | null {
  79 |   const subject = String(value ?? '').trim()
  80 |   if (!subject || subject.length < 4) return null
  81 |   if (/^[\d\s.,]+$/.test(subject)) return null
  82 |   if (subject.toLowerCase().includes('заст. директора')) return null
  83 |   if (subject.startsWith('РОЗПОДІЛ')) return null
  84 |   return subject.replace(/\*+/g, '').trim()

  94 | function isGroupCode(value: string): boolean {

  97 |   if (/^[\d.,]+$/.test(code)) return false
