 101 | export function parseNavPlanWorkbook(workbook: XLSX.WorkBook, sheetName?: string): NavPlanRow[] {
 102 |   const name =
 103 |     sheetName ??
 104 |     workbook.SheetNames.find((n) => n.toLowerCase().includes('навчальн')) ??
 105 |     workbook.SheetNames[0]
 106 |   const rows = XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json<unknown[]>(workbook.Sheets[name], {
 107 |     header: 1,
 108 |     defval: '',
 109 |   })
 110 | 
 111 |   const headerRow = findHeaderRow(rows)
 112 |   const dataStart = headerRow + 2
 113 |   const result: NavPlanRow[] = []
 114 | 
 115 |   for (let i = dataStart; i < rows.length; i += 1) {
 116 |     const row = rows[i] ?? []
 117 |     const subject = normalizeSubject(row[COL.subject])
 118 |     const groupRaw = String(row[COL.group] ?? '').trim()
 119 |     if (!subject || !isGroupCode(groupRaw)) continue
 120 | 
 121 |     const teacherRaw = String(row[COL.teacher] ?? '').trim()
 122 | 
 123 |     result.push(
 124 |       normalizeNavPlanRow({
 125 |         id: newId('np'),
 126 |         subject,
 127 |         subjectNorm: normalizeSubjectKey(subject),
 128 |         teacher: teacherRaw,
 129 |         hoursTotal: parseNumber(row[COL.hoursTotal]),
 130 |         hoursCourse: parseNumber(row[COL.hoursCourse]),
 131 |         hoursSelf: parseNumber(row[COL.hoursSelf]),
 132 |         fallLectures: parseNumber(row[COL.fallLectures]),
 133 |         fallPractical: parseNumber(row[COL.fallPractical]),
 134 |         fallLab: parseNumber(row[COL.fallLab]),
 135 |         fallCoursework: parseNumber(row[COL.fallCoursework]),
 136 |         fallConsult: parseNumber(row[COL.fallConsult]),
 137 |         fallCredits: parseNumber(row[COL.fallCredits]),
 138 |         fallExams: parseNumber(row[COL.fallExams]),
 139 |         hoursFall: parseNumber(row[COL.fallTotal]),
 140 |         springLectures: parseNumber(row[COL.springLectures]),
 141 |         springPractical: parseNumber(row[COL.springPractical]),
 142 |         springLab: parseNumber(row[COL.springLab]),
 143 |         springCoursework: parseNumber(row[COL.springCoursework]),
 144 |         springConsult: parseNumber(row[COL.springConsult]),
 145 |         springSupervised: parseNumber(row[COL.springSupervised]),
 146 |         springCredits: parseNumber(row[COL.springCredits]),
 147 |         springExams: parseNumber(row[COL.springExams]),
 148 |         springDpa: parseNumber(row[COL.springDpa]),
 149 |         springDkk: parseNumber(row[COL.springDkk]),
 150 |         hoursSpring: parseNumber(row[COL.springTotal]),
 151 |         groupCode: normalizeGroupCode(groupRaw),
 152 |         budget: parseNumber(row[COL.budget]),
 153 |         extraBudget: parseNumber(row[COL.extraBudget]),
 154 |       }),
 155 |     )
 156 |   }

 167 | export function parseGroupsWeeksWorkbook(workbook: XLSX.WorkBook): Map<string, { weeksFall: number; weeksSpring: number }> {

   1 | import type { EnrichedEntry } from '../types/schedule'

   4 | export function clusterKeyForGroup(entry: EnrichedEntry): string {
   5 |   if (entry.parallelBundleId) return `b|${entry.parallelBundleId}|${entry.slotId}`
   6 |   return `g|${entry.groupId}|${entry.slotId}|${parallelSubjectKey(entry.subject)}`
   7 | }
   8 | 
   9 | export function parallelDisplaySubject(entries: EnrichedEntry[]): string {
  10 |   if (entries.length === 1) return entries[0].subject
  11 |   const bases = new Set(entries.map((e) => parallelSubjectKey(e.subject)))
  12 |   if (bases.size === 1) {
  13 |     return (
  14 |       entries[0].subject
  15 |         .replace(/\d+\s*ст(?:уд(?:ент(?:ів|и|a)?)?)?\.?/gi, ' ')
  16 |         .replace(/\([^)]*\d+\s*ст[^)]*\)/gi, ' ')
  17 |         .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')
  18 |         .trim() || entries[0].subject
  19 |     )
  20 |   }
  21 |   return entries[0].subject
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | export type ScheduleEntryCluster = {
  25 |   key: string
  26 |   entries: EnrichedEntry[]
  27 |   primary: EnrichedEntry
  28 |   parallel: boolean
  29 |   teachers: string[]
  30 |   rooms: string[]
  31 |   subject: string
  32 | }
  33 | 
  34 | export function clusterEntries(entries: EnrichedEntry[]): ScheduleEntryCluster[] {
  35 |   const map = new Map<string, EnrichedEntry[]>()
  36 |   for (const entry of entries) {
  37 |     const key = clusterKeyForGroup(entry)
  38 |     const bucket = map.get(key) ?? []
  39 |     bucket.push(entry)
  40 |     map.set(key, bucket)
  41 |   }
  42 | 
  43 |   return [...map.entries()].map(([key, cluster]) => {
  44 |     const primary = cluster[0]
  45 |     const parallel = cluster.length > 1 || Boolean(primary.parallelBundleId)
  46 |     return {
  47 |       key,
  48 |       entries: cluster,
  49 |       primary,
  50 |       parallel,
  51 |       subject: parallelDisplaySubject(cluster),
  52 |       teachers: [...new Set(cluster.map((e) => e.teacher).filter(Boolean))].sort((a, b) =>
  53 |         a.localeCompare(b, 'uk'),
  54 |       ),
  55 |       rooms: [...new Set(cluster.map((e) => e.room).filter(Boolean))],
  56 |     }
  57 |   })
  58 | }

  60 | export function shortDisplayText(value: string, max = 22): string {
  61 |   const trimmed = value.trim()
  62 |   if (trimmed.length <= max) return trimmed
  63 |   return `${trimmed.slice(0, max - 1)}…`
  64 | }

   6 |   dayIndex: number

  11 | export function slotContext(slotId: number, meta: ScheduleMeta): SlotContext {
  12 |   const { dayIndex, day, period } = slotToDayPeriod(slotId, meta)
  13 |   return { slotId, dayIndex, day, period }
  14 | }
  15 | 
  16 | export function shiftPeriodRange(shift: 1 | 2): { from: number; to: number } {
  17 |   return shift === 1 ? { from: 1, to: 4 } : { from: 5, to: 8 }
  18 | }
  19 | 
  20 | export function allowedSlotIds(meta: ScheduleMeta, shift: 1 | 2): number[] {
  21 |   const { from, to } = shiftPeriodRange(shift)
  22 |   const slots: number[] = []
  23 |   for (let dayIndex = 0; dayIndex < meta.days.length; dayIndex += 1) {
  24 |     for (let period = from; period <= to; period += 1) {
  25 |       slots.push(dayIndex * meta.periodsPerDay + period)
  26 |     }
  27 |   }
  28 |   return slots
  29 | }
  30 | 
  31 | export function isPhysicalEducation(subject: string): boolean {
  32 |   const s = subject.toLowerCase()
  33 |   return s.includes('фізич') || s.includes('фізкульт') || s.includes('фіз. к')
  34 | }
  35 | 
  36 | export function teacherAllowsSlot(
  37 |   teacherPref: string | undefined,
  38 |   ctx: SlotContext,
  39 | ): boolean {
  40 |   if (!teacherPref) return true
  41 |   const rules = teacherPref.split(/[,;\s]+/).filter(Boolean)
  42 |   for (const rule of rules) {
  43 |     if (rule === 'не_1' && ctx.period === 1) return false
  44 |     if (rule === 'не_4' && ctx.period === 4) return false
  45 |     if (rule === 'не_перші' && ctx.period <= 2) return false
  46 |     if (rule === 'не_останні' && ctx.period >= 7) return false
  47 |     if (rule === 'не_понеділок' && ctx.dayIndex === 0) return false
  48 |     if (rule === 'не_пятниця' && ctx.dayIndex === 4) return false
  49 |     if (rule === 'тільки_зміна_1' && ctx.period > 4) return false
  50 |     if (rule === 'тільки_зміна_2' && ctx.period < 5) return false
  51 |   }
  52 |   return true
  53 | }
  54 | 
  55 | /** Макс. пар викладача на день. За замовчуванням 4; преференції max_1_день … max_5_день. */
  56 | export function teacherDayPairLimit(teacherPref: string | undefined): number {
  57 |   if (!teacherPref) return 4
  58 |   if (teacherPref.includes('max_5_день')) return 5
  59 |   if (teacherPref.includes('max_4_день')) return 4
  60 |   if (teacherPref.includes('max_3_день')) return 3
  61 |   if (teacherPref.includes('max_2_день')) return 2
  62 |   if (teacherPref.includes('max_1_день')) return 1
  63 |   return 4
  64 | }
  65 | 
  66 | /**
  67 |  * Оцінка завантаження викладача в день (менше = краще).
  68 |  * За замовчуванням прагнемо 3–4 пари на день, уникаємо «розмазування» по 1–2.
  69 |  * null — слот заборонено (перевищено денний ліміт).
  70 |  */
  71 | export function scoreTeacherDailyLoad(
  72 |   pairsOnDayBefore: number,
  73 |   teacherPref: string | undefined,
  74 | ): number | null {
  75 |   const after = pairsOnDayBefore + 1
  76 |   const max = teacherDayPairLimit(teacherPref)
  77 |   if (after > max) return null
  78 | 
  79 |   if (pairsOnDayBefore === 0) return 150
  80 |   if (after === 4 && max >= 4) return -140
  81 |   if (after === 3) return -115
  82 |   if (after === 2) return -65
  83 |   return -15
  84 | }
  85 | 
  86 | export function subjectDayLimit(subjectPref: string | undefined): number {
  87 |   if (!subjectPref) return 2
  88 |   if (subjectPref.includes('max_1_день')) return 1
  89 |   if (subjectPref.includes('max_2_день')) return 2
  90 |   return 2
  91 | }
  92 | 
  93 | export function subjectAllowsDay(subjectPref: string | undefined, dayIndex: number): boolean {
  94 |   if (!subjectPref) return true
  95 |   if (subjectPref.includes('не_1_день') && dayIndex === 0) return false
  96 |   if (subjectPref.includes('не_5_день') && dayIndex === 4) return false
  97 |   return true
  98 | }

 101 | export { isSchedulableSubject, isSchedulableNavPlanRow } from './navPlanClassify'
 102 | 
 103 | export function pePeriodScore(ctx: SlotContext, shift: 1 | 2): number {
 104 |   if (ctx.period === 1 || ctx.period === 8) return 0
 105 |   if (shift === 2 && (ctx.period === 5 || ctx.period === 8)) return 0
 106 |   return Math.abs(ctx.period - (shift === 1 ? 1 : 5)) + 1
 107 | }

   1 | export const CYLINDER_RADIUS = 4.2

   3 | export const LAYER_GAP = 0.12
   4 | export const CELL_DEPTH = 0.28
   5 | export const CELL_WIDTH = 0.34
   6 | export const TIME_RING_OFFSET = 0.82
   7 | export const TIME_RING_HEIGHT = 0.22
   8 | 
   9 | export function computeCylinderLayout(groupCount: number) {
  10 |   const totalHeight = groupCount * (LAYER_HEIGHT + LAYER_GAP)
  11 |   const baseY = -totalHeight / 2
  12 |   const yTop = baseY + totalHeight
  13 |   const ringY = baseY - TIME_RING_OFFSET
  14 |   const ringBottom = ringY - TIME_RING_HEIGHT
  15 |   const orbitPivotY = (yTop + ringBottom) / 2
  16 | 
  17 |   return {
  18 |     totalHeight,
  19 |     baseY,
  20 |     yTop,
  21 |     ringY,
  22 |     orbitPivotY,
  23 |   }
  24 | }

   1 | import type { EnrichedEntry, Filters, Group, ScheduleMeta, Teacher } from '../types/schedule'
   2 | import { matchesAnyTerm, matchesAnyText, splitFilterTerms } from './filterTerms'
   3 | import { normalizeGroupCode, normalizeTeacherField } from './normalize'
   4 | import { slotToDayPeriod } from './slots'
   5 | 
   6 | export const defaultScheduleFilters: Filters = {
   7 |   specialty: '',
   8 |   course: '',
   9 |   groupCode: '',
  10 |   teacher: '',
  11 |   day: '',
  12 |   conflictsOnly: false,
  13 | }
  14 | 
  15 | function matchesTeacherTerm(teacher: string, term: string): boolean {
  16 |   const normalizedRow = normalizeTeacherField(teacher).toLowerCase()
  17 |   const normalizedQuery = normalizeTeacherField(term).toLowerCase()
  18 |   if (normalizedQuery && normalizedRow.includes(normalizedQuery)) return true
  19 |   return teacher.toLowerCase().includes(term.trim().toLowerCase())
  20 | }
  21 | 
  22 | export function teacherMatchesFilter(teacher: string, filter: string): boolean {
  23 |   return matchesAnyTerm(filter, matchesTeacherTerm, teacher)
  24 | }
  25 | 
  26 | function matchesGroupTerm(group: Group, term: string): boolean {
  27 |   const code = normalizeGroupCode(group.code)
  28 |   const query = normalizeGroupCode(term)
  29 |   return (
  30 |     code.includes(query) ||
  31 |     group.name.toLowerCase().includes(term.trim().toLowerCase()) ||
  32 |     group.code.toLowerCase().includes(term.trim().toLowerCase()) ||
  33 |     group.specialty.toLowerCase().includes(term.trim().toLowerCase())
  34 |   )
  35 | }
  36 | 
  37 | export function groupMatchesFilter(group: Group, filter: string): boolean {
  38 |   return matchesAnyTerm(filter, matchesGroupTerm, group)
  39 | }
  40 | 
  41 | export function filterGroups(groups: Group[], filters: Filters): Group[] {
  42 |   return groups.filter((group) => {
  43 |     if (!matchesAnyText(group.specialty, filters.specialty)) return false
  44 |     if (splitFilterTerms(filters.course).length > 0 && !matchesAnyText(String(group.course), filters.course)) {
  45 |       return false
  46 |     }
  47 |     if (!groupMatchesFilter(group, filters.groupCode)) return false
  48 |     return true
  49 |   })
  50 | }
  51 | 
  52 | export function filterEntries(
  53 |   entries: EnrichedEntry[],
  54 |   meta: ScheduleMeta,
  55 |   visibleGroupIds: Set<string>,
  56 |   filters: Filters,
  57 | ): EnrichedEntry[] {
  58 |   return entries.filter((entry) => {
  59 |     if (!visibleGroupIds.has(entry.groupId)) return false
  60 |     if (!teacherMatchesFilter(entry.teacher, filters.teacher)) return false
  61 |     if (splitFilterTerms(filters.day).length > 0) {
  62 |       const { day } = slotToDayPeriod(entry.slotId, meta)
  63 |       if (!matchesAnyText(day, filters.day)) return false
  64 |     }
  65 |     if (filters.conflictsOnly && entry.conflict === 'none') return false
  66 |     return true
  67 |   })
  68 | }
  69 | 
  70 | export function resolveSingleGroup(groups: Group[], filter: string): Group | null {
  71 |   if (splitFilterTerms(filter).length === 0) return null
  72 |   const matched = groups.filter((group) => groupMatchesFilter(group, filter))
  73 |   return matched.length === 1 ? matched[0]! : null
  74 | }
  75 | 
  76 | export function resolveTeachers(filter: string, teachers: Teacher[]): string[] {
  77 |   if (splitFilterTerms(filter).length === 0) return []
  78 |   return teachers.filter((teacher) => teacherMatchesFilter(teacher.name, filter)).map((teacher) => teacher.name)
  79 | }
  80 | 
  81 | export function hasActiveScheduleFilters(filters: Filters): boolean {
  82 |   return (
  83 |     filters.specialty.trim() !== '' ||
  84 |     filters.course.trim() !== '' ||
  85 |     filters.groupCode.trim() !== '' ||
  86 |     filters.teacher.trim() !== '' ||
  87 |     filters.day.trim() !== '' ||
  88 |     filters.conflictsOnly
  89 |   )
  90 | }

   1 | import type { ScheduleDocument } from '../types/documents'
   2 | import type {
   3 |   Group,
   4 |   Room,
   5 |   ScheduleData,
   6 |   ScheduleEntry,
   7 |   ScheduleMeta,
   8 |   Teacher,
   9 | } from '../types/schedule'

  11 | import { downloadJsonFile } from './schedulePrintExport'

  13 | export const SCHEDULE_JSON_TYPE = 'schedule3d-schedule-v1'

  15 | export type ScheduleImportDocument = {
  16 |   label: string
  17 |   savedAt: string
  18 |   savedBy: string
  19 |   note?: string
  20 |   edited: boolean
  21 |   schedule: ScheduleData
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | function isRecord(value: unknown): value is Record<string, unknown> {
  25 |   return typeof value === 'object' && value !== null
  26 | }
  27 | 
  28 | function isScheduleDataShape(raw: Record<string, unknown>): boolean {
  29 |   return (
  30 |     isRecord(raw.meta) &&
  31 |     Array.isArray(raw.groups) &&
  32 |     Array.isArray(raw.teachers) &&
  33 |     Array.isArray(raw.rooms) &&
  34 |     Array.isArray(raw.entries)
  35 |   )
  36 | }
  37 | 
  38 | function normalizeMeta(raw: Record<string, unknown>): ScheduleMeta {
  39 |   const days = Array.isArray(raw.days) ? raw.days.map(String) : ['Пн', 'Вт', 'Ср', 'Чт', 'Пт']
  40 |   const periodsPerDay = Number(raw.periodsPerDay ?? 8)
  41 |   const totalSlots = Number(raw.totalSlots ?? days.length * periodsPerDay)
  42 | 
  43 |   return {
  44 |     sourceFile: String(raw.sourceFile ?? 'імпорт JSON'),
  45 |     generatedAt: String(raw.generatedAt ?? new Date().toISOString()),
  46 |     note: String(raw.note ?? ''),
  47 |     days,
  48 |     periodsPerDay: Number.isFinite(periodsPerDay) ? periodsPerDay : 8,
  49 |     totalSlots: Number.isFinite(totalSlots) ? totalSlots : days.length * periodsPerDay,
  50 |   }
  51 | }
  52 | 
  53 | function normalizeGroup(raw: unknown, index: number): Group {
  54 |   const row = isRecord(raw) ? raw : {}
  55 |   const code = String(row.code ?? `G${index + 1}`)
  56 |   return {
  57 |     id: String(row.id ?? `g${index + 1}`),
  58 |     code,
  59 |     name: String(row.name ?? `Група ${code}`),
  60 |     specialty: String(row.specialty ?? code.replace(/\d.*/, '')),
  61 |     course: Number(row.course ?? 1) || 1,
  62 |     room: String(row.room ?? ''),
  63 |   }
  64 | }
  65 | 
  66 | function normalizeTeacher(raw: unknown, index: number): Teacher {
  67 |   const row = isRecord(raw) ? raw : {}
  68 |   const name = String(row.name ?? '').trim()
  69 |   return {
  70 |     id: String(row.id ?? `t${index + 1}`),
  71 |     name: name || `Викладач ${index + 1}`,
  72 |   }
  73 | }
  74 | 
  75 | function normalizeRoom(raw: unknown, index: number): Room {
  76 |   const row = isRecord(raw) ? raw : {}
  77 |   return {
  78 |     id: String(row.id ?? `r${index + 1}`),
  79 |     code: String(row.code ?? `room-${index + 1}`),
  80 |   }
  81 | }
  82 | 
  83 | function normalizeEntry(raw: unknown, index: number): ScheduleEntry {
  84 |   const row = isRecord(raw) ? raw : {}
  85 |   const entry: ScheduleEntry = {
  86 |     id: String(row.id ?? `e${index + 1}`),
  87 |     groupId: String(row.groupId ?? ''),
  88 |     slotId: Number(row.slotId ?? 0),
  89 |     subject: String(row.subject ?? ''),
  90 |     teacher: String(row.teacher ?? ''),
  91 |     room: String(row.room ?? ''),
  92 |   }
  93 |   if (row.parallelBundleId) entry.parallelBundleId = String(row.parallelBundleId)
  94 |   return entry
  95 | }
  96 | 
  97 | export function normalizeScheduleData(raw: Record<string, unknown>): ScheduleData {
  98 |   if (!isScheduleDataShape(raw)) {
  99 |     throw new Error('Некоректна структура розкладу (meta, groups, teachers, rooms, entries)')
 100 |   }
 101 | 
 102 |   return {
 103 |     meta: normalizeMeta(raw.meta as Record<string, unknown>),
 104 |     groups: (raw.groups as unknown[]).map(normalizeGroup),
 105 |     teachers: (raw.teachers as unknown[]).map(normalizeTeacher),
 106 |     rooms: (raw.rooms as unknown[]).map(normalizeRoom),
 107 |     entries: (raw.entries as unknown[]).map(normalizeEntry),
 108 |   }
 109 | }
 110 | 
 111 | function documentToImport(doc: ScheduleDocument): ScheduleImportDocument {
 112 |   return {
 113 |     label: doc.label,
 114 |     savedAt: doc.savedAt,
 115 |     savedBy: doc.savedBy,
 116 |     note: doc.note,
 117 |     edited: doc.edited,
 118 |     schedule: normalizeScheduleData(doc.schedule as unknown as Record<string, unknown>),
 119 |   }
 120 | }
 121 | 
 122 | export function parseScheduleImport(raw: unknown): ScheduleImportDocument {
 123 |   if (!isRecord(raw)) throw new Error('Некоректний JSON')
 124 | 
 125 |   if (raw.type === SCHEDULE_JSON_TYPE && isRecord(raw.schedule) && isScheduleDataShape(raw.schedule)) {
 126 |     return {
 127 |       label: String(raw.label ?? 'Імпорт'),
 128 |       savedAt: String(raw.savedAt ?? new Date().toISOString()),
 129 |       savedBy: String(raw.savedBy ?? 'невідомо'),
 130 |       note: raw.note ? String(raw.note) : undefined,
 131 |       edited: Boolean(raw.edited),
 132 |       schedule: normalizeScheduleData(raw.schedule),
 133 |     }
 134 |   }
 135 | 
 136 |   if ('schedule' in raw && isRecord(raw.schedule) && isScheduleDataShape(raw.schedule)) {
 137 |     return documentToImport(raw as ScheduleDocument)
 138 |   }
 139 | 
 140 |   if (isScheduleDataShape(raw)) {
 141 |     const meta = raw.meta as Record<string, unknown>
 142 |     return {
 143 |       label: String(meta.sourceFile ?? 'Імпорт'),
 144 |       savedAt: String(meta.generatedAt ?? new Date().toISOString()),
 145 |       savedBy: 'імпорт',
 146 |       edited: false,
 147 |       schedule: normalizeScheduleData(raw),
 148 |     }
 149 |   }
 150 | 
 151 |   throw new Error('У файлі немає даних розкладу (очікується schedule-full.json або збережена версія)')
 152 | }
 153 | 
 154 | export function exportScheduleDataFile(schedule: ScheduleData, filename?: string): void {
 155 |   const datePart = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10)
 156 |   downloadJsonFile(schedule, filename ?? `schedule-full-${datePart}.json`)
 157 | }
 158 | 
 159 | export function exportCurrentScheduleJson(
 160 |   schedule: ScheduleData,
 161 |   options?: { label?: string; note?: string },
 162 | ): void {
 163 |   const label = options?.label?.trim() || `Розклад ${new Date().toLocaleDateString('uk-UA')}`
 164 |   const savedAt = new Date().toISOString()
 165 |   const payload = {
 166 |     type: SCHEDULE_JSON_TYPE,
 167 |     label,
 168 |     savedAt,
 169 |     savedBy: ensureEditorName(),
 170 |     note: options?.note?.trim() || undefined,
 171 |     edited: false,
 172 |     schedule: structuredClone(schedule),
 173 |   }
 174 |   const safe = label.replace(/[^\w\u0400-\u04FF-]+/g, '_').slice(0, 40) || 'schedule'
 175 |   downloadJsonFile(payload, `schedule-${safe}-${savedAt.slice(0, 10)}.json`)
 176 | }

   1 | import type { PrintScheduleDocument, PrintWeekRow } from '../types/documents'
   2 | import type { EnrichedEntry, Group, ScheduleEntry, ScheduleMeta } from '../types/schedule'
   3 | import { enrichEntries } from './conflicts'
   4 | import { clusterEntries } from './scheduleClusters'
   5 | import { slotLabel, slotToDayPeriod } from './slots'
   6 | 
   7 | export function buildPrintWeekRows(
   8 |   entries: ScheduleEntry[],
   9 |   groups: Group[],
  10 |   meta: ScheduleMeta,
  11 |   mode: 'group' | 'teacher',
  12 | ): Array<{ day: string; rows: PrintWeekRow[] }> {
  13 |   const groupById = new Map(groups.map((g) => [g.id, g]))
  14 |   const enriched = enrichEntries(entries) as EnrichedEntry[]
  15 |   const conflictIds = new Set(enriched.filter((e) => e.conflict !== 'none').map((e) => e.id))
  16 | 
  17 |   return meta.days.map((day) => {
  18 |     const dayEntries = enriched.filter((entry) => slotToDayPeriod(entry.slotId, meta).day === day)
  19 | 
  20 |     if (mode === 'group') {
  21 |       const rows = clusterEntries(dayEntries)
  22 |         .map((cluster) => {
  23 |           const { period } = slotToDayPeriod(cluster.primary.slotId, meta)
  24 |           return {
  25 |             slot: slotLabel(cluster.primary.slotId, meta),
  26 |             period,
  27 |             subject: cluster.subject,
  28 |             teacher: cluster.teachers.join(' · '),
  29 |             room: cluster.rooms.join(' · '),
  30 |             groupCode: groupById.get(cluster.primary.groupId)?.code ?? '?',
  31 |             parallel: cluster.parallel,
  32 |             teachers: cluster.teachers,
  33 |             hasConflict: cluster.entries.some((entry) => conflictIds.has(entry.id)),
  34 |           }
  35 |         })
  36 |         .sort((a, b) => a.period - b.period)
  37 |       return { day, rows }
  38 |     }
  39 | 
  40 |     const rows = dayEntries
  41 |       .map((entry) => {
  42 |         const { period } = slotToDayPeriod(entry.slotId, meta)
  43 |         return {
  44 |           slot: slotLabel(entry.slotId, meta),
  45 |           period,
  46 |           subject: entry.subject,
  47 |           teacher: entry.teacher,
  48 |           room: entry.room,
  49 |           groupCode: groupById.get(entry.groupId)?.code ?? '?',
  50 |           parallel: false,
  51 |           hasConflict: conflictIds.has(entry.id),
  52 |         }
  53 |       })
  54 |       .sort((a, b) => a.period - b.period)
  55 | 
  56 |     return { day, rows }
  57 |   })
  58 | }
  59 | 
  60 | function escapeHtml(value: string): string {
  61 |   return String(value ?? '')
  62 |     .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
  63 |     .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
  64 |     .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
  65 |     .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
  66 | }
  67 | 
  68 | function shortSubject(subject: string, max = 42): string {
  69 |   const trimmed = subject.trim()
  70 |   if (trimmed.length <= max) return trimmed
  71 |   return `${trimmed.slice(0, max - 1)}…`
  72 | }
  73 | 
  74 | function buildSubjectSummary(doc: PrintScheduleDocument): Array<{ subject: string; tags: string[] }> {
  75 |   const map = new Map<string, Set<string>>()
  76 | 
  77 |   for (const { rows } of doc.weeks) {
  78 |     for (const row of rows) {
  79 |       const key = row.subject.trim()
  80 |       if (!key) continue
  81 |       const tag = doc.kind === 'teacher' ? row.groupCode : row.teacher
  82 |       const set = map.get(key) ?? new Set<string>()
  83 |       set.add(tag)
  84 |       map.set(key, set)
  85 |     }
  86 |   }
  87 | 
  88 |   return [...map.entries()]
  89 |     .sort((a, b) => a[0].localeCompare(b[0], 'uk'))
  90 |     .map(([subject, tags]) => ({
  91 |       subject: shortSubject(subject, 48),
  92 |       tags: [...tags].sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, 'uk')),
  93 |     }))
  94 | }
  95 | 
  96 | function renderLessonRow(doc: PrintScheduleDocument, row: PrintWeekRow & { hasConflict?: boolean }): string {
  97 |   const secondary =
  98 |     doc.kind === 'teacher'
  99 |       ? `<span class="tag group">${escapeHtml(row.groupCode)}</span>`
 100 |       : `<span class="tag teacher">${escapeHtml(row.teacher)}</span>`
 101 | 
 102 |   return `<li class="lesson${row.hasConflict ? ' conflict' : ''}${row.parallel ? ' parallel' : ''}">
 103 |     <div class="lesson-top">
 104 |       <span class="slot">${escapeHtml(row.slot)}${row.parallel ? ' · поділ' : ''}</span>
 105 |       ${secondary}
 106 |     </div>
 107 |     <div class="subject" title="${escapeHtml(row.subject)}">${escapeHtml(shortSubject(row.subject))}</div>
 108 |     <div class="room">${escapeHtml(row.room)}</div>
 109 |   </li>`
 110 | }

 325 |     @media print {

 327 |       .print-doc { padding: 0; }
 328 |     }

 332 |   <div class="print-doc">
 333 |     <header class="print-header">
 334 |       <div>
 335 |         <h1>${escapeHtml(doc.title)}</h1>
 336 |         <p class="meta">
 337 |           ${kindLabel}: <strong>${escapeHtml(doc.targetName)}</strong><br>
 338 |           Весняний семестр · ${escapeHtml(doc.meta.sourceFile || 'розклад')} · ${savedAt} · ${escapeHtml(doc.savedBy)}
 339 |           ${doc.note ? `<br>Примітка: ${escapeHtml(doc.note)}` : ''}
 340 |         </p>
 341 |       </div>
 342 |       <div class="stats">
 343 |         <strong>${totalLessons} ${totalLessons === 1 ? 'пара' : totalLessons < 5 ? 'пари' : 'пар'}</strong>
 344 |         на тиждень
 345 |       </div>
 346 |     </header>
 347 |     <div class="week-grid">${gridHtml}</div>
 348 |     ${summaryHtml}
 349 |     <footer class="print-footer">Згенеровано в schedule-3d · ${savedAt}</footer>
 350 |   </div>
 351 |   <script>
 352 |     window.addEventListener('load', function () {
 353 |       setTimeout(function () { window.focus(); window.print(); }, 150);
 354 |     });
 355 |   </script>
 356 | </body>
 357 | </html>`
 358 | }
 359 | 
 360 | function printHtmlInHiddenFrame(html: string): void {
 361 |   const iframe = document.createElement('iframe')
 362 |   iframe.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true')
 363 |   iframe.style.position = 'fixed'
 364 |   iframe.style.right = '0'
 365 |   iframe.style.bottom = '0'
 366 |   iframe.style.width = '0'
 367 |   iframe.style.height = '0'
 368 |   iframe.style.border = '0'
 369 |   document.body.appendChild(iframe)
 370 | 
 371 |   const frameDoc = iframe.contentDocument ?? iframe.contentWindow?.document
 372 |   if (!frameDoc) {
 373 |     iframe.remove()
 374 |     return
 375 |   }
 376 | 
 377 |   frameDoc.open()
 378 |   frameDoc.write(html.replace(/<script[\s\S]*?<\/script>/gi, ''))
 379 |   frameDoc.close()
 380 | 
 381 |   const printFrame = () => {
 382 |     iframe.contentWindow?.focus()
 383 |     iframe.contentWindow?.print()
 384 |     window.setTimeout(() => iframe.remove(), 1500)
 385 |   }
 386 | 
 387 |   iframe.onload = printFrame
 388 |   window.setTimeout(printFrame, 300)
 389 | }
 390 | 
 391 | export function printScheduleDocumentHtml(doc: PrintScheduleDocument): void {
 392 |   const html = buildPrintScheduleHtml(doc)
 393 |   const win = window.open('', '_blank', 'noopener,noreferrer')
 394 |   if (!win) {
 395 |     printHtmlInHiddenFrame(html)
 396 |     return
 397 |   }
 398 | 
 399 |   win.document.open()
 400 |   win.document.write(html)
 401 |   win.document.close()
 402 | }
 403 | 
 404 | export function createPrintScheduleDocument(
 405 |   schedule: { meta: ScheduleMeta; groups: Group[] },
 406 |   kind: 'group' | 'teacher',
 407 |   targetName: string,
 408 |   title: string,
 409 |   entries: ScheduleEntry[],
 410 |   savedBy: string,
 411 |   note?: string,
 412 | ): PrintScheduleDocument {
 413 |   return {
 414 |     id: 'print-preview',
 415 |     kind,
 416 |     targetName,
 417 |     title,
 418 |     savedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
 419 |     savedBy,
 420 |     note: note?.trim() || undefined,
 421 |     meta: schedule.meta,
 422 |     entries: structuredClone(entries),
 423 |     weeks: buildPrintWeekRows(entries, schedule.groups, schedule.meta, kind),
 424 |   }
 425 | }
 426 | 
 427 | export function downloadJsonFile(data: unknown, filename: string): void {
 428 |   const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json;charset=utf-8' })
 429 |   const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob)
 430 |   const link = document.createElement('a')
 431 |   link.href = url
 432 |   link.download = filename
 433 |   link.click()
 434 |   URL.revokeObjectURL(url)
 435 | }

Рядків: 27

   1 | import type { ScheduleMeta } from '../types/schedule'
   2 | 
   3 | export function slotToDayPeriod(slotId: number, meta: ScheduleMeta) {
   4 |   const index = slotId - 1
   5 |   const dayIndex = Math.floor(index / meta.periodsPerDay)
   6 |   const period = (index % meta.periodsPerDay) + 1
   7 |   return {
   8 |     dayIndex,
   9 |     day: meta.days[dayIndex] ?? '?',
  10 |     period,
  11 |   }
  12 | }
  13 | 
  14 | export function slotLabel(slotId: number, meta: ScheduleMeta) {
  15 |   const { day, period } = slotToDayPeriod(slotId, meta)
  16 |   return `${day}${period}`
  17 | }
  18 | 
  19 | export function slotAngle(slotId: number, totalSlots: number) {
  20 |   const index = slotId - 1
  21 |   return (index / totalSlots) * Math.PI * 2 - Math.PI / 2
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | export function allSlotLabels(meta: ScheduleMeta) {
  25 |   return Array.from({ length: meta.totalSlots }, (_, index) => slotLabel(index + 1, meta))
  26 | }
  27 |

   3 | /** Лекції + практичні (сем.) + лаби для тижневого розкладу весни. */
   4 | export function springTeachingFromColumns(row: NavPlanRow): number {
   5 |   return row.springLectures + row.springPractical + row.springLab
   6 | }
   7 | 
   8 | /** Контактні години весни (те саме джерело, що й для розкладу). */
   9 | export function springTeachingContactHours(row: NavPlanRow): number {
  10 |   const fromColumns = springTeachingFromColumns(row)
  11 |   if (fromColumns > 0) return fromColumns
  12 |   return row.hoursSpring
  13 | }
  14 | 
  15 | /** Години для planKind=schedule → розрахунок пар/тиждень. */
  16 | export function springSchedulableHours(row: NavPlanRow): number {
  17 |   if (row.planKind !== 'schedule') return 0
  18 |   const fromColumns = springTeachingFromColumns(row)
  19 |   if (fromColumns > 0) return fromColumns
  20 |   if (row.hoursSpring <= 0) return 0
  21 |   return row.hoursSpring
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | /** Одна академічна пара = 2 астрономічні години. */
  25 | export const HOURS_PER_PAIR = 2
  26 | 
  27 | /** Скільки пар за семестр (контактні години ÷ 2). */
  28 | export function semesterPairs(contactHours: number): number {
  29 |   if (contactHours <= 0) return 0
  30 |   return contactHours / HOURS_PER_PAIR
  31 | }
  32 | 
  33 | /** Пар на тиждень: (години ÷ 2) ÷ кількість тижнів семестру. */
  34 | export function pairsPerWeek(contactHours: number, weeks: number): number {
  35 |   if (contactHours <= 0 || weeks <= 0) return 0
  36 |   return Math.max(1, Math.round(contactHours / HOURS_PER_PAIR / weeks))
  37 | }
  38 |

Файл: src/utils/tableRowFilters.ts
Рядків: 29
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   1 | import { matchesAnyText } from './filterTerms'
   2 | 
   3 | export function filterTableRows<T extends object>(
   4 |   rows: T[],
   5 |   filters: Record<string, string>,
   6 |   fieldKeys: (keyof T)[],
   7 |   queryKey = 'query',
   8 | ): T[] {
   9 |   const query = filters[queryKey]?.trim() ?? ''
  10 |   const activeFields = fieldKeys.filter((key) => {
  11 |     const value = filters[String(key)]?.trim()
  12 |     return Boolean(value)
  13 |   })
  14 | 
  15 |   if (activeFields.length === 0 && !query) return rows
  16 | 
  17 |   return rows.filter((row) => {
  18 |     for (const key of activeFields) {
  19 |       const filterVal = filters[String(key)] ?? ''
  20 |       if (!matchesAnyText(String(row[key] ?? ''), filterVal)) return false
  21 |     }
  22 |     if (query) {
  23 |       const haystack = fieldKeys.map((key) => String(row[key] ?? '')).join(' ')
  24 |       if (!matchesAnyText(haystack, query)) return false
  25 |     }
  26 |     return true
  27 |   })
  28 | }
  29 |

Файл: src/utils/teacherOptions.ts
Рядків: 89
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   1 | import type { PlanningStore } from '../types/planning'
   2 | import type { ScheduleData } from '../types/schedule'
   3 | import { normalizeTeacherField } from './normalize'
   4 | 
   5 | const TEACHER_SPLIT = /[,;/\n\r]+|(?:\s+та\s+)|(?:\s+і\s+)/i
   6 | 
   7 | function cleanTeacherRaw(value: string): string {
   8 |   return String(value ?? '')
   9 |     .replace(/\u00a0/g, ' ')
  10 |     .replace(/\u200b/g, '')
  11 |     .trim()
  12 | }
  13 | 
  14 | function isPlaceholder(value: string): boolean {
  15 |   const raw = cleanTeacherRaw(value).toLowerCase()
  16 |   return raw === 'викладач' || raw === 'прізвище'
  17 | }
  18 | 
  19 | /** Розбиває комірку навплану на окремих викладачів. */
  20 | export function splitTeacherField(value: string): string[] {
  21 |   const raw = cleanTeacherRaw(value)
  22 |   if (!raw || isPlaceholder(raw)) return []
  23 | 
  24 |   const set = new Set<string>()
  25 |   const chunks = raw.split(TEACHER_SPLIT).map((part) => part.trim()).filter(Boolean)
  26 |   const parts = chunks.length > 0 ? chunks : [raw]
  27 | 
  28 |   for (const part of parts) {
  29 |     const normalized = normalizeTeacherField(part)
  30 |     if (normalized.length >= 3) set.add(normalized)
  31 |   }
  32 | 
  33 |   const whole = normalizeTeacherField(raw)
  34 |   if (whole.length >= 3) set.add(whole)
  35 | 
  36 |   return [...set]
  37 | }
  38 | 
  39 | export function collectTeacherOptions(store: PlanningStore, schedule?: ScheduleData | null): string[] {
  40 |   const set = new Set<string>()
  41 | 
  42 |   const add = (value: string) => {
  43 |     for (const teacher of splitTeacherField(value)) set.add(teacher)
  44 |   }
  45 | 
  46 |   for (const row of store.navPlan) add(row.teacher)
  47 |   for (const row of store.roomRules) add(row.teacher)
  48 | 
  49 |   if (schedule) {
  50 |     for (const teacher of schedule.teachers) add(teacher.name)
  51 |     for (const entry of schedule.entries) add(entry.teacher)
  52 |   }
  53 | 
  54 |   return [...set].sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, 'uk'))
  55 | }
  56 | 
  57 | export function countNavPlanRowsWithTeacher(store: PlanningStore): number {
  58 |   return store.navPlan.filter((row) => cleanTeacherRaw(row.teacher).length > 0).length
  59 | }
  60 | 
  61 | export function countNavPlanTeachers(store: PlanningStore): number {
  62 |   const set = new Set<string>()
  63 |   for (const row of store.navPlan) {
  64 |     for (const teacher of splitTeacherField(row.teacher)) set.add(teacher)
  65 |   }
  66 |   return set.size
  67 | }
  68 | 
  69 | /** Пошук викладача за частиною прізвища або ПІБ. */
  70 | export function matchesTeacherSearch(name: string, query: string): boolean {
  71 |   const q = cleanTeacherRaw(query).toLowerCase()
  72 |   if (!q) return true
  73 | 
  74 |   const raw = cleanTeacherRaw(name).toLowerCase()
  75 |   const normalized = normalizeTeacherField(name).toLowerCase()
  76 |   const surname = normalized.split(/\s+/)[0] ?? raw.split(/\s+/)[0] ?? ''
  77 | 
  78 |   if (raw.includes(q) || normalized.includes(q)) return true
  79 |   if (surname.startsWith(q)) return true
  80 | 
  81 |   return false
  82 | }
  83 | 
  84 | export function filterTeacherOptions(options: string[], query: string, limit = 40): string[] {
  85 |   const q = cleanTeacherRaw(query)
  86 |   const filtered = q ? options.filter((opt) => matchesTeacherSearch(opt, q)) : options
  87 |   return filtered.slice(0, limit)
  88 | }
